<sūtraprasthānam ||>
<anuvyākhyānam ||>
{1,1}
[1,1.1]	nārāyaṇaṃ nikhilapūrṇaguṇaikadehaṃ nirdoṣamāpyatamamapyakhilaiḥ suvākyaiḥ / asyodbhavādidamaśeṣaviśeṣato 'pi vandyaṃ sadā priyatamaṃ mama sannamāmi //
[1,1.2]	tameva śāstraprabhavaṃ praṇamya jagadgurūṇāṃ gurumañjasaiva / viśeṣato me paramākhyavidyāvyākhyāṃ karomyanvapi cāhameva //
[1,1.3]	prādurbhūto harirvyāso viriñcabhavapūrvakaiḥ / arthitaḥ paravidyākhyaṃ cakre śāstramanuttamam //
[1,1.4]	gururgurūṇāṃ prabhavaḥ śāstrāṇāṃ bādarāyaṇaḥ / yatastaduditaṃ mānamajādibhyastadarthataḥ //
[1,1.5]	vaktṛśrotṛprasaktīnāṃ yadāptiranukūlatā / āptavākyatayā tena śrutimūlatayā tathā //
[1,1.6]	yuktimūlatayā caiva prāmāṇyaṃ trividhaṃ mahat / dṛśyate brahmasūtrāṇāmekadhānyatra sarvaśaḥ //
[1,1.7]	ato naitādṛśaṃ kiñcit pramāṇatamamiṣyate / svayaṃ kṛtāpi tadvayākhyā kriyate spaṣṭatārthataḥ //
[1,1.8]	tatra tārāthamūlatvaṃ sarvaśaśastrasya ceṣyate / sarvatrānugatatvena pṛthagoṅkriyate 'khilaiḥ //
[1,1.9]	otatvavācī hyoṅkāro vaktayasau tadguṇotatām / sa eva brahmaśabdārtho nārāyaṇapadoditaḥ //
[1,1.10]	sa eva bhargaśabdārtho vyāhṛtīnāṃ ca bhūmataḥ / bhāvanāccaiva sutvācca so 'yaṃ puruṣa ityapi //
[1,1.11]	sa eva sarvavedārtho jijñāsyo 'yaṃ vidhīyate / jñānī priyatamo 'to me taṃ vidvāneva cāmṛtaḥ //
[1,1.12]	vṛṇute yaṃ tena labhya ityādyuktibalena hi / jijñāsotthajñānajāt tatprasādādeva mucyate //
[1,1.13]	dravyaṃ karma ca kālaśca svabhāvo jīva eva ca / yadanugrahataḥ santi na santi yadupekṣayā //
[1,1.14]	narte tvat kriyate kiñcidityāderna hariṃ vinā / jñānasvabhāvato 'pi syānmuktiḥ kasyāpi hi kvacit //
[1,1.15]	ajñānāṃ jñānado viṣṇurjñānināṃ mokṣadaśca saḥ / ānandadaśca muktānāṃ sa evaiko janārdanaḥ //
[1,1.16]	ityukterbandhamithyātvaṃ naiva muktirapekṣate / mithyātvamapi bandhasya na pratyakṣavirodhataḥ //
[1,1.17]	mithyātvaṃ yadi duḥkhādestadvākyāgrato bhavet / mithyāyāḥ sādhakatvaṃ ca na siddhaṃ prativādinaḥ //
[1,1.18]	tacca mithyāpramāṇena satā vā sādhyate tvayā / satā ced dvaitasiddhiḥ syānna siddhaṃ cānyasādhanam //
[1,1.19]	sādhakatvaṃ satastena sākṣiṇā siddhimicchatā / svīkṛtaṃ hyaviśeṣasya sādhyā sādhakatā punaḥ //
[1,1.20]	taccāviśeṣamānena sādhyamityanavasthitiḥ / anaṅgīkurvatāṃ viśvasatyatāṃ tanna vāditā //
[1,1.21]	tasmād vyavahṛtiḥ sarvā satyetyeva vyavasthitā / vyāvahārikametasmāt satyamityeva cāgatam //
[1,1.22]	vyavahārasataścāpi sādhakatvaṃ tu pūrvavat / sattraividhyaṃ ca mānena siddhayet keneti pṛcchyate //
[1,1.23]	tasyāpyuktaprakāreṇa naiva siddhiḥ kathañcana / vailakṣaṇyaṃ sadasatorapyetena niṣidhyate //
[1,1.24]	vailakṣaṇyaṃ sataścāpi svayaṃ sadbhedavādinaḥ / asataścāpi viśvasya tenāniṣyaṃ kathaṃ bhavet //
[1,1.25]	yadyucyate 'pi sarvasmāditi sadbhedasaṃsthitiḥ / sanmātratvaṃ brahmaṇo 'pi tasmāt tadapi no bhavet //
[1,1.26]	jñānabādhyatvamapi tu na siddhaṃ prativādinaḥ / vijñātasyānyathā samyag vijñānaṃ hyeva tanmatam //
[1,1.27]	asadvilakṣaṇajñaptyai jñātavyamasadeva hi / tasmādasatpratītiśca kathaṃ tena nivāryate //
[1,1.28]	anyathātvamasat tasmād bhrāntāveva pratīyate / sattvasyāsata evaṃ hi svīkāryaiva pratītatā //
[1,1.29]	tasyānirvacanīyatve syādeva hyanavasthitiḥ / nirviśeṣe svayaṃ bhāte kimajñānāvṛtaṃ bhavetaḥ //
[1,1.30]	mithyāviśeṣo 'pyajñānasiddhimeva hyapekṣate / nacāavaraṇamajñānamasatye tena ceṣyate //
[1,1.31]	aprakāśasvarūpatvājjaḍe 'jñānaṃ na manyate / ajñānābhāvataḥ śāstraṃ sarvaṃ vyarthībhaviṣyati //
[1,1.32]	ajñānasya ca mithyātvamajñānāditi kalpane / anavasthitistathāca syādanyonyāśrayatāthavā //
[1,1.33]	svabhāvājñānavādasya nirdoṣatvānna tad bhavet / avidyādurghaṭatvaṃ cet syādātmāpi hi tādṛśaḥ //
[1,1.34]	ato 'dhikāriviṣayaphalayogādivarjitam / anantadoṣaduṣṭaṃ ca heyaṃ māyāmataṃ śubhaiḥ //
[1,1.35]	satyatvāt tena duḥkhādeḥ pratyakṣeṇa virodhataḥ / na brahmatāṃ vaded vedo jīvasya hi kathañcana //
[1,1.36]	yajamānaprastaratvaṃ yathā nārthaḥ śruterbhavet / brahmatvamapi jīvasya pratyakṣasyāviśeṣataḥ //
[1,1.37]	sārvajñyādiguṇaṃ jīvād bhinnaṃ jñāpayati śrutiḥ / īśaṃ tāmupajīvyaiva vartate hyaikyavādinī //
[1,1.38]	upajīvyavirodhena nāsyāstanmānatā bhavet / svātantrye ca viśiṣṭatve sthānamattyaikyayorapi //
[1,1.39]	sādṛśye caikyavāk samyak sāvakāśā yatheṣyataḥ / avakāśojkhitā bhedaśrutirnātibalā katham //
[1,1.40]	ajñānāsambhavādeva mithyābhedo nirākṛtaḥ / ato yathārthabandhasya vinā viṣṇuprasādataḥ //
[1,1.41]	anivṛttestadarthaṃ hi jijñāsātra vidhīyate / yathā dṛṣṭayā prasannaḥ san rājā bandhāpanodakṛt //
[1,1.42]	evaṃ dṛṣṭaḥ sa bhagavān kuryād bandhavibhedanam / kāryatā ca na kācit syādiṣṭasādhanatāṃ vinā //
[1,1.43]	kāryaṃ na hi kriyāvyāpyaṃ niṣiddhasya samatvataḥ / na bhaviṣyatkriyā kāryaṃ srakṣyatīśa iti hyapi //
[1,1.44]	kāryaṃ syānnaiva cākartumaśakyaṃ kāryamiṣyate / sāmyādeva niṣiddhasya tadiṣṭaṃ sādhanaṃ tathā //
[1,1.45]	kāryaṃ sādhanamiṣṭasya bhagavāniṣṭadevatā / mukhyeṣyaṃ vā sumanasāṃ preyastaditi ca śrutiḥ //
[1,1.46]	prāṇabuddhimanaḥkhātmadehāpatyadhanādayaḥ / yatsamparkāt priyā āsaṃstataḥ ko nvaparaḥ priyaḥ //
[1,1.47]	ityādivākyairākāṅkṣāsannidhiryogyatā yataḥ / asminneva samastasyetīṣye vyutpattiriṣyate //
[1,1.48]	attyapūpāṃstava bhrātetyādāvāvāpato 'pi ca / udvāpād vartamānatvādākāṅkṣādibalādapi //
[1,1.49]	bālo vyutpattimapyeti nānayetyādivākyataḥ / ānīyamānadṛṣṭayaiva vyutpatteḥ sambhave sati //
[1,1.50]	eṣyadānayanāyāyaṃ kuta eva pratīkṣate / vyutpanno vartamāne tu kriyāśabde bhaviṣyati //
[1,1.51]	punardṛṣṭyaiva śabdaśrut paścāt vyutpattimeṣyati / vartamānamatītaṃ ca bhaviṣyaditi ca kramāt //
[1,1.52]	ākāṅkṣādiyutaṃ yasmād vidhervyutpādanaṃ kutaḥ / dṛṣṭyā jñātapadārthasya padākāṅkṣā bhaviṣyati //
[1,1.53]	vyutpattiḥ prathamā tasmād vatarmāne gate tataḥ / iṣṭamākāṅkṣate sarvo na pravṛttimapekṣate //
[1,1.54]	aparokṣaṃ parokṣaṃ vā jñānamiṣṭasya sādhanam / kvāpi ceṣyā tadarthā syādattirhi rasavittaye //
[1,1.55]	vākyārthajñānamātreṇa kvacidiṣṭaṃ bhavedapi / na ca srukasruvavahnayādāvatātparyaṃ śruterbhavet //
[1,1.56]	yatkiñcitkaraṇarasyāpi yajñataivānyathā bhavet / tasmādupāsanārthaṃ ca svārthe tātparyavad bhavet //
[1,1.57]	iti śabdonnaye 'gnāvityunnīte smṛtirbhavet / itiśabdavyapetāni hyapi santi vacāṃsyalam //
[1,1.58]	ātmānamevetyādīni yoge 'gnāvapi tat samam / ekavākyatvayoge tu vedasyāpi hyaśeṣataḥ //
[1,1.59]	vākyabhedo na yuktaḥ syād yogaśca syānmahāphale / iti brūyāditi vaco gatamagnau samīpagam //
[1,1.60]	kalpanāgauravaṃ cet syāt pṛthak tātparyasambhave / kalpanāgauravādeva padārthā na syureva hi //
[1,1.61]	pramāṇāvagatatvaṃ cet tātparyāṇaśaṃ tathaiva hi / tasmāt padārthe vākyārthe tātparyamubhayatra ca //
[1,1.62]	pṛthageva ca vākyatvaṃ pṛthaganvayato bhavet / avāntaratvād vākyānāṃ vākyabhedo na dūṣaṇam //
[1,1.63]	aṅgīkṛtatvādapi taiḥ padārthānāṃ pṛthak pṛthak / kriyāpadenānvayasya vākyabhedāddhi dūṣaṇam //
[1,1.64]	pratyakṣādivirodhe 'to gauṇārthasyāpi sambhavāt / atātparyaṃ padārthe 'pi na kalpyamavirodhataḥ //
[1,1.65]	ato jñānaphalānyeva karmāṇi jñānameva hi / mukhyaprasādadaṃ viṣṇorjijñāsāyāśca tad bhavet //
[1,1.66]	kartavyā tena jijñāsā śrutiprāmāṇyayogataḥ / pratyakṣavacca prāmāṇyaṃ svata evāgamasya hi //
[1,1.67]	anavasthānyathā hi syādaprāmāṇyaṃ tathānyataḥ / mithyājñaptipralambhādestena vedavirodhi yat //
[1,1.68]	na mānamapi vedānāmaṅgīkāryā hi nityatā / na hi dharmādisiddhiḥ syānnityavākyaṃ vinā kvacit //
[1,1.69]	avipralambhastajjñānaṃ tatkṛtatvādayo 'pi ca / kalpyā gauravadoṣeṇa puṃvākyaṃ jñāpakaṃ na tat //
[1,1.70]	pratyakṣaḥ kasyacid dharmo vastutvāditi codite / na buddho dharmadarśī syāt puṃstvādityanumāhatiḥ //
[1,1.71]	adharmavādino vākyamaprayojanameva hi / dharmābhāvo 'pi no tena pratyakṣāvagato bhavet //
[1,1.72]	ataḥ saṃśayasampattau vākyaṃ pratyakṣavat pramā / śaktiścaivānvite svārthe śabdānāmanubhūyate //
[1,1.73]	ato 'nvitābhidhāyitvaṃ gauravaṃ kalpane 'nyathā / nacāśakyābhidhāyitvaṃ pravṛttiśca dvidhānyathā //
[1,1.74]	etat sarvaṃ tarkaśāstre brahmatarke hi vistarāt / uktaṃ vidyāpṛthaktavāttu saṅkṣepeṇātra sūcitam //
[1,1.75]	pramāṇanyāyasacchikṣā kriyate tarkaśāstrataḥ / mānanyāyaistu tatsiddhaimīmāṃsā meyaśodhanam //
[1,1.76]	brahmatarkaṃ ca bhagavān sa eva kṛtavān prabhuḥ / pañcāśatkoṭivistārānnārāyaṇatanau kṛtāt //
[1,1.77]	uddhṛtya pañcasāhasraṃ kṛtavān bādarāyaṇaḥ / atastadarthaṃ saṅkṣepādata ityabhyasūcayat //
[1,1.78]	yato 'nubhavataḥ sarvaṃ siddhametadato 'pi ca / devaiśca durgamārtheṣu vyāpṛto nātivistṛtim //
[1,1.79]	cakāraitā hyavajñeyā yuktayaḥ pratipakṣagāḥ / pratyakṣekṣākṣamaḥ pakṣaṃ kamevātrābhivīkṣate //
[1,1.80]	tasmādakṣamapakṣatvānmokṣaśāstre 'bhyupekṣitaḥ / svayaṃ bhagavatā viṣṇurbrahmetyetat puroditam //
[1,1.81]	sa viṣṇurāha hīyante devaśāstrasya tena hi / ādyantaṃ devaśāstrasya svayaṃ bhagavatā kṛtam //
[1,1.82]	madhyaṃ tadājñayā pailaśeṣābhyāṃ kṛtamañjasā / atastatraiva viṣṇutvasiddherbrahmetyasūcayat //
[1,1.83]	doṣāracchidraśabdānāṃ paryāyatvaṃ yatastataḥ / guṇā nārā iti jñeyastadvān nārāyaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ //
[1,1.84]	brahmaśabdo 'pi hi guṇapūrtimeva vadatyayam / ato nārāyaṇasyaiva jijñāsātra vidhīyate //
[1,1.85]	siddhatvād brahmaśabdasya viṣṇau spaṣṭatayā śrutau / ambhasyapāra ityukto nārāyaṇapaderitaḥ //
[1,1.86]	āpo nārā iti hyāha sa evāpsvantarīritaḥ / kāmato vidhirudrādipadadātṛyā svayaṃ śriyā //
[1,1.87]	yonitvenātmano viṣṇostiṣṭhantītyuditasya ca / yasmin devā adhītyuktavā samudraṃ sthānameva ca //
[1,1.88]	nāma cākṣaramityeva ṛca ityuditaṃ tu yat / yataḥ prasūtetyuktavā ca tadeva brahma cābravīt //
[1,1.89]	antaḥsamudragaṃ viśvaprasūteḥ kāraṇaṭha tu yat / sūktopaniṣadādyuktaṃ janmādyasyeti lakṣyate //
[1,1.90]	sṛṣṭiḥ sthitiśca saṃhāro niyatirjñānamāvṛtiḥ / bandhamokṣāvapi hyāsu śrutiṣūktā hareḥ sadā //
[1,1.91]	yaṃ nāmāni viśantyaddhā yo devānāmiti hyapi / śruternāmāni sarvāṇi viṣṇoreva yatastataḥ //
[1,1.92]	ato na mukhyato nāma tadanyasya hi kasyacit / guṇāḥ śrutā iti hyasmānna doṣo 'rthaḥ śruterbhavet //
[1,1.93]	prītyā mokṣaparatvācca tātparyaṃ naiva dūṣaṇe / sarveṣāmapi vākyānāṃ mahātātparyamatra hi //
[1,1.94]	tadvirodhe na mānatvaṃ phalaṃ muktirhi vākyataḥ / na purāṇādimānatvaṃ viruddhārthe śruterbhavet //
[1,1.95]	darśanāntaramūlatvānmohārthaṃ cājñayā hareḥ / na sarvanāmatānyeṣāṃ śrutāvuktā hi kutracit //
[1,1.96]	adoṣavacanāccaiva niyamena hareḥ śrutau / ajñānaṃ pāratantryaṃ ca praḷaye 'bhāva eva ca //
[1,1.97]	aśaktiścoditānyeṣāṃ sarveṣāmapi ca śrutau / janmādyasyeti tenaitad viṣṇoreva svalakṣaṇam //
[1,1.98]	asyodbhavādihetutvaṃ sākṣādeva svalakṣaṇam / kṛṣṇaddhayānacchalenaiva svayaṃ bhāgavate 'bravīt //
[1,1.99]	ato jīvaikyamapi sa nirācakre jagadguruḥ / na hi janmādihetutvaṃ jīvasya jagato bhavet //
[1,1.100]	hitākriyādidoṣaṃ ca vakṣyatyeva svayaṃ prabhuḥ / nirguṇatvaṃ ca tenaiva niṣiddhaṃ prabhuṇā svayam //
[1,1.101]	bhedenaiva tu mukhyārthasambhave lakṣaṇā kutaḥ / kathaṃ nityaguṇasyāsya syādaikyaṃ guṇahānataḥ //
[1,1.102]	sadaiva guṇavattve 'sya bhinnaṃ syānnirguṇaṃ sadā / na ca mithyāguṇatvaṃ syādanirvācyasya dūṣaṇāt //
[1,1.103]	nirguṇatvaṃ tadā ca syādāsuratvaṃ nacānyathā / lakṣyalakṣaṇayorbhedo 'bhedo vā yadi vobhayam //
[1,1.104]	iti pṛṣṭe tadaikyasya gatireva na vidyate / aikyābhede na śāstreṇa jñeyaṃ tat svaprakāśataḥ //
[1,1.105]	bhede mithyātvato bhedasatyatvaṃ syād balādapi / bhedābhedau yadi tadā syādeva hyanavasthitiḥ //
[1,1.106]	svanirvāhakatā cet syād bāhyaṃ bāhakamityapi / paryāyo bhedavān vā syādanavasthobhayatra ca //
[1,1.107]	satyajñānādike 'pyeva na vyāvṛttyā prayojanam / vyāvṛttasyāviśeṣatve tadakhaṇḍaṃ ca khaṇḍitam / nirviśeṣatvametena mūko 'hamitivad bhavet //
[1,1.108]	abhinne 'pi viśeṣo 'yaṃ balādāpatati hyataḥ / viśeṣatadvatoścaiva svanirvāhakatā bhavet //
[1,1.109]	bhedahīne tvaparyāyaśabdāntaraniyāmakaḥ / viśeṣo nāma kathitaḥ so 'sti vastuṣvaśeṣataḥ //
[1,1.110]	viśeṣāste 'pyanantāśca parasparaviśeṣiṇaḥ / svanirvāhakatāyuktāḥ santi vastuṣvaśeṣataḥ //
[1,1.111]	ato 'nantaguṇaṃ brahma nirbhedamapi bhaṇyate / evaṃ dharmāniti śrutyā tadabhedo 'pyudīryate //
[1,1.112]	śaivādyāgamasamprāptadṛṣṭagena phalena tu / tadvākyopamayānyacca pramāṇatve 'numīyate //
[1,1.113]	īśavākyatvata iti cet tadgavyabhicāriṇā / aprāmāṇyānumā ca syānna pṛthak cānumeśvare //
[1,1.114]	puṃstvahetubalādeva pūrvoktenaiva vartmanā / śāstrayonitvametena kāraṇasya balād bhavet //
[1,1.115]	nāvedavinna tarkeṇa matirityādivākyataḥ / tarko jñāpayituṃ śakto neśitāraṃ kathañcana //
[1,1.116]	vanakṛttvādirūpeṇa pakṣabhūtasya ceśituḥ / kiñcijjñānaṃ hi puṃstvena śakyaṃ sādhayituṃ sukham //
[1,1.117]	vṛkṣakṛnnākhilaṃ vṛkṣaṃ vetti puṃstvāddhi caitravat / ityādyanumayā spardhi nānumānaṃ pareśituḥ / śaktaṃ vijñāpane cātiprasaṅgo 'numayedṛśā //
[1,1.118]	vastutvāt turagaḥ śṛṅgī puṣpavat khaṃ sutairyutā / citriṇī ca rasaḥ ṣaṣṭho rasatvāt sottaro bhavet / upakramādiliṅgebhyo nānyāsyādanumā tataḥ //
[1,1.119]	ta evānvayanāmānastaiḥ samyak pravicārite / mukhyārtho bhagavān viṣṇuḥ sarvaśāstrasya nāparaḥ //
[1,1.120]	īkṣaṇīyatvato viṣṇurvācya eva nacānyathā / lakṣyatvaṃ kvāpi dṛṣṭaṃ hi kiṃ tadityanavasthitiḥ //
[1,1.121]	mādhuryādiviśeṣāśca tacchabdairuditāḥ sadā / vākyārtho 'pi hi vākyārthaśabdenaivodito bhavet //
[1,1.122]	nāvācyaṃ tena kiñcit syād yata ityādikairvadan / avācyatvaṃ kathaṃ brūyānmūko 'hamitivat sudhīḥ //
[1,1.123]	yena lakṣyamiti proktaṃ lakṣyaśabdena so 'vadat / ekasyāpi hi śabdasya gauṇārthasvīkṛtau satām //
[1,1.124]	mahatī jāyate lajjā yatra tatrākhilā ravāḥ / amukhyārthā iti vadan yastanmārgānuvartinām / kathaṃ na jāyate lajjā vaktuṃ śābdatvamātmanaḥ //
[1,1.125]	ātmabrahmādayaḥ śabdāḥ sākṣāt pūrṇābhidhāyinaḥ / janmādikāraṇaṃ brahma lakṣitaṃ ca yadā tadā //
[1,1.126]	vandhyāputropamaṃ māyāśabalaṃ vācyamityapi / kalpayitvā vinā mānaṃ lakṣyaṃ śuddhaṃ vadan padaiḥ //
[1,1.127]	ātmaśabdoditasyaiva jñānaṃ muktāvasādhanam / āha śrutaparityāgaḥ syāccāsyāśrutakalpanam //
[1,1.128]	syāt sarvatra ca yatraikamapi loko jugupsate / niyamenobhayaṃ syāddhi yasya svaparayormate //
[1,1.129]	alaṅkṛtaḥ sadaivāyaṃ durghaṭaireva bhūṣaṇaiḥ / andhantamo nityuduḥkhaṃ tasya syād vasanadvayam //
[1,1.130]	anandā nāma te lokā andhena tamasā'vṛtāḥ / tāṃste pretyābhigacchantyavidvāṃso budho janāḥ //
[1,1.131]	asuryā nāma te lokā andhena tamasā'vṛtāḥ / tāṃste pretyābhigacchanti ye kecātmahano janāḥ //
[1,1.132]	ityādiśrutayo mānaṃ śataśo 'tra samantataḥ / heyatvāvacanāccaiva nātmā gauṇaḥ śrutau śrutaḥ //
[1,1.133]	tamevaikaṃ jānathānyā vāco muñcatha ceti ha / ukta ātmā kathaṃ gauṇo heyapakṣe hyasau śrutaḥ //
[1,1.134]	parivāratayā grāhyā api heyāḥ pradhānataḥ / pūrṇasya pūrṇamādāya pūrṇamevāvaśiṣyate //
[1,1.135]	iti svasyaiva pūrṇasya pūrṇe 'pyaya udāhṛtaḥ / kathaṃ māyāvyavacchinnaḥ pūrṇo mukhyatayā bhavet //
[1,1.136]	padaṃ ca nirguṇa iti kathaṃ gauṇaṃ vadiṣyati / guṇābhāvopalakṣyaṃ cet padaṃ tadapi vācakam //
[1,1.137]	ato 'navasthitimukhasarvadoṣamahāspadam / kathametanmataṃ sadbhirādriyeta vicakṣaṇaiḥ //
[1,1.138]	na ca sāṅkhayanirākṛtyai sūtrāṇyetānyacīkḷpat / bhagavān nahyaśabdatvaṃ pradhāne 'ṅgīkarotyasau //
[1,1.139]	samanvaye pratijñāte śabdagocarataiva hi / prathamapratipādyā syāt tadabhāve kuto 'nvayaḥ //
[1,1.140]	kathaṃ ca lakṣaṇāvādī brūyād brahmasamanvayam / yo 'sau śabdasya mukhyārthastatraiva syāt samanvayaḥ //
[1,1.141]	janmādikāraṇe sākṣādāha devaḥ samanvayam / uktaṃ tadeva jijñāsyaṃ kvāvakāśo 'tra nirguṇe //
[1,1.142]	kathañcāsambhavastasya mukhyārthasya nirākṛtau / mānena kena vijñeyamavācyājñeyanirguṇam //
[1,1.143]	ameyaṃ cenna śāstrasya tatra vṛttiḥ kathañcana / tasmācchāstreṇa jijñāsyamasmadīyaṃ guṇārṇavam //
[1,1.144]	vāsudevākhyamadvandvaṃ paraṃ brahmākhilottamam / vijñeyavācyalakṣyatvapūrvāśeṣaviśeṣataḥ //
[1,1.145]	nirgataṃ manaso vāco yadi tat syādagocaram / astu tanmā vaded vādī nacāsmacchāstragaṃ tu tat //
[1,1.146]	avācyaṃ vācyamityuktavā kimityunmattavanmṛṣā / asmacchāstrasya cauryāya yatate svoktidūṣakaḥ //
[1,1.147]	janmādikāraṇaṃ yattat sākṣānnārāyaṇābhidham / vadantu śrutayo brahma śāstraṃ caitat tadarthataḥ //
[1,1.148]	svaprakāśatvamapi tu yairjñānasya nivāritam / kathaṃ sarvajñatā tasya svajñānādhigamaṃ vinā //
[1,1.149]	pravṛttamastvavācyaṃ te maiva brūyāḥ kathañcana / sarvaśabdairavācyaṃ taduktavā tadviṣayaṃ punaḥ //
[1,1.150]	vayaṃ tvāṃ śrutiyuktibhyāṃ baddhvāsmacchāstramañjasā / vicārayāmaḥ śrutibhiryuktibhiścaiva sādaram //
[1,1.151]	adbhutatvādavācyaṃ tadatarkyājñeyameva ca / anantaguṇapūrṇatvādityūde paiṅgināṃ śrutiḥ / avācyamiti loke 'pi vaktayāścāryatamaṃ bhuvi //
[1,1.152]	evaṃ śāstrāvagamyatve vibhāgena samanvayam / ānandamaya ityādinādhyāyena vadatyajaḥ //
[1,1.153]	tatrānyatra prasiddhānāṃ viṣṇāveva samanvayam / śabdānāṃ prathame pāde guṇisāmānyavācinām //
[1,1.154]	guṇavācināṃ ca prathamamāha devaḥ samanvayam / samudraśāyinaṃ sarvaprasūtiprasavaṃ śrutiḥ //
[1,1.155]	tadeva brahma paramamiti sāvadhṛtirjagau / yato 'to brahmaśabdasya tatraiva niyatatvataḥ //
[1,1.156]	yo 'nnaṃ brahmetyādirūpādabhyāsāt taittirīyake / anyāsu caitadrūpāsu śākhāsvapi sahasraśaḥ //
[1,1.157]	ānandamaya ityādyaiḥ śabdairvācyo hariḥ svayam / upalakṣaṇatvaṃ śabdānāmānandamayapūrviṇām //
[1,1.158]	sūtrasyālpākṣaratvena sarvaśākhāvinirṇaye / punaśca prāpakāddhetostatrādhikaraṇāntaram //
[1,1.159]	sarve vedā āmananti yat padaṃ tviti hi śrutiḥ / ānandamayarūpe tu brahmaṇaḥ pucchatoktitaḥ //
[1,1.160]	samastābrahmatāprāpterānandamayanāma hi / brahmaśabdasya cābhyāsāt pañcarūpādiṣu sphuṭam //
[1,1.161]	brahmatāvayave 'pi syāt tathāvayavini svataḥ / yathaiva kṛṣṇakeśasya kṛṣṇasya brahmatākhilā //
[1,1.162]	darśitā caiva pārthāya niḥsīmāḥ śaktayo 'sya hi / ṛtaṃ satyaṃ paraṃ brahma puruṣaṃ kṛṣṇapiṅgalam //
[1,1.163]	viṣṇvākhyamuktamanyatra hyūrdhvaretaṃ ca tat prati / virūpākṣākhyamavaraṃ brahmoktaṃ tadvrate sthitam //
[1,1.164]	samānādhikṛtatvaṃ ceduttaraṃ nīlalohitam / kṛṣṇapiṅgalarūpeṇa punaruktaṃ bhaviṣyati //
[1,1.165]	brahmādhipatirityatra tāpanīyaśrutau puraḥ / svaritabrahmaśabdāntaṃ bahuvrīhitvameṣyati //
[1,1.166]	svāhendraśatruvardhasva yad bahuvrīhitāmagāt / mahāvyākaraṇe sūtramiti svaravinirṇaye //
[1,1.167]	pūrvāntasvarite puṃsorbahuvrīhitvameṣyati / mahāvyākaraṇe sūtramiti svaravinirṇaye //
[1,1.168]	ṛtaṃ satyaṃ paraṃ brahmetyādyuddeśyadvitīyakā / vibhaktirūrdhvaretādiḥ prathamā rudragocarā //
[1,1.169]	tasmād viṣṇuṃ paraṃ brahma prati rudro vrate sthitaḥ / ūrdhvaretā iti hyeva śrutyartho 'vasito bhavet //
[1,1.170]	ṛtaṃ satyaṃ paraṃ brahma prati viṣṇuṃ sadāśivaḥ / ūrdhvaretā dhyāyati ha śaṅkaro nīlalohitaḥ //
[1,1.171]	ityarthametamevāha nīlagrīvaśrutiḥ parā / ārtharvaṇī paraṃ brahma tasmādeko hariḥ śrutau //
[1,1.172]	tadevartamiti prāha kathamevānyathā śrutiḥ / avadhārayantī tasyaiva hyṛtatvādikamañjasā //
[1,1.173]	eko nārāyaṇa āsīnna brahmā na ca śaṅkaraḥ / vāsudevo 'gra evāsīnna brahmā na ca śaṅkaraḥ //
[1,1.174]	nendrasūryau na ca guho na somo na vināyakaḥ / ityādivākyato viṣṇorutpattiravatāragā //
[1,1.175]	mukhyaṃ brahma haristasmāt prastāvaḥ paramityapi / mukhyabrahmagrahe yukte nāmukhyaṃ yujyate kvacit //
[1,1.176]	asambhave hi mukhyasya gauṇārthāṅgīkṛtirbhavet / prācuryārthāśca mayaṭaḥ sarve 'tra pratipāditāḥ //
[1,1.177]	bhogyatvamatra cādyatvamupajīvyatayā hareḥ / mahābhoktā mahābhogya ityartho 'nnamaye bhavet //
[1,1.178]	mahāprāṇo mahābodho mahāvijñānavānapi / viśeṣasāmānyatayā vijñānaṃ mana ityapi //
[1,1.179]	ekasya jñānarūpasya hareruktirvibhāgataḥ / abhede 'pi viśeṣeṇaivānya ityudito hariḥ //
[1,1.180]	bhedaśabdā viśeṣaṃ tu harāvanyatra bhinnatvāt / brūyurharerjīvajaḍairapi bhedaṃ hi mukhyataḥ //
[1,1.181]	brahmatarkavaco 'pyevamata ekaḥ sa pañcadhā / ukto 'nnamaya ityādi bhṛgoścaitad vadiṣyati //
[1,1.182]	prāpyatvena mayaṭprokterna tatrāpyanyaducyate / pracurānnādirevāto hyannamannamayetyapi //
[1,1.183]	ucyate hyaviśeṣeṇa nānyat kiñcidihocyate / mahānandatva evāsya hetuḥ ko 'nyāditi sphuṭam //
[1,1.184]	uktaḥ śrutyantare yasmāt sukhaṃ labdhvā karotyayam / karoti nāsukhī bhūmā sukhaṃ nālpe sukhaṃ bhavet //
[1,1.185]	ityuktaṃ yat pravṛttiśca nṛttagānādikā sukhāt / duḥkhād rodādikā caiva sarvakartṛtvato 'sya ca //
[1,1.186]	sarvaśakter na duḥkhaṃ syādataḥ kevalalīlayā / pravartako na cedeṣa prāṇyādanyācca kaḥ pumān //
[1,1.187]	brahmavit paramāpnotīti yat prathamasūcitam / tadeva mantravarṇena satyaṃ jñānamanantavat //
[1,1.188]	lakṣitaṃ tatra satyatvaṃ sṛṣṭayānnaprāṇayorapi / uktaṃ jñānaṃ tu manasā vijñānenāpyudīritam //
[1,1.189]	anantatvaṃ tathā'nandamayavācāpyudāhṛtam / sadbhāvaṃ yāpayed yasmāt satyaṃ tat tena kathyate //
[1,1.190]	iti sṛṣṭiriha proktā jagatsadbhāvayāpakam / brahmeti sthāpanāyaiva sattvaṃ jīvanameva ca //
[1,1.191]	viśīrṇatā ca sattvaṃ syāt sannamityāhureva yat / ato 'dyatāttṛtānnatvaṃ satyaśabdārtha eva hi //
[1,1.192]	prāṇaṃ devā anuprāṇanti manuṣyāḥ paśavaśca ye / āyuḥ prāṇo hi bhūtānāmiti yad gatijīvane //
[1,1.193]	ukte saditidhātvartho gatiścāto hi satyatā / prāṇatvamavabodhārtho manudhātuḥ prakīrtitaḥ //
[1,1.194]	nālpe sukhamiti proktayaivānandamayatoktitaḥ / anantatvaṃ sunirṇītaṃ pūrṇānando hi nālpake //
[1,1.195]	ato hi mantravarṇoktavistṛtistu samastayā / kriyate parayā yasmāditaro 'tra na kathyate //
[1,1.196]	puruṣaṃ vetti yo mucyennānyaḥ panthā hi vidyate / iti śruteranyavedī kathaṃ muktiṃ prayāsyati //
[1,1.197]	puruṣaḥ para ātmājo brahma nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ / mahānānanda ud viṣṇurbharga oma itīryate //
[1,1.198]	svayaṃ nārāyaṇo devo nānyasyaitāni kasyacit / tasmādomityudāhṛtya yajñadānādi kurvate //
[1,1.199]	sūktena pauruṣeṇainaṃ yajantyadhyātmakovidāḥ / iti paiṅgiśrutistena nānyajñānād vimucyate //
[1,1.200]	brahmaśabdodite tasminnātmaśabdaṃ prayujya ca / tasmādākāśasṛṣṭiṃ ca provācātra catuvirdhām //
[1,1.201]	bhūtaṃ bhūtābhimānī ca taddeho 'ntarniyāmakaḥ / hariścākāśaśabdokto mukhyato harireva ca //
[1,1.202]	ā samantāt kāśate yadākāśo mukhyato hariḥ / balajñānasvarūpatvād vāyuragniragaṃ nayan //
[1,1.203]	āpa āpālanāccaiva pṛthivī prathito yataḥ / uṣyānāmāśrayatvena sa evoṣadhināmakaḥ //
[1,1.204]	oṣadhīṣu sthito viṣṇuḥ kṣudhitairāśrito bhavet / puri śete yataḥ so 'tha puruṣaśceti gīyate //
[1,1.205]	kriyāpravartakatvena prādurbhāvo harerjaniḥ / ākāśādiṣu nānyāsti hyabhimāno 'bhimāninaḥ //
[1,1.206]	abhimāniśarīrasya sākṣād bhūtasya codbhavaḥ / evaṃ dehādiparyantamāgataṃ harimeva tu //
[1,1.207]	parāmṛśati tasyaiva pañcarūpatvavittaye / tyaktavā bhūtādikaṃ sarvaṃ sa vā eṣa iti śrutiḥ //
[1,1.208]	sa ityātmapadoddiṣṭa eṣa jīvaśarīragaḥ / sārānnamaya evāyaṃ na lokānnamayaḥ prabhuḥ //
[1,1.209]	iti taṃ rasaśabdena viśinaṣṭi śarīragam / idamityeva nirdeśo vastraprāvṛtavad vibhoḥ //
[1,1.210]	śira āderbhavejjīvaśira ādau vyavasthiteḥ / taṃ viditvāsya muktiḥ syānnānyajñānāt kathañcana //
[1,1.211]	āditye puruṣe cāyamiti bhedopadeśataḥ / nāsyābhedo 'sti jīvena nānumā kāmacāriṇī //
[1,1.212]	vimatāni śarīrāṇi madbhogāyatanāni yat / śarīrāṇītyādikā tu tattvajñāne hyapekṣyate //
[1,1.213]	pratyakṣādiviruddhatvādakṣāgamabhayojkhitā / anumā kāmavṛttā hi kutra nāvasaraṃ vrajet //
[1,1.214]	jaḍa ātmaiva vastutvāt prameyatvājjaḍaṃ citiḥ / ghana ākāśa ityādyā vāryante kena hetunā //
[1,1.215]	na jīvabhedasūtrāṇāṃ śaṅkayātra punaruktatā / vākyāntaradyotakatvāt pṛthagityatra pūrṇatā / yogamannamayādyairyat phalatvenāsya śaṃsati / sthānadvaye 'pyataḥ kośā eta ityatisāhasam //
[1,1.216]	upasaṅkramaṇaṃ caiva dvitīyoddeśitaṃ prati / atikramaṃ vadantaṃ tamupaśabdo nivārayet //
[1,1.217]	aśrutasyātiśabdasya sthānaṃ dadyāt kathaṃ punaḥ / śrutāśrutaparityāgakalpane vigatahriyām //
[1,1.218]	mṛtāveva parityāgaḥ kṛto hyannamayasya ca / ye 'nnaṃ brahmetyādyupāsāṃ sāmānādhikaraṇyataḥ //
[1,1.219]	uktavā pañcasvarūpāṇāṃ punastatprāptivādinī / sthānadvayagatā vedavāṇī tadapalāpinām //
[1,1.220]	tamaso 'nyatra saṃsthānaṃ kathameva saheta sā / adhīhi bhagavo brahmetyukto 'nnaprāṇapūrvakam //
[1,1.221]	āha brahma kathaṃ tanna dvāraṃ taditi vādinaḥ / upasattiṃ kathaṃ vidyurupasannāya hi triśaḥ //
[1,1.222]	vaktavyaṃ brahma guruṇā caturvāramathāpi vā / sakṛd vetyāgamā brūyuḥ sampradāyavido 'pi ca //
[1,1.223]	tad yatkiñcit kathaṃ brūyādupasannāya dikpatiḥ / na vaded brahma ca kathaṃ māyāvī na hi vārirāṭ //
[1,1.224]	caṣṭa ityeva taccakṣuḥ śravaṇācchrotramucyate / vacanādeva vāg brahma sṛṣṭisthityādikāraṇam //
[1,1.225]	tacca vāghūlaśākhāyāmaṣṭarūpamudāhṛtam / vijñānānandasahitaṃ pṛthak sṛṣṭayādilakṣaṇaiḥ //
[1,1.226]	āvāpodvāpataṣa śākhā yata āhuḥ paraṃ padam / yato bhūtāni jāyanta ityādyairlakṣaṇaiḥ svayam //
[1,1.227]	lakṣitaṃ guruṇā paścāt tapasaivāparokṣataḥ / dṛṣṭvaikaikaṃ svarūpaṃ tu samastoktānudarśanam //
[1,1.228]	icchatā'jñāṃ guroḥ prāpya tapasaivārokṣitam / abrahmetyeva vadatāṃ śrutahānyaśrutagrahau //
[1,1.229]	sākṣāllakṣaṇatāṃ prāptāviti lajjā taduktiṣu / samīpe sahabhogasya muktitvenoktito 'sakṛt //
[1,1.230]	bhedo jīveśayormithyetyeva mithyā svayaṃ bhavet / etena mayaṭaścaiva dvaividhyenārthakalpanāt / tadanyeṣāṃ matamapi satsaṃsatsu na bhāsate //
[1,1.231]	ato nārāyaṇo devo niḥśeṣaguṇavācakaiḥ / guṇisāmānyavacanairapi mukhyatayoditaḥ //
[1,1.232]	adhyātmagaiśca prāṇādyaistathaiva hyadhibhūtagaiḥ / annādiśabdairbhagavāneko mukhyatayoditaḥ //
[1,1.233]	janmādyasyeti sūtreṇa guṇasarvasvasiddhaye / brahmaṇo lakṣaṇaṃ proktaṃ śāstramūlaṃ yatastataḥ //
[1,1.234]	anvayaḥ sarvaśabdānāṃ guṇasarvasvavedakaḥ / śabdapravṛttihetūnāṃ tasmin mukhyasamanvayāt //
[1,1.235]	anyārtheṣvalpatāhetostannimittatvatastathā / tadvācakatvaṃ śabdānāṃ bahulātiprayogataḥ //
[1,1.236]	rūḍhamityeva sādhyaṃ syād rūḍhirhi dvividhā matā / avidvadvidvadāptyaiva mukhyā hi viduṣāṃ tu sā //
[1,1.237]	vidvadrūḍhirvaidikā syāt sā yogādeva labhyate / tasmānmukhyārthatā viṣṇoriti kṛtvā hṛdi prabhuḥ //
[1,1.238]	samanvayaṃ sādhayati devānāṃ tatra śaktatām / āśaṅkaya tatra rūḍhiṃ ca tacchabdānāmapi svayam //
[1,1.239]	samudrāntasthitatvādyaistaddharmairviṣṇurūḍhatām / sādhayitvābhidāṃ taiśca punareva nyavārayat //
[1,1.240]	ceṣṭā hi cetanānāṃ yā sā bhavet tatprasādataḥ / acetanasvabhāvastu vivarādiḥ kathaṃ tataḥ //
[1,1.241]	iti śaṅkānivṛttyarthamākāśa iti nāma ca / parato 'pivarīyastvapūrvālliṅgāddharerbhavet //
[1,1.242]	iti śaṅkānivṛttyarthamākāśa iti nāma ca / parato 'pi varīyastva pūrvālliṅgāddharerbhavet //
[1,1.243]	prāṇādihetutādṛṣṭeratideśo hi tādṛśaḥ / liṅgaṃ balavadeva syāt prerako 'syāpi yaddhariḥ //
[1,1.244]	nityatvādeva śabdasya tatsvabhāvaḥ kathaṃ hareḥ / kathaṃ prasiddhabahulaśabdānāmayathārthatā //
[1,1.245]	iti cet taddharereva bāhulyācchrutiliṅgayoḥ / tādṛśatvācca tacchakterbāhulye śrutiliṅgayoḥ //
[1,1.246]	anyasya mukhyavācyatvamiti tannātragasya hi / viṣṇoreva tu liṅgāni prāṇasthāni tu sarvaśaḥ //
[1,1.247]	prāṇasaṃvādapūrvāṇi mukhyato jīvagāni ca / abhyārcacchatavarṣāṇi prāṇavaṃśatvamityapi //
[1,1.248]	tasmādanyatragaiḥ śabdairuktanyāyaiḥ samantataḥ / eko nārāyaṇo devo bhaṇyate nātra saṃśayaḥ //
[1,1.249]	vāsudevādirūpeṇa caturmūrtiśca sarvaśaḥ / athavā pañcamūrtiḥ sa prokto 'dhikaraṇaṃ prati //
[1,1.250]	pratisūtraṃ pratipadaṃ pratyakṣaramathāpi vā / taistairyuktiśrutinyāyaviśeṣairyogyatā yathā //
[1,1.251]	bṛhattantrapramāṇena bahvarthamapi saṅgrahāt / ucyate narabuddhīnāmapi kiñcidgrahārthataḥ //
[1,1.252]	grantho 'yamapi bahvartho bhāṣyaṃ cātyarthavistaram / bahujñā eva jānanti viśeṣaṇārthametayoḥ / tasmānmahāguṇo viṣṇurnāmnāyapunaruktitaḥ //
<iti śrīmadānandatīrthabhagavatpādācāyarviracite śrīmadbrahmasūtrānuvyākhyāne prathamādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pādaḥ ||>
{1,2}
[1,2.1]	liṅgātmakānāṃ śabdānāṃ vṛttirnārāyaṇe pare / cintyate sarvagatvaṃ tu prathamaṃ pravicāryate //
[1,2.2]	tatra tatra sthito viṣṇustattacchaktiprabodhakaḥ / dūrato 'pyatiriktaḥ sa līlayā kevalaṃ prabhuḥ //
[1,2.3]	iti jñāpayituṃ karmakartrorutsargato bhidā / abhedo 'pi viśeṣe syād balī so 'pyanapoditaḥ //
[1,2.4]	etad bhāvābhidhaṃ liṅgaṃ kriyāliṅge tataḥ param / antaryāmyantaraśceti kriyābhāvākhyamucyate //
[1,2.5]	adṛśyatvādyabhāvākhyaṃ śrutirliṅgādhikā parā / anityatvāt kriyāṇāṃ tu kathameva svarūpatā //
[1,2.6]	iti cet sa viśeṣo 'pi kriyāśaktayātmanā sthiraḥ / śaktitā vyaktatā ceti viśeṣo 'pi viśeṣavān //
[1,2.7]	abhinno 'pi kriyādiśca svabhāva iti hi śrutiḥ / jñānaṃ nityaṃ kriyā nityā balaṃ śaktiḥ parātmanaḥ //
[1,2.8]	iti paiṅgiśrutiścāha śaktisadbhāva eva tu / kriyādinityatā jñeyā tadanyatra tvanityatā //
[1,2.9]	iti sattattvavacanaṃ dvitvaṃ caikasya yujyate / yaḥ seturiti caikatvavacanena viśeṣaṇāt //
[1,2.10]	antaḥ sthitvā ramaṇakṛdantaraḥ samudāhṛtaḥ / ramaṇaṃ cātmaśabdenādeyaṃ mātīti cocyate //
[1,2.11]	viśiṣṭasukhavattvācca brahmatvaṃ ca viśiṣṭatā / anyonyaniyatiśceśaniyame nānyathā bhavet //
[1,2.12]	cetanānāṃ viśeṣo yaḥ svabhāvo 'pīśvarāpirtaḥ / anyonyaniyame tasmādanavasthityasambhavau //
[1,2.13]	īśvaraścenniyantā ca sa eva prathamāgataḥ / kimityapodyate kasmād vṛthāvasthitikalpanā / doṣavatyeva tasmāt sā naiva kāryā kathañcana //
[1,2.14]	ramaṇaṃ nātiyatnasya vikṣepādeva yujyate / iti cet sarvaniyamo yasya kasmānna śakyate //
[1,2.15]	ātmanāniyataṃ vastu pratīpaṃ hyātmano bhavet / svādhīnasattāśaktayādi kathamātmapratīpakam //
[1,2.16]	guṇakriyādayo bhāvā yadivā syurabhedinaḥ / abhedo 'bhāvadharmāṇāṃ brahmaṇā yujyate katham //
[1,2.17]	nābhāvo bhāva iti ca viśeṣaḥ prāyaśo bhavet / atadbhāvo 'nyatā ceti na viśeṣo 'sti kaścana //
[1,2.18]	doṣābhāvo guṇa iti prasiddho laukikeṣvapi / adṛśyatvādikāṃstasmād guṇānāha svayaṃ prabhuḥ //
[1,2.19]	bhāvābhāvavirodho 'pi na tu sarvatra vidyate / tadabhāvo hi tadbhāvavirodhī na tato 'paraḥ //
[1,2.20]	pṛthaktavābhāvatadrūpān bhedāṃstrīn kalpayanti cet / kalpanāgauravādyāstu doṣāstatra virodhinaḥ //
[1,2.21]	pṛthaktavānyatvabhedāstu paryāyeṇaiva laukikaiḥ / vyavahriyante satataṃ vaidikairapi sarvaśaḥ //
[1,2.22]	dṛṣṭahāniradṛṣṭasya kalpanetyeva dūṣaṇam / yadā tadadhiko doṣo vidyate ko nu vādinām //
[1,2.23]	bhāvābhāvasvarūpāstu viśeṣā eva vastunaḥ / abhinnā eva saṅgrāhyā vyavahāraprasiddhaye //
[1,2.24]	yathaikaḥ samavāyo 'pi bhedābhedau ca vastuni / aṅgīkāryā viśeṣeṇa sthāneṣu vyavahartṛbhiḥ //
[1,2.25]	akhaṇḍavādino' pi syādviśeṣo 'nicchato 'pyasau / vyāvṛtte nirviśeṣe tu kiṃ vyāvartyabahutvataḥ //
[1,2.26]	bahuliṅgasamāyuktairbahubhī rūḍhanāmabhiḥ / prasiddhairanyagatvena vācyaḥ sākṣājjanārdanaḥ //
[1,2.27]	vaiśvānarādayaḥ śabdā api tadvācinastataḥ / tāni liṅgāni te śabdā api tadgā hi sarvaśaḥ / bahulāpyajñarūḍhistatprajñārūḍhiṃ na bādhate //
<iti śrīmadānandatīrthabhagavatpādaviracite śrīmadbrahmasūtrānuvyākhyāne prathamādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ ||>
{1,3}
[1,3.1]	tatrānyatra ca siddhānāṃ liṅganāmnāṃ punarhariḥ / viśeṣānmukhyato vṛttiṃ svasminnevātra vaktayajaḥ //
[1,3.2]	viṣṇāvevātmaśabdasya rūḍhatvānna śivādikān / śrutirvaktyakhileśatvād bhūmā viṣṇuḥ sukhādhikaḥ //
[1,3.3]	ato viruddhavad bhātamapi vyākhyāya tattvataḥ / yojanīyaṃ harau vākyaṃ viruddhairlakṣaṇairyutam //
[1,3.4]	brahmaiva tāni liṅgāni tadanyatra tvasantyapi / avirodhena govinde santyasthūlādikāni ca //
[1,3.5]	anyavastusvabhāvānāṃ sthaulyādīnāmapākṛtim / nārāyaṇe śrutirvakti natu tasyāsvabhāvatām //
[1,3.6]	sarvadharmā sarvanāmā sarvakarmā guṇāḥ śrutāḥ / doṣāḥ śrutāśca netyādyā pramāṇaṃ śrutiratra ca //
[1,3.7]	liṅgaṃ sādhāraṇaṃ śabdau sthānaṃ liṅgamanugrahaḥ / punaḥ śabdā liṅgaśabdau vicāryā dvisthitā iha //
[1,3.8]	bāhulyaṃ liṅgaśabdānāmanuktiśca viruddhatā / adṛṣṭiranvayābhāvo viparītaśrutibhramaḥ //
[1,3.9]	liṅgāvakāśarāhityabhramastādṛg dvayaṃ tathā / bahutādṛktavamuktasya virodho 'rthāt tathā gatiḥ / samastametadityatra pūrvapakṣeṣu yuktayaḥ //
[1,3.10]	tā eva balavantastu gatyantaravivarjitāḥ / siddhāntayuktayo jñeyā dṛśyante tāśca sarvaśaḥ //
[1,3.11]	muktopasṛpyatā prāṇādādhikyaṃ sarvatastathā / vailakṣaṇyaṃ svabhāvasya prekṣāpūrvakriyā tathā //
[1,3.12]	arasya ṇyasya ceśatvaṃ sūryādyanukṛtistathā / vāmanākhyā sarvakampastacchabdānanyasiddhatā //
[1,3.13]	anāmarūpatā bhedasyopajīvyapramāṇatā / sarvaiśvaryādikādyāstā vedeśena pradarśitāḥ //
[1,3.14]	adhikāraśca taddhāniḥ prasaṅgādeva cintitau / tatphalāya vidhiḥ siddhe copāsāyā nirākṛtaḥ //
[1,3.15]	yato jaimininānyārthamasiddhe 'rthe vidhistathā / vidyādhirājasya matamavirodhastayostataḥ //
[1,3.16]	mokṣe phalaviśeṣo 'sti na ca sarvaṃ prakāśate / sarvadā tena devānāmapi yuktā hyupāsanā //
[1,3.17]	nityaṃ vṛddhikṣayāpetaṃ viṣṇoḥ pūrṇaṃ tu vedanam / spaṣṭātispaṣṭaviśadaṃ brahmaṇo 'śeṣavastugam //
[1,3.18]	anyeṣāṃ kramaśo jñānaṃ mitavastugataṃ sadā / ityādayo viśeṣāstu sadā vidyāpaterhṛdi //
[1,3.19]	jaiminyādyāstu sāmānyavettṛtvāt tat tathāvadan / vidyeśamatametasmānnaiva sadbhirviruddhayate //
<iti śrīmadānandatīrthabhagavatpādācāryaviracite śrībrahmasūtrānuvyākhyāne prathamādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ ||>
{1,4}
[1,4.1]	duḥkhibaddhāvarādyāstu tadadhīnatvahetutaḥ / śabdā brahmaṇi vartante rājñi yadvat parājayaḥ //
[1,4.2]	svātantryaṃ tadgatatvaṃ ca śabdavṛtterhi kāraṇam / svātantryaṃ tatra mukhyaṃ syāt kuto rājñi jayo 'nyathā //
[1,4.3]	na hi bhṛtyasya vijayiśabdastāvat prayujyate / yāvad rājñyanyagatve 'pi svātantryābhāsamātrataḥ //
[1,4.4]	bhṛtyabandhādikaṃ rājñi rājño bandhādiyogyataḥ / kāraṇaṃ saṃśayasya syāditi naiva prayujyate //
[1,4.5]	amaṅgalatvācchabdānāṃ rājñā yogādamaṅgale / apriyatvāttu śabdasya syāt prayoganivartanam //
[1,4.6]	guṇāstu tādṛśā yatra prayujyante 'khilā api / pūjyeṣveva viśeṣeṇa svātantryaṃ mukhyakāraṇam //
[1,4.7]	tato doṣātidūratvāt saṃśayasyāpyasambhavāt / doṣāṇāṃ viṣṇugatvasya prājñabuddhivyapekṣayā //
[1,4.8]	svātantryārthamabhipretya doṣaśabdāśca viṣṇavi / vāsudevaśrutiścāha naiva viṣṇāvamaṅgalam //
[1,4.9]	maṅgalāmaṅgale 'nyatra tato nāmaṅgalaṃ vadet / svātantryāpekṣayā viṣṇau doṣo nāmaṅgaloktitaḥ //
[1,4.10]	bahubhuktavaṃ yathā doṣo nṛṣu naiva harau kvacit / evaṃ duḥkhyādiśabdāśca svātantryāpekṣayoditāḥ //
[1,4.11]	naiva doṣā harau tadgabuddhayoktā doṣakāriṇaḥ / tasmāt te doṣaśabdāśca tatraiva guṇavācakāḥ //
[1,4.12]	jātamotaṃ harau yasmājjyotiḥ ṣaḥ prāṇarūpataḥ / āyajñetaścāyajeto vasantiśca vasantataḥ //
[1,4.13]	vigatacchādanatvāt tu gaccha bhūtakṣayaṅkaraḥ / bhuṅkṣetyukto harir huṃ ca hutamasmin jagad yataḥ //
[1,4.14]	sphuṭatvāt phaḍiti proktaḥ kavarakṣaṇa ityataḥ / kavacaṃ vatarte yasmāt ṣaḍguṇatvena sarvadā / vaṣaṭ tadgatvatasteṣāṃ vauṣaḍityeva kathyate //
[1,4.15]	svīyaṃ svīkurute yasmāt svāhetyukto janārdanaḥ / namantyasmin guṇā yasyānnama ityeva kathyate //
[1,4.16]	ityaśeṣakriyānāmaśabdaireko janārdanaḥ / ucyate mukhyato yasmāt padavarṇasvarādibhiḥ //
[1,4.17]	tasmādanantaguṇatā śrutitātparyato 'sya hi / vijñānārthatvataḥ sarvaśabdānāṃ nāsti dūṣaṇam //
[1,4.18]	aṅgīkṛte 'pi naivāsti doṣo vākyasamanvaye / tadarthatvena karmādeḥ sambhavādalpabuddhaye //
[1,4.19]	kaśchandasāṃ yogamiti śruteryogārthatattvavit / brahmaiko naiva cānyo 'sti ka ityasyarobhayārthataḥ //
[1,4.20]	tasyāpi pūrvasiddhasya jñānameveti niścayāt / nityayogo 'pi śabdānāmarthairnaiva niṣiddhayate / strīśabdāśca niṣedhārthāḥ sarve 'pi brahmavācakāḥ //
[1,4.21]	virodhisarvabāhulyakāraṇastrīniṣedhinām / pṛthak samanvayārthāni sthānānyetāni sarvaśaḥ //
[1,4.22]	sarvamānairvirodhaśca vyutpatterapyaśakyatā / parasparavirodhaśca virodhaḥ kāryatadvatoḥ / strīliṅgatvaṃ niṣedhaśca pūrvapakṣeṣu hetavaḥ //
[1,4.23]	doṣātyaspṛṣṭiniyamaḥ śabdārthānekatā tathā / bahurūpatvamīśasya vyaktayavyaktiviśeṣitā //
[1,4.24]	utpādanaṃ svadehācca durjanāvyaktatā tathā / itayādyā yuktayaḥ sākṣāt siddhāntasthāpakā iha //
[1,4.25]	anvayaḥ sarvaśabdānāmaśakyo jñātumañjasā / iti yallokavaimukhyaṃ jaiminyādimataṃ vadan //
[1,4.26]	vidyādhinātho bhagavānapācakre svayaṃ prabhuḥ / svaśiṣyāṇāṃ prasiddhayarthaṃ matamātmīyamaṃśataḥ //
[1,4.27]	vijñātaṃ tairjagādātra tāratamyaṃ nṛṇāṃ vadan / teṣu teṣu padārtheṣu rūḍhiraṅgīkṛtā yataḥ //
[1,4.28]	prayojanabahutvena tasya tasyāvirodhataḥ / upadeśādisāmarthyād viṣṇau śaktiśca gṛhyate //
[1,4.29]	tathāpyetadvirodhe tu tadvācitvamapodyate / avirodhe tu bahvarthā etanmūlatayā matāḥ //
[1,4.30]	ito hi rūḍhatānyeṣāmupajīvyatvamatra hi / tatsiddhistadapekṣā ca sāpekṣā ca harīcchayā //
[1,4.31]	tasmāt paramamukhyatvaṃ viṣṇāvanyatra mukhyatā / upalakṣaṇā ca gauṇī ca tisraḥ śabdasya vṛttayaḥ //
[1,4.32]	pravṛttihetorbāhulyaṃ jñeyaṃ paramamukhyatā / tatra prayogabāhulyaṃ yadi tatparatā kimu //
[1,4.33]	ubhayaṃ dṛśyate viṣṇau śabdānāmapi sarvaśaḥ / prayogamātrabāhulyaṃ rūḍhirityabhidhīyate //
[1,4.34]	prayogayuktasādṛśyaṃ sambandho vāpyamukhyataḥ / vṛttiheturiti jñeyaḥ pūrvāyoge paragrahaḥ //
[1,4.35]	etameva tathā santaṃ śatarcītyādināmabhiḥ / ācakṣata iti hyatra santamityavadhāraṇā //
[1,4.36]	yogasya rūḍheḥ prābalyaṃ vidvadrūḍhiṃ ca tatragām / bahuśo darśayatyañjastātparyāt saniruktikam //
[1,4.37]	a iti brahma kathitaṃ tadvayākhyānānmatā tathā / śabdānāmapi sarveṣāṃ nāmavitkṛtakṛtyatā //
[1,4.38]	viṣṇunāmārtharūpatvaṃ saṃhitāderathābravīt / ṇakāraṃ ca ṣakāraṃ ca balaceṣṭātmakaṃ vadan //
[1,4.39]	tajjñānapūrvakatvena saṃhitādhyayanaṃ tathā / upasargatvato vestu tācchīlyārthādunastathā //
[1,4.40]	ṇakāraśca ṣakāraśca nāmarūpatayā matau / tasmāt samanvayo viṣṇau svaravarṇapadātmanaḥ //
[1,4.41]	api vedasya kimuta vākyarūpeṇa saṅgatiḥ / ghoṣāḥ sarve 'pi vedāśca sarve vedāśca yat padam //
[1,4.42]	indraṃ mitraṃ yamindraṃ ca prathamaḥ saṅkṛtistathā / nāmadhāḥ sarvadevānāmeka ityādikā śrutiḥ //
[1,4.43]	pramāṇamuktaviṣaye tadevoktamupakramāt / iti svayaṃ bhagavatā bruvatāśeṣamanvayam //
[1,4.44]	na śabdavācyataivātra pradhanasya niṣiddhayate / sarvavedetihāseṣu purāṇeṣu ca saṅgrahāt //
[1,4.45]	sattvaṃ rajastama iti guṇāḥ prakṛtisambhavāḥ / nibadhnanti mahābāho dehe dehinamavyayam //
[1,4.46]	ityādivākyarūpeṇa yatrārtho nānya iṣyate / tejo 'bannātmakaṃ vāpi yadyupādānamiṣyate //
[1,4.47]	anādyevāparādhaḥ kaḥ pradhānamiti codite / ajāmekāmiti prāha śrutiretāṃ yadā tadā / ko doṣaḥ sarvathaivāsti pariṇāmi jaḍaṃ yadi //
[1,4.48]	asmākaṃ paramamukhyārtho bhagavāneka eva tu / mukhyamātratayā rūḍhaṃ sarvamabhyupagamyate //
[1,4.49]	sarveṣāmapi śabdānāṃ gauṇyādyaṃ tadayogataḥ / arthadvayamabhipretya pravṛtte hariruktavān //
[1,4.50]	kāryāṇāṃ kāraṇaṃ pūrvaṃ vacasāṃ vācyamuttamam / yogānāṃ paramāṃ siddhiṃ paramaṃ te padaṃ viduḥ //
[1,4.51]	iti buddhau samārohādubhayoryogarūḍhayoḥ / tyāge ca kāraṇābhāvādubhayārthatvamiṣyate //
[1,4.52]	viparītapramābhāve pūrvārohastu kāraṇam / sā bhaved yatra sa vyarthaḥ pūrvāroho bhramo yathā / ato jagadupādānaṃ pradhānaṃ vakti sā śrutiḥ //
[1,4.53]	yattat triguṇamavyaktaṃ nityaṃ sadasadātmakam / pradhānaṃ prakṛtiṃ prāhuraviśeṣaṃ viśeṣavat //
[1,4.54]	pañcabhiḥ pañcabhirbrahma caturbhirdaśabhistathā / etaccaturviṃśatikaṃ gaṇaṃ prādhānikaṃ viduḥ //
[1,4.55]	iti bhāgavate prāha vidyādhīśaḥ svayaṃ prabhuḥ / na ca prakṛtiśabdena brahmopādānamucyate //
[1,4.56]	avikāraḥ sadā śuddho nitya ātmā sadā hariḥ / sadaikarūpavijñānabala ānandarūpakaḥ //
[1,4.57]	nirvikāro 'kṣaraḥ śuddho nirātaṅko 'jaro 'maraḥ / aviśvo viśvakartājo yaḥ paraḥ so 'bhidhīyate //
[1,4.58]	nirvikāramanaupamyaṃ sadaikarasamakṣayam / brahmeti paramātmeti yaṃ vidurvaidikā janāḥ //
[1,4.59]	iti śrutipurāṇoktayā na vikārī janārdanaḥ / parādhīnaviśeṣāptiranivartyānyathābhavaḥ //
[1,4.60]	kṣīrādivad vikāraḥ syānnaiva sa syāddhareḥ kvacit / apādānatvamevāsya yadyupādānateṣyate //
[1,4.61]	aṅgīkṛtaṃ tat pitṛvannatu viśvātmanā bhavaḥ / na corṇanābhijanitṛmātṛṇāṃ ca vikāritā //
[1,4.62]	cetanatvāt tadannaṃ hi kāryarūpatayā bhavet / apādānatayā viśvakartṛtvaṃ buddhipūrvakam //
[1,4.63]	uktaṃ bhāllaviśākhāyāṃ brahmatarke ca sādaram / icchāmātrāt prabhoḥ sṛṣṭiravikārasya sarvadā //
[1,4.64]	svabhāvo 'yamanantasya rajo yenābhavajjagat / svadehādicchayā viśvaṃ bhuktapūrvaṃ janārdanaḥ //
[1,4.65]	sasarja mātāpitṛvadūrṇanābhivadeva vā / pradhānaṃ pariṇāmyeśo nirvikāraḥ svayaṃ sadā //
[1,4.66]	na cetanavikāraḥ syād yatra kvāpi hyacetanam / nācetanavikāro 'pi cetanaḥ syāt kadācana //
[1,4.67]	nacānyasyānyarūpatvaṃ vikṛtatve 'pi dṛśyate / na kṣīrādanyatā dadhnaḥ kenacid dṛśyate kvacit //
[1,4.68]	sarvajñād brahmaṇo 'nyatvaṃ jagato hyanubhūyate / abhedaḥ sattvamātreṇa syād kharvasvaṇayorapi //
[1,4.69]	bhāgena pariṇāmaśced bhāgayorbheda eva hi / yo bhāgo na vikārī syāt sa evāsmākamīśvaraḥ //
[1,4.70]	bhinnānāṃ samudāyasya nāma brahmeti ced bhavet / brahmopādānatā na syāt tadā viśvasya hi kvacit //
[1,4.71]	śṛṅgāccharo 'vilomabhyo dūrvā gomayatastathā / vṛścikaścetyevamādyeṣvapādānatvamiṣyate //
[1,4.72]	upādānaikadeśatvaṃ yadyapyatra pradṛśyate / apyapādānataivātra dṛṣṭānto brahmaṇo bhavet //
[1,4.73]	na hy upādānataivātra bāhyāvayavagauravāt / na cācetanatas tatra cetanasya samudbhavaḥ //
[1,4.74]	upādānatayā kintarhyapādānaṃ hyacetanam / kāryadehagatasyāsya cetanasya pradṛśyate //
[1,4.75]	sacca tyaccābhavaditi nāsya viśvatvamucyate / tat sṛṣṭveti giraivāsya pūrvaṃ viśvasya siddhitaḥ //
[1,4.76]	sattvāt tatervaidikatvāt samyag vaktumaśakyataḥ / āśrayatvāt svāśrayatvājjñānatvād durvidatvataḥ //
[1,4.77]	sattateryātanāccaiva hyaprāptatvācca durjanaiḥ / nityāsādhuguṇavyāptiyantṛrūpatvataḥ sadā / jagadgatena rūpeṇa brahmaiva hi tathocyate //
[1,4.78]	vyaktiruktaguṇānāṃ hi puruṣāpekṣayā nṛṇām / bhavedabhavadityādyaḥ prayogaścātra yujyate //
[1,4.79]	tasmādaśeṣakartaiko nirvikāro ramāpatiḥ / śabdaiḥ prakṛtirityādyaiḥ strīliṅgairabhidhīyate //
[1,4.80]	bahu syāmiti tasyaiva hyuktamārgeṇa yujyate / tattadgatena rūpeṇa tadarthaṃ hyasṛjajjagat //
[1,4.81]	yaccāvikṛtamevaitad brahma viśvātmanā mṛṣā / dṛśyate mandadṛṣṭayaiva sa sarga iti kathyate //
[1,4.82]	sā mandadṛṣṭistasyaiva brahmaṇaḥ kiṃ tato 'nyagā / brahmaṇaścet kva sārvajñyamanyagā cet svato 'nyatā //
[1,4.83]	nādehayogino dṛṣṭiriti tat kāraṇaṃ svataḥ / dehinaḥ kāraṇayutā dehāśca yadi na bhramāt //
[1,4.84]	kiṃ bhrāntikalpitaṃ tatra bhedo 'pi bhramajo yadi / bhrānterajñānamūlatvāt tasya bhedavyapekṣayā //
[1,4.85]	nājñānakalpakaṃ kiñcidanyonyāśrayatā yataḥ / bhramatve tviyamuktiśca tadantaḥpatanānnahi //
[1,4.86]	vyāvahārikatā cāsya syādabādhyatva eva hi / bādhyaṃ nārthakriyākāri na ca svapno 'pi no mṛṣā //
[1,4.87]	vāsanājanitatvena tasyāpyaṅgīkṛtatvataḥ / sa hi karteti vākyācca jāgrattvamiti hi bhramaḥ //
[1,4.88]	sarpabhramādāvapi hi jñānamastyeva tādṛśam / tadevārthakriyākāri tat sadevārthakārakam //
[1,4.89]	brahma tvarthakriyākāri parataḥ svata eva vā / aṅgīkṛtaṃ hi tenaiva paratastve na ca pramā //
[1,4.90]	amukhyasatyamānasya sādhakatve sadā'vayoḥ / na hi sampratipattiḥ syādatastiṣṭhatu sā pramā //
[1,4.91]	na hi vipratipannena śakyaṃ sādhayituṃ kvacit / sādhakatvaṃ tu satyasya sākṣiṇo hyāvayordvayoḥ / samyak sampratipannaṃ tanna vivatarmamataṃ bhavet //
[1,4.92]	yadi nāṅgīkṛtaṃ kiñcidanaṅgīkṛtatāpi hi / nāṅgīkṛteti mūkaḥ syāditi nāsmadvivāditā //
[1,4.93]	viśvaṃ satyaṃ yacciketa praghānvasya yathārthataḥ / ityādiśrutayaḥ sarvā viśvasatyatvavācakāḥ //
[1,4.94]	satyatvaṃ gaganādeśca sākṣipratyakṣasādhitam / sākṣisiddhasya na kvāpi bādhyatvaṃ tadadoṣataḥ //
[1,4.95]	savarkāleṣvabādhyatvaṃ sākṣiṇaiva pratīyate / kālo hi sākṣipratyakṣaḥ suṣuptau ca pratītitaḥ //
[1,4.96]	atītānāgatau kālāvapi nāsākṣigocarau / pakṣīkartumaśakyatvānnānumā tatra vartate //
[1,4.97]	tadetaditi sarvaṃ ca dṛśyaṃ vā smṛtigocaram / sākṣisiddhena kālena khacitaṃ hyeva vartate //
[1,4.98]	tasmānna taṃ vinā kiñcit smartuṃ draṣṭumathāpi vā / śakyaṃ tannityasiddherhi nānumāvasaro bhavet //
[1,4.99]	ato 'doṣapratītasya satyatvaṃ sākṣiṇā matam / parīkṣādeśca satyatvaṃ tena hyeva mataṃ bhavet //
[1,4.100]	anyathā śrutiyuktayādipramāṇaiśca sahaiva tu / akasmād vinivṛttiśca kiṃ viśvasya na śaṅkayate //
[1,4.101]	itaḥ pūrvaṃ tathābhāvād yadi no saṃsṛtergatiḥ / vākyānumāditaścet syāt tatprāmāṇyaṃ ca sākṣitaḥ //
[1,4.102]	tatprāmāṇyaṃ yathā sākṣī sthāpayatyevameva hi / sarvakāleṣvapi sthairyād vyabhicāramapohya ca //
[1,4.103]	evamakṣajamānatvasiddhāṃ viśvasya satyatām / kimiti sthāpayennāyaṃ nirdoṣajñānaśaktitaḥ //
[1,4.104]	ekajñānakṛtaṃ viśvamiti yaccoṣyate mṛṣā / bahujñānakṛtaṃ viśvamiti tasyottaraṃ bhavet //
[1,4.105]	parasya satyatāṃ jānannapi yaḥ svātmataskaraḥ / paro nāstīti vadati kimityunmattavad vadet //
[1,4.106]	parābhāve hi vāg vyarthā yadi naivocyate tadā / kaśāvetrādikaṃ tasya taskarasyottaraṃ vadet //
[1,4.107]	prapañco yadi vidyeta nivarteta na saṃśayaḥ / māyāmātramidaṃ dvaitamadvaitaṃ paramārthataḥ //
[1,4.108]	vikalpo vinivarteta kalpito yadi kenacit / upadeśādayaṃ vādo 'jñāte dvaitaṃ na vidyate //
[1,4.109]	ityatra yadiśabdau ca nivarteteti ca dvayam / viśvasya satyatāmāhurvidyetotpattimeva ca //
[1,4.110]	vidotpattāviti hyasmād dhātorutpattireva hi / nivṛttivyāptiyuk prāyaḥ prapañco bhedapañcakaḥ //
[1,4.111]	jīveśvarabhidā caiva jaḍeśvarabhidā tathā / jīvabhedo mithaścaiva jaḍajīvabhidā tathā / mithaśca jaḍabhedo yaḥ prapañco bhedapañcakaḥ //
[1,4.112]	so 'yaṃ satyo hyanādiśca sādiścennāśamāpnuyāt / dvaitaṃ na vidyata iti tasmādajñānināṃ matam //
[1,4.113]	iti śrutermitaṃ trātaṃ māyākhyaharividyayā / uttamo 'rtho haristvekastadanyanmadhyamādhyamam //
[1,4.114]	vācārabdhaṃ tu sāṅketyaṃ nāma syād vikṛtaṃ bahu / nityaṃ tu nāmadheyaṃ yanmṛttiketyādi vaidikam //
[1,4.115]	prādhānyāt tatparijñānāt prākṛtājño 'pi pūruṣaḥ / vidvānityucyate sadbhirevaṃ nityaparātmavit //
[1,4.116]	sadātanaṃ satyamiti nityamevocyate budhaiḥ / prayogaścottaratrāsti jarā yadyenamāpnuyāt //
[1,4.117]	dehaḥ pradhvaṃsate vāyaṃ kiṃ tato 'syātiśiṣyate / hanyate na vadhenāyaṃ jarayā ca na jīryati //
[1,4.118]	etat satyaṃ brahmapuramiti nityatva eva hi / vācārambhaṇamityukte mithyetyaśrutakalpanam //
[1,4.119]	punaruktirnāmadheyamitītyasya nirarthatā / ekaḥ piṇḍo maṇiśceti padavaiyathyarmeva ca //
[1,4.120]	vikāratvavivakṣāyāṃ nacaikanakhakṛntanam / sarvakārṣṇāyasaṃ ca syādataḥ sādṛśya eva ca //
[1,4.121]	vivakṣātra tu nityatve prādhānye coktavartmanā / prādhānyapratipattyarthaṃ sṛṣṭayādeścaiva vistaraḥ //
[1,4.122]	tasmāt kenāpi mārgeṇa na vivartamataṃ bhavet / tadasaṅkhayātadoṣetaṃ heyameva śubhārthibhiḥ //
[1,4.123]	asaṅkhayatvena doṣāṇāṃ granthādhikyabhayādapi / uparamyate tato viṣṇuricchāpūrvakamaśramaḥ / karoti pitṛvad viśvaṃ pūrṇaśeṣaguṇātmakaḥ //
{2,1}
[2,1.1]	|| iti śrīmadānandatīrthabhagavatpādācāryaviracite śrīmadbrahmasūtrānuvyākhyāne prathamo 'dhyāyaḥ || uktaḥ samanvayaḥ sākṣādavirodho 'tra sādhyate / caturvidhasya tasyādau yauktastatrāpi ca smṛteḥ //
[2,1.2]	tasyāścatuḥsvarūpatvāt pratyekaṃ caturātmakāḥ / pādāḥ sarve tadaṃśāśca mūrtīnāṃ varṇamā'gamāt //
[2,1.3]	āptatā samatādṛṣṭiśrutisāmyabalādbhavāḥ / sarvānusāro laghutā viśeṣādarśanāphale //
[2,1.4]	iṣṭasiddhiśca niyamaḥ pūrvapakṣeṣu yuktayaḥ / etā eva tvatibalā siddhāntasya niyāmakāḥ //
[2,1.5]	āptaiḥ pratyakṣato dṛṣṭvā proktamarthaṃ kathaṃ śratiḥ / pipīlikālipinibhā vārayeta sarvagā hi te //
[2,1.6]	iti ced yadyaśeṣajñā rudrādyā haripūrvakāḥ / kiṃ nāśeṣavido mānaṃ hy ubhayatra samaṃ bhavet //
[2,1.7]	nacāptiniścayastatra śakyate vyabhicārataḥ / nacāsyā vyabhicāre 'pi hīyate mānatā kvacit //
[2,1.8]	vedoktasyādhikārasya durnirūpatvataḥ sadā / niyamo vyabhicāro vā naiva jñātuṃ hi śakyate //
[2,1.9]	adhikāro hi sulabhaḥ kathito 'nyāgameṣvalam / vedokto hy adhikārastu durlabhaḥ sarvamānuṣaiḥ //
[2,1.10]	anyāgameṣu vipratvamapi caṇḍālajanmanām / maṇḍalāntaḥpraveśena kramaśaḥ pratipādyate //
[2,1.11]	adhikāraṃ durāpādyamuktavātisulabhaṃ punaḥ / aśakyaṃ sādhanaṃ coktavā suśakaṃ tatphalāptaye / ucyate 'tastaduktaṃ hi vyabhicāri phale 'pi tu //
[2,1.12]	kathaṃ pramāṇatāṃ gacchennityatvāt puruṣodbhavaiḥ / ujkhitaṃ sarvadoṣaiśca kathaṃ no mānatāṃ vrajet //
[2,1.13]	virūpa nityayā vācā nityayānityayā sadā / ityādiśrutibhirvedo nitya ityavagamyate //
[2,1.14]	pipīlikālipiścāpi pramāṇamavirodhataḥ / yathā drauṇerulūkena kṛtamapyāsa bodhakam //
[2,1.15]	aviruddhaṃ viruddhaṃ tu virodhādeva bādhitam / virodhādarśanāt tasmād vedaprāmāṇyamiṣyate //
[2,1.16]	tanmūlatvāt smṛtīnāṃ ca virodho yatra na kvacit / virodho 'pi sa evoktaḥ pratyakṣeṇāgamena vā //
[2,1.17]	āgamenāgamasyaiva virodhe yuktiriṣyate / upajīvyavirodhe tu vedasyānyārthakalpanā //
[2,1.18]	pratyakṣamupajīvyaṃ syāt prāyo yuktirapi kvacit / āgamaikapramāṇeṣu tasyaiva hyupajīvyatā //
[2,1.19]	yukto 'yuktaśca yadyartha āgamasya pratīyate / syāt tatra yukta evārtho yuktiśca trividhā matā //
[2,1.20]	vyāptiḥ pratyakṣatā yasyā yuktigā'gamagā tathā / pratyakṣāgamamūlā tu yuktistatra balīyasī //
[2,1.21]	yāthārthyameva mānatvaṃ tanmukhyaṃ jñānaśabdayoḥ / arthatvamaryataiva syānna kriyārtheṣu sā matā //
[2,1.22]	jñānārthe jñeyatā mukhyā śabdārthe tadanantaram / yathārthajñānajanakā yathārthā yuktayaḥ smṛtāḥ //
[2,1.23]	anupramāṇametāni hyakṣayuktivacāṃsyataḥ / prāmāṇyaṃ nānuvādasya smṛterapi vihīyate //
[2,1.24]	yāthārthyameva prāmāṇyaśabdārtho yad vivakṣitaḥ / aṅgīkṛtaṃ cet prāmāṇyaṃ smṛtyādeḥ kā virodhatā //
[2,1.25]	nacāphalatvaṃ vaktavyaṃ sarvasmṛtyanuvādayoḥ / phalavattvaṃ nacāsmābhiḥ prāmāṇyaṃ hi vivakṣitam //
[2,1.26]	tṛṇādidarśane kiṃ ca phalavattvaṃ nigadyate / sukhaduḥkhādikaṃ kiñcit smṛtāvapi hi dṛśyate //
[2,1.27]	na paricchedakāryeva pramāṇamiti ca pramā / nirdoṣākṣodbhavaṃ hyatra pratyakṣamiti gīyate //
[2,1.28]	prākṛtaṃ śuddhacaitanyamakṣaṃ tu dvividhaṃ matam / śuddhamīśaramāmukteṣvanyatra prākṛtairyutam //
[2,1.29]	nirdoṣameva caitanyamanyatrobhayamiṣyate / sukhaduḥkhādiviṣayaṃ śuddhaṃ saṃsārageṣvapi //
[2,1.30]	nirdoṣatvātiniyamāt tad baliṣṭhatamaṃ matam / pañcendriyamanobhedāt prākṛtaṃ ṣaḍvidhaṃ smṛtam //
[2,1.31]	anumā yuktirevoktā vyāptireva tu sā smṛtā / pratijñātārthasiddhayarthaṃ vyāptireva yadoditā //
[2,1.32]	avaśiṣṭaṃ kimatrāsti liṅgaṃ tatra vijānataḥ / yadi liṅgamasiddhaṃ syāt kuta evāsya mānatā //
[2,1.33]	yadi smārakamātraṃ syāt smarturnātra prayojanam / na pañcāvayoktau ca vivādāvasitirbhavet //
[2,1.34]	dṛṣṭāntādiṣu caivaṃ syāt sādhanaṃ punareva hi / liṅgoktāvapi caivaṃ syādanumāvasitirdhruvā //
[2,1.35]	virodho 'saṅgatiścaiva sākṣād yuktestu dūṣaṇam / pratijñāyāmasambandho yukteruktā hyasaṅgatiḥ //
[2,1.36]	virodho 'pi tridhaiva syāt pratijñārthaviruddhatā / liṅgarāhityamavyāptirnyūnādhikye tu vācike //
[2,1.37]	sādhyavyāpakavailomyamavyāptiḥ sādhanasya ca / durbalena virodhe 'pi na pramāṇamasādhakam //
[2,1.38]	svavākyena virodhe 'pi naiva sādhakatāṃ vrajet / saṃvādānuktisaṃyuktā eta eva ca nigrahāḥ //
[2,1.39]	vādo jalpo vitaṇḍeti kathāstisro vijānatām / svārthaṃ parārthamapi vā tattvanirṇayasādhanī //
[2,1.40]	kevalaṃ tu kathā vādo jalpo 'rthādivyapekṣayā / satāmeva kathā jñeyā vitaṇḍā tvasatāṃ satām //
[2,1.41]	aprakāśya svasiddhāntamasatāṃ pakṣadūṣaṇam / ukte taiḥ prathamaṃ māne vaktavyaṃ tasya dūṣaṇam //
[2,1.42]	vidyāparīkṣāpūrvaiva vitaṇḍā jalpa eva ca / uccanīcatvanirṇītiryato jayaparājayau //
[2,1.43]	vinaiva tattvanirṇītiṃ na hi jalpādinā kvacit / uccanīcatvavijñānamiti vidyāparīkṣaṇam //
[2,1.44]	vādena coccanīcatvavijñānaṃ bhavati sphuṭam / iti vādasya pūrvatvaṃ tatsiddhau vyarthatānyayoḥ //
[2,1.45]	bahuvidyatvasiddhau tu naiva vādo 'pi kāraṇam / sabhāsabhāpaprāśnīkapūrvastu spardhināmapi //
[2,1.46]	vāda evobhayārthaḥ syānnirṇītijayakārakaḥ / tattvāprakāśa evaiko vitaṇḍājalpayoḥ phalam //
[2,1.47]	vinā vādena vidyāyā yadi śakyaṃ parīkṣaṇam / syājjalpādirapi kvāpi vāda evānyathā bhavet //
[2,1.48]	jalpa ityapi nāma syād vādasyaitādṛśasya tu / pratijñāmātrasādhyatvamapi syād yājñavalkyavat //
[2,1.49]	sabhā sabhāpatiścaiva prāśnikāścaiva vaiṣṇavāḥ / rāgadveṣavihīnāśca syuḥ sabhyāḥ sarvavedinaḥ //
[2,1.50]	prāśnikāścaitadajñāne sabhyāścaiṣāṃ ca dūragāḥ / pramāṇaṃ nirṇayāya syuḥ pakṣapātavivarjitāḥ //
[2,1.51]	ubhābhyāṃ sādhanaṃ caiva dūṣaṇaṃ vādajalpayoḥ / sadbhirāgama evaikaḥ prayojyo 'bhīṣyasādhakaḥ //
[2,1.52]	svasiddhāntānusāreṇa hyasadbhiranumocyate / pratyakṣāgamavairūpyamāśrityānyārthataiva tu //
[2,1.53]	āgame daśarnīyātra doṣo liṅgavilomatā / liṅgānukūlyaṃ svārthasya śrutyādīnāmanugrahaḥ //
[2,1.54]	tripañcāvayavāmeva yugmāvayavinīmapi / niyamād yo 'numāṃ brūyād taṃ brūyād yadi tādṛśī / nānumeti tadā kena sādhyāvayavakalpanā //
[2,1.57]	niyatāvayavāsiddhau vyāptimātreṇa sādhanam / kartavyameva tena syāt tasmāt saivānumā matā //
[2,1.58]	anubhūtiḥ pramāṇaṃ cet kena smṛtirapodyate / pūrvānubhūte kiṃ mānamityukte syāt kimuttaram //
[2,1.59]	mānasaṃ taddhi vijñānaṃ tacca sākṣipramāṇakam / atītānāgataṃ yadvad yogibhirdṛśyate 'ñjasā / evaṃ pūrvānubhūtaṃ ca manasaivāvagamyate //
[2,1.60]	vijñātaṃ manasā pūrvaṃ mayaitat kṛtamityapi / sākṣādanubhavāt siddhaṃ kathameva hyapodyate //
[2,1.61]	evaṃ lakṣaṇake mānatraye brahmādivastuṣu / pramāṇaṃ veda evaikas tatprāmāṇyaṃ ca sādhitam //
[2,1.62]	tathāpi mṛjjalādīnāṃ buddhivāgādivācakaḥ / dṛṣṭavyāptiviruddhatvāt tatra mānaṃ kathaṃ bhavet //
[2,1.63]	tatastannāmakaḥ kaścit pumānanyo bhavediti / yuktayāgamāvirodhena prāptamatrābhidhīyate //
[2,1.64]	bālarūḍhiṃ vinaivāpi vidvadrūḍhisamāśrayāt / tattannāmāna evaite tattadvastvabhimāninaḥ //
[2,1.65]	santi teṣāṃ viśeṣeṇa śaktiranyebhya ucyate / vyāptiścoktānusāreṇa dṛśyante cādhikāribhiḥ //
[2,1.66]	śāstroktavastunaścaiva vyutpattiḥ śāstraliṅgataḥ / vyutpattiḥ sā balavatī mūrkhavyutpattitā hi yat //
[2,1.67]	dṛḍhayuktivirodhe tu sarvatra nyāya īdṛśaḥ / alpavākyayutā yuktirbahulaiva virodhinī //
[2,1.68]	yatra tatra kathaṃ vastunirṇayaḥ syāditīrite / virodhiyuktibāhulyāditi nyāyo viniścitaḥ //
[2,1.69]	yuktestu yuktibāhulyamāgamādāgamasya ca / kathaṃ na nirṇayaṃ kuryādityasat kāraṇaṃ na hi //
[2,1.70]	śrutyartho bhavati kvāpi śrutiprāyopapattibhiḥ / avirodhaścaturthe tu pāte samyak samarthyate //
[2,1.71]	asat kāryaṃ yathā dṛṣṭaṃ vastutvāt kāraṇaṃ tathā / iti cenna niṣedhaikasvarūpasya na kartṛtā //
[2,1.72]	buddhipūrvapravṛttirhi kartṛtvamiha niścitam / pratiṣedhātmakatvaṃ tu bhāvasyābhāvadharmataḥ / dharmadharmaikyataścaiva natu tanmātratā bhavet //
[2,1.73]	abhāvasya ca bhāvo 'pi dharmo 'thāpi hi dharmiṇaḥ / tādṛktavaṃ mātratehoktā buddhirāhityameva tat //
[2,1.74]	viśeṣyataiva dharmitvaṃ prathamapratipattiṣu / niṣedhavidhirūpatvaṃ bhāvābhāvatvamatra hi //
[2,1.75]	sarvanāśeṣvapi sadā śiṣṭatvād yasya kasya nuḥ / nāśo 'yaṃ vimato 'pi syānnāśatvāt kartṛśeṣavān //
[2,1.76]	nacāśeṣanṛnāśastu dṛṣṭo dṛśyo 'sti vā kvacit / dharmādharmāśrayatvena svīkāryo 'pi naro laye //
[2,1.77]	anāditvaṃ vinādṛṣṭaṃ kathaṃ syāt kāraṇaṃ kvacit / pūrvādṛṣṭāt parādṛṣṭaṃ yadi naivottaraṃ kutaḥ //
[2,1.78]	adṛṣṭaṃ kāraṇaṃ no cellaye mānaṃ ca kiṃ bhavet / utpattināśakārī hi buddhimān dṛśyate kvacit //
[2,1.79]	taddṛṣṭāntena sarvatra kartā kiṃ nānumīyate / āgamānugṛhītā tu mānameṣānumāpitu //
[2,1.80]	āgamānugrahābhāve na tarkaḥ syāt pratiṣṭhitaḥ / akṣajāgamamūlasya syādevāsya pratiṣṭhitiḥ / anyathāsyāpratiṣṭhā ca svavācā vyāhataiva hi //
[2,1.81]	na ca śiṣyāgṛhītatvaṃ nirīśādīśavādinaḥ / ato 'vaśiṣṭajīvādikartṛtātra niṣiddhayate //
[2,1.82]	tanmano 'kurutetyāderasato manaso janiḥ / nivāritā tu pūrvatra hyakasmāditi tadvinā //
[2,1.83]	asato viśvajananamāśaṅkayātra niṣiddhayate / prāpakaṃ vākyamātraṃ tu parihāro viśeṣitaḥ //
[2,1.84]	kvacijjīvākṛtaṃ dṛṣṭvā cetanādeva cākṛtam / tadvadevānumānyatra vastutvāt kriyate śruteḥ //
[2,1.85]	nānyadanyatvamāpannaṃ kvacid dṛṣṭaṃ kathañcana / ato jīvasya na brahmabhāvaḥ syāddhi kadācana //
[2,1.86]	kvacid bhinnatayā dṛṣṭaṃ tadabhinnatayā katham / dṛśyenno dṛṣṭapūrvaṃ hi tādṛśaṃ na ca dṛśyate //
[2,1.87]	bhoktṛtvāpattita iti yanmataṃ tat kuto hariḥ / bhoktrāpatteriti prāha kathaṃ ca tadananyatā //
[2,1.88]	jagatastvavikāratva uktanyāyena sādhite / svatantrakāraṇānyatvaṃ tena hyatra niṣiddhayate //
[2,1.89]	dravyaṃ karma ca kālaśca svabhāvaścetanā dhṛtiḥ / yatprasādādime santi na santi yadupekṣayā / iti śrutestadvaśasya bhāvo na para ityataḥ //
[2,1.90]	śakto 'pi hyanyathākartuṃ svecchāniyamato hariḥ / kāraṇairniyataireva karotīdaṃ jagat sadā //
[2,1.91]	nityabhedo nimittena hyupādānena tu dvayam / asad yat kāryarūpeṇa kāraṇātmatayāsti hi //
[2,1.92]	anavasthānyathā hi syāt sarvatrotpattināśayoḥ / śakto 'pi bhagavān viṣṇurakartuṃ kartumanyathā //
[2,1.93]	svabhinnaṃ kāraṇābhinnabhinnaṃ viśvaṃ karotyajaḥ / iti śruteravasita uktārtho 'yamaśeṣataḥ //
[2,1.94]	anaṃśasyāpi jīvasya kiñcit sāmarthyayojanām / kāryeṣu yaḥ karotyaddhā namastasmai svayambhuve //
[2,1.95]	yadi bhāgena kāryeṣu jīvaśaktiṃ na yojayet / haristadā hi sarvatra kṛtsnayatnoṃ'śitāpi vā //
[2,1.96]	aṃśino hi paṭādyā ye bhinnaireva parasparam / aṃśairaṃśina ucyante naivameva hi cetanāḥ //
[2,1.97]	ato 'naṃśina ityeva śrutireteṣu vartate / apyanekasvarūpeṣu viśeṣādeva kevalam //
[2,1.98]	bahusvarūpatākhyā tu teṣvastyeva hi sāṃśatā / bahutvenāvinābhāvād bhinnatā niyamād bhavet //
[2,1.99]	yadi naivaṃ niyamakṛd bhagavān puruṣottamaḥ / tasya tvaśeṣaśaktitvād yujyate savarmeva ca //
[2,1.100]	virodhaḥ sarvavaiśiṣṭaye yo dvitīye nirasyate / nārāyaṇasya tvadhyāye tadanye tatratatragāḥ //
[2,1.101]	sṛṣṭisaṃhāravākyānāṃ jīvarūpābhidhāyinām / apyanyonyāvirodhastu dvitīyādhyāyagocaraḥ //
[2,1.102]	mānameyaviśeṣeṇa punaruktirna jāyate / sadā pravṛttirīśasya svabhāvādeva kevalam //
[2,1.103]	aṅgaceṣyā yathā puṃsaḥ kāściduddeśavarjitāḥ / devasyaiṣa svabhāvo 'yamityāha śrutirañjasā //
[2,1.104]	krīḍāṃ prayojanaṃ kṛtvā sṛṣṭiḥ śrutivirodhinī / iti kevalalīlaiva nirṇītā prabhuṇā svayam //
[2,1.105]	ātmaprayojanārthāya spṛhāṃ śrutiravārayat / na prayojanavattvenetyata āha jagadguruḥ //
[2,1.106]	icchāmātraṃ prabhoḥ sṛṣṭiriti sṛṣṭau viniścitāḥ / iti praśaṃsayā kāmaśrutibhyaścaiva yuktitaḥ / mahātātparyayukteśca necchāmātraṃ niṣiddhayate //
[2,1.107]	mokṣārthāḥ śrutayo yasmāt sa ca tasya prasādataḥ / unninīṣativākyācca lokadṛṣṭānusārataḥ //
[2,1.108]	icchāṃnimittako yasmāt tadabhāve kutaḥ śrutiḥ / mahātātparyarahitā pramāṇatvaṃ gamiṣyati //
[2,1.109]	yāthārthyameva mānatvamapi vākyaṃ prayojakam / mānatvameti tatrāpi yat sampūrṇaprayojanam //
[2,1.110]	vaiṣamyaṃ caiva nairghṛṇyaṃ vedāprāmāṇyakāraṇam / nāṅgīkāryamato 'nyattu na vaiṣamyādināmakam //
[2,1.111]	yadadhīnā guṇāścaiva doṣā api hi sarvaśaḥ / guṇāstasya kathaṃ na syuḥ syurdeṣāśca kathaṃ punaḥ //
[2,1.112]	sarvadharmāpapattestad vākyairapi hi tādṛśaiḥ / nirdoṣāśeṣaguṇako nirṇīto bhagavān hariḥ //
<iti śrīmadānandatīrthabhagavatpādācāryaviracite śrībrahmasūtrānuvyākhyāne dvitīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pādaḥ ||>
{2,2}
[2,2.1]	smṛtiyuktiśrutiguṇayuktayo bahuyuktayaḥ / evaṃ caturvidhā naiva viruddhayante 'nvayaṃ prati //
[2,2.2]	iti prathamapādena nirṇīte 'pyabhiyogataḥ / darśanānāṃ pravṛttatvānmanda āśaṅkate punaḥ //
[2,2.3]	anādikālato vṛttāḥ samayā hi pravāhataḥ / nacocchedo 'sti kasyāpi samayasyetyato vibhuḥ //
[2,2.4]	bhrāntimūlatvameteṣāṃ pṛthag darśayati sphuṭam / tarkairdṛḍhatamaireva vākyaiścāgamavādinām //
[2,2.5]	daurlabhyācchuddhabuddhīnāṃ bāhulyādalpavedinām / tāmasatvācca lokasya mithyājñānaprasaktitaḥ / vidveṣāt parame tattve tattvavediṣu cāniśam //
[2,2.6]	anādivāsanāyogādasurāṇāṃ bahutvataḥ / durāgrahagṛhītatvād vartante samayāḥ sadā //
[2,2.7]	tathāpi śuddhabuddhīnāmīśānugrahayoginām / yuyuktayastamo hanyurāgamānugatāḥ sadā //
[2,2.8]	iti vidyāpatiḥ samyak samayānāṃ nirākṛtim / cakāra nijabhaktānāṃ buddhiśāṇatvasiddhaye //
[2,2.9]	cetanācetanaṃ tattvadvayameva nirīśvarāḥ / āhustat pañcapañcatvavibhāgasthamacetanam / cetanaṃ tadasaṅkhayātaṃ bhinnamanyad layaṃ bhavet //
[2,2.10]	acetanasya kartṛtvaṃ svātantryeṇa nigadyate / parasparavibhedaśca kāryāṇāmālayaṃ bhavet //
[2,2.11]	bhoktṛṇāṃ cetanasyāhuḥ kecit tāmapi nāpare / svarūpacaitanyabalāt svaprakāśācca bhogitām //
[2,2.12]	prakṛteśca svarūpasya vivekāgrahameva tu / abhogavādino bhogamāhurbhedagrahāt tayoḥ //
[2,2.13]	bhogināṃ muktiruddiṣṭā sa evābhogavādinām / īśasyāsaṅgrahādeva na yuktau tāvubhāvapi //
[2,2.14]	cetanecchānusāreṇa yadā dṛṣṭaḥ paṭodbhavaḥ / etādṛśatvamanyasya vastutvāt kena vāryate //
[2,2.15]	na ca kācit pramoktārthe śrutireva pramā hi naḥ / āptatvamuktamārgeṇa vakturnaivopapadyate //
[2,2.16]	aprāmāṇyasvatastvasya svīkārādapi māyivat / svoktākhilaniṣedhī syānna ca kiñcit prasiddhayati //
[2,2.17]	idaṃ nācetanavaśaṃ vastutvāt pratipannavat / ityeva pratiṣiddhasya kena mūlānumā bhavet //
[2,2.18]	svatantravṛttī racanā sā caivācetane kutaḥ / acetanatvaṃ svātantryamiti cātmapramāhatam //
[2,2.19]	svecchānusāritāmeva svātantryaṃ hi vido viduḥ / kuta icchācetanasya secchaṃ cet kimacetanam //
[2,2.20]	icchāmyahamiti hyeva nijānubhavarodhataḥ / acetanecchāpagatā yadi bhedāgraho 'tra ca //
[2,2.21]	kathaṃ na sa ghaṭasya syānmano ma iti bhedataḥ / manaso 'pi gṛhītatvādubhayātmakatā yataḥ //
[2,2.22]	kāmasya tu manaḥ kāmaḥ priyāpriyavibhedataḥ / dvaividhyaṃ dṛśyate cāsya tasmād bhedāgrahaḥ kutaḥ //
[2,2.23]	racanānupapattestanna sarvajñānumāgatam / acetanaṃ jagatkartṛ payo 'mbvādi ca nopamā //
[2,2.24]	etatpraśāstivacanāccetanācetanasya ca / dvaividhye 'pitu kāmādeḥ kutaḥ svāmitvamātmanaḥ //
[2,2.25]	sākṣādanubhavārūḍhaṃ śakyate 'podituṃ kvacit / icchāsvāmitvamevoktamicchāvattvaṃ nacāparam //
[2,2.26]	kiñcit tadvaśagatve 'pi svāmitvaṃ lokavad bhavet / sarvātmatantrakāmādeḥ kimutaiva pareśituḥ //
[2,2.27]	na cānubhavagaṃ kāmasvāmitvaṃ vedavāgapi / śaktāpavadituṃ tasmāt sā tadanyābhidhāyinī //
[2,2.28]	mokṣakāmo bhavedanyo yadi muktād bhaviṣyataḥ / mokṣakāmasya kiṃ tena svanāśārthaṃ ca ko yatet //
[2,2.29]	kartṛtvaṃ yasya tasyaiva bhoktṛtvamupalabhyate / vibhāge ca tayormānaṃ naiva kiñcit kvacid bhavet //
[2,2.30]	sarvamānavirodhaikadurdīkṣādīkṣitastvayam / māyāvādyupamāṃ yāyāt taccaśabdānnirākṛtaḥ //
[2,2.31]	sāṅkhayastu seśvaro brūte kṣetrānugrahaśaktimān / astīśvaraḥ svayambhātaḥ kleśakarmādivarjitaḥ //
[2,2.32]	kṣetraśaktimatī saiva prakṛtirbījaśaktimān / jīvaḥ parjanyavad daivaśaktimānīśvaraḥ smṛtaḥ //
[2,2.33]	pṛthivīvat pradhānaṃ tajjīvaḥ sannidhimātrataḥ / bījāvapanakartevetyatra prāha prabhuḥ svayam //
[2,2.34]	anyatra kāpi śaktirna svātantryeṇeśa eva hi / śaktīstāḥ prerayatyañjastadadhīnāśca sarvadā //
[2,2.35]	sattāpradhānapuruṣaśaktīnāṃ ca pratītayaḥ / pravṛttayaśca tāḥ sarvā nityaṃ nityātmanā yataḥ //
[2,2.36]	yathā nityatayā nityaṃ nityaśaktayā svayeśvaraḥ / niyāmayati nityaṃ ca na ṛte tvaditi śruteḥ //
[2,2.37]	svabhāvajīvakarmāṇi dravyaṃ kālaḥ śrutiḥ kriyāḥ / yatprasādādime santi na santi yadupekṣayā //
[2,2.38]	iti śruterna sattādyā api nārāyaṇaṃ vinā / tatpatañjalivindhyādimataṃ na puruṣārthadam //
[2,2.39]	cārvākairucyate mānamakṣajaṃ nāparaṃ kvacit / deha ātmā pumarthaśca kāmārthābhyāṃ vinā na hi //
[2,2.40]	yadevaṃ darśanenāsya ko 'rthaḥ pratyakṣagocaraḥ / labdhastenaiva hi naraiḥ śāstrāt kiṃ mohanaṃ vinā //
[2,2.41]	svaparārthavihīnatvāt svamatenaiva niṣphalam / kimityunmattavacchāstraṃ vṛthā pralapati svayam //
[2,2.42]	dehādanyo 'nubhavata ātmā bhāti śarīriṇām / mama deha iti vyaktaṃ mamārtha itivat sadā //
[2,2.43]	pratyakṣasyaiva mānatvamiti kenāvasīyate / yadi tatsādhakaṃ vedaprāmāṇye na kathaṃ bhavet //
[2,2.44]	na cānyāmānatā kvāpi pramāṇenāvasīyate / svamatenārtharahita upekṣyaḥ pakṣa īdṛśaḥ //
[2,2.45]	sannidhānāccetanasya vartate yadyacetanam / tathāpyabuddhipūrvatvāduktadoṣaḥ samo bhavet //
[2,2.46]	aṅgitvaṃ puruṣasyaiva sarvairapyanubhūyate / tadaṅgatvoktitaścaiva syāt sarvasyāpalāpakaḥ / kimu sarveśvarasyāsya hyapalāṣād yato 'khilam //
[2,2.47]	aṅgitvaṃ yadi tasyaiva svātantryaṃ cennacākhilam / tatpreraṇe 'pyaśaktatvāt svatantro 'nyo hyapekṣitaḥ //
[2,2.48]	na ca svātantryamasyaiva pratyakṣādivirodhataḥ / hitākṛtyādidoṣācca bhadraṃ nānīśvaraṃ matam //
[2,2.49]	saṃsāriṇo 'nyaṃ sarveśaṃ sarvaśaktimanaupamam / cetanācetanasyāsya sattvādestadadhīnatām / nāṅgīkurvanti ye teṣāṃ sarveṣāṃ ca samā ime //
[2,2.50]	tasmācchrutipramāṇena yuktibhiśca paro hariḥ / aṅgīkāyartamo nityaḥ sarvairapi suniścitam //
[2,2.51]	nityajñānaprayatnecchaṃ saṅkhayadyairapi pañcabhiḥ / yuktamīśaṃ vadantyanye tadicchādṛṣṭacoditāḥ / paramāṇavaścaturvargāḥ saṃyujyante dviśo 'khilāḥ //
[2,2.52]	paramāṇudvayenaiva dvayaṇukaṃ nāma jāyate / dvayaṇukatrayeṇa tṛyaṇukaṃ taiścaturbhistadātmakam //
[2,2.53]	tatastvaniyamenaiva khaṇḍāvayavināṃ bhavaḥ / tataścāniyamenaiva sarvāvayavisambhavaḥ //
[2,2.54]	kāraṇaṃ samavāyyākhyaṃ paramāṇvādi tatra hi / īśecchādṛṣṭakālāstu nimittaṃ kāraṇaṃ matam //
[2,2.55]	sāmānyāntyaviśeṣau ca samavāyaśca tattrayam / nityaṃ kriyā anityāstu guṇadravye dvirūpake //
[2,2.56]	kārye guṇakriyāṇāṃ tu samavāyyanyakāraṇam / kāraṇasthā guṇādyāstu saṃyogo dravyakāraṇam //
[2,2.57]	evaṃ sthite 'pi siddhānte viśeṣastatra kalpitaḥ / dvayaṇuke paramāṇau ca hrasvatvaṃ parimaṇḍalam //
[2,2.58]	na kāraṇaṃ kāryaguṇe vairūpyaṃ tatra kāraṇam / ityāhustānathovāca vidyādhīśaḥ svayaṃ prabhuḥ //
[2,2.59]	mahattvaṃ caiva dīrghatvaṃ tṛyaṇukādyeṣu kalpitam / tasmācca sadṛśaṃ kāryaṃ tatkāryeṣūpajāyate //
[2,2.60]	yathā tathaiva hrasvatvāt pārimāṇḍalyato 'pi hi / jāyeta sadṛśaṃ kārye parimāṇaṃ samatvataḥ //
[2,2.61]	na cenmahattvataścaiva dīghartvādapi no bhavet / sadṛśasya hi kāryasya naiva yogaḥ kathañcana //
[2,2.62]	apratyakṣatvamevaṃ syād yataḥ kāryeṣvaṇutvataḥ / iti cenna mahattvaṃ ca paramāṇāvaṇāvapi / kathaṃ tṛyaṇukapūrveṣu nāṇutvamapi kathyate //
[2,2.63]	pratyakṣatvatadanyatve puruṣāpekṣayākhile / aṇutvaṃ ca mahattvaṃ ca yato vastuvyapekṣayā //
[2,2.64]	tāratamyasthitā yasmāt padārthāḥ sarva eva ca / yathā mahattvaviśrāntistathāṇutvasya ceṣyate //
[2,2.65]	parimāṇatvataścenna mahattvasyāpi viśramaḥ / dṛśyate 'nanta ityeva tathānantyamaṇāvapi //
[2,2.66]	na mahattatvaguṇata etāvāniti hīśvaraḥ / paricchinnastathāṇośca naitāvadbhāgatā kvacit //
[2,2.67]	viśrānto yadyanantāṃśaḥ kaścidastīti gamyate / nāvasāyayituṃ śakyo virodhādeva kevalam //
[2,2.68]	kevalaṃ sākṣimānena kālo deśo 'pi nāntavān / aparyavasitiścāṇordṛśyate sakṣiṇā dvayoḥ //
[2,2.69]	yadi no sākṣigamyaṃ tanmahattvaṃ kena gamyate / viśrāntistāratamyena dṛśyate hyanumānataḥ //
[2,2.70]	yadyāgamādanantaṃ tanmahattvamavagamyate / anantameva cāṇutvaṃ kuto naivāvasīyate //
[2,2.71]	mahattvāṇutvayornaiva viśrāntirupalabhyate / anyadeva hyanantatvaṃ mahattvāṇutvayoḥ samam //
[2,2.72]	bahutvālpatvayoryadvat sāṅkhayāyāmupalabhyate / ānantyamekabhāgānāṃ tāvattvaṃ hyeva gaṇyate //
[2,2.73]	aṇīyāṃśca mahīyāṃśca bhagavānāgamoditaḥ / ānantyavācakaḥ śabdo dvidhānantye 'pi mānatām //
[2,2.74]	yāti naiva guṇālpatvaṃ kālātpatvaṃ ca mānagam / sarvakālagatasyālpakāle 'pi syādavasthitiḥ //
[2,2.75]	mahāguṇasya cālpo 'pi guṇaḥ syāditi ced bhavet / tāvattvameva naiva syād deśe 'pyetanna no matam //
[2,2.76]	mahato 'lpatvamapi hi vyomavat prāha vedavit / yadyalpadeśasaṃsthānaṃ na sarvatrāpi no bhavet //
[2,2.77]	sthitasya hyalpadeśeṣu sarvagatvaṃ bhaved dhruvam / ekatrāpyanavasthasya kuta evākhilasthatā //
[2,2.78]	śūnyatvameva tasya syād yasyaikatrāpi na sthitiḥ / ato nāṇutvaviśrāntirna mahattvasya ca kvacit //
[2,2.79]	ubhayānantyayuk tasmād yadi mukhyamahad bhavet / tacca brahma paraṃ sākṣāt sarvānantyayutaṃ sadā //
[2,2.80]	yadi sākṣī svayambhāto na mānaṃ kena gamyate / akṣajādeśca mānatvamanavasthāthavā bhavet //
[2,2.81]	ataḥ sarvapadārthānāṃ bhāgāḥ santyeva sarvadā / sarvadikṣvapi sambandhādavibhāgaḥ parāṇutā //
[2,2.82]	tatsaṃyogādaniyatāt padārthānāṃ janirbhavet / dvayoreva tu saṃyoga iti kenāvasīyate //
[2,2.83]	kāraṇasya guṇāstena bhaveyuḥ kāryagā api / tāratamyena sarve 'pi mahāntaścāṇavo yataḥ //
[2,2.84]	na ca tatproktasṛṣṭau tu mānaṃ kevalakalpanā / kathaṃ sākṣimitasyāsya śaknuyād vāraṇe kvacit //
[2,2.85]	yadi sākṣimitaṃ naitannānumā tatra vartate / pakṣīkartumaśakyatvāt kuta evānumā bhavet //
[2,2.86]	yatra nāsti padanyāsaḥ kastaṃ viṣayamāpnuyāt / deśāntarādiśabdaśca śaśaśṛṅgādiśabdavat //
[2,2.87]	sadṛśaṃ ca sajātīyaṃ nāsmatpakṣe kim eva hi / yenaiva ca prakāreṇātyasiddhamanumīyate / tenaiva śaśṛṅgādeḥ śakyamastitvakalpanam //
[2,2.88]	pratyakṣamāgamo vāpi bhaved yatra niyāmakaḥ / saiva vyāptirbhavenmānaṃ nānyā sandigdhamūlataḥ //
[2,2.89]	sahadarśanamātreṇa na vyāptiravasīyate / yadaivāvyatirekasya hyakṣajaṃ vāgamo bhavet / tannirdhāritayuktirvā vyāptiḥ saivāparā na hi //
[2,2.90]	anyathā saptamarasabhavo 'pyanumayā'patet / aniṣṭāni ca sarvāṇi hyanumā kāmacāriṇī //
[2,2.91]	kāryakāraṇayoścaiva guṇādeḥ pañcakasya ca / bhinnasyaiva tu sambandhaḥ samavāyo 'nya īryate //
[2,2.92]	bhinnatvasāmyatastasya tābhyāṃ yogo bhaved dhruvam / sa svanirvāhakaścet syād dravyameva tathā na kim //
[2,2.93]	viśeṣastadgatatvādiryadyabhinne 'vasīyate / guṇakriyādirūpasya niṣedhaḥ kena hetunā //
[2,2.94]	dravyameva tato 'nantaviśeṣātmatayā sadā / nānāvyavahṛterheturanantatvaṃ viśeṣataḥ //
[2,2.95]	viśeṣaśca viśeṣī saḥ svenaiva samavāyavat / kalpanāgurutādoṣāt padārthāntaratā na hi //
[2,2.96]	kalpayitvā ṣaṭ padārthān sābhāvānapi kevalam / ekasmin sa viśeṣaścet kiṃ pūrvaṃ tasya vismṛtiḥ //
[2,2.97]	yena pratyakṣasiddhena vyavahāro 'khilo bhavet / bhāvābhāvavibhāgena yaṃ vinā na kathañcana //
[2,2.98]	abhedena pratītiśca kāryakāraṇapūrvake / abhāvānte padārthe 'smin saviśeṣāvasīyate //
[2,2.99]	sāmānyādipadārtheṣu tanniṣṭhatvādayo 'khilāḥ / kathaṃ dharmā nivāryante vastvaikye 'pi hi vādibhiḥ //
[2,2.100]	kāryasya tattanniṣṭhatvaṃ guṇādervyāpitādikaḥ / kathaṃ viśeṣo naivāsti sa ca dharmo 'paro yadi //
[2,2.101]	ṣaṭpadārthātirekaḥ syāt padārthāniyame 'pi hi / dharmasya dharmasantānādanavasthākaro bhavet //
[2,2.102]	sāmānyasyāpi sāmānyaṃ guṇasyāpi guṇo hyataḥ / nāṅgīkṛtaḥ sa ca yadi nānavasthā kvacid bhavet //
[2,2.103]	asmatpakṣe guṇādyāśca tadvanto hi viśeṣataḥ / ananyatvānnānavasthā bhedo nāśe bhavet tathā //
[2,2.104]	viśeṣameva saṃśritya viśeṣo balavān yataḥ / dṛṣṭipramāṇataścaiva virodho darśane katham //
[2,2.105]	virodho hyavirodhaśca yato darśanamānagau / tato dṛṣṭe virodhastu sadbhirāpādyate katham //
[2,2.106]	abhinno bhagavān svena tadanyena vibhedavān / nityā dharmāstadīyāstu sarve 'smānnaiva bhedinaḥ //
[2,2.107]	sāmastyocchedino 'nyatra dharmā ubhayarūpakāḥ / bhāve ta eva cocchedāt tadanye ca samastaśaḥ //
[2,2.108]	aṃśāṃśinorabhedena tvaṃśasaṃyoga eva hi / aṃśino nānavasthāto yadyapyaṃśeṣvaviśramaḥ //
[2,2.109]	ekasmin jāta evānyaḥ saṃyogo jāyate yadi / anavasthā tadaiva syāt saṃyogaikye bhavet kva sā //
[2,2.110]	aṃśe saṃyogadṛṣṭeśca dṛṣṭe kā sānavasthitiḥ / yadyaṃśago na saṃyogaḥ kāryeṣu prathimā katham //
[2,2.111]	paramāṇoraṇornāsti mahattetyadbhutaṃ vacaḥ / aṇūnāṃ prathimāpekṣāṃ vinaiva tṛyaṇuke 'pi saḥ / paramāṇormahattvaṃ ca vinetyetad vacaḥ katham //
[2,2.112]	aṃśino 'ṃśairabhedo 'yamaṃśena tu bhidābhidā / sarvapratyakṣaviṣayaḥ kathameva hyapohyate //
[2,2.113]	saṃyogaśca vibhāgaśca bhedaścaiva pṛthak pṛthak / anyonyapratiyogena hyubhayorapi dṛśyate //
[2,2.114]	bhinnā iti tu bhedānāṃ samudāyo hi dṛśyate / yathaiva ca padārthānāmanayorbheda ityapi //
[2,2.115]	ito 'muṣyāmuto 'pyasya bhedo dṛṣṭo dvidharmikaḥ / tatraikavacanaṃ yattad viprāṇāṃ bhojanaṃ yathā //
[2,2.116]	naratvādikamapyevaṃ tattaddharmatayeyate / na sarvadharma eko 'sti samudāyastu bhinnagaḥ //
[2,2.117]	etādṛśaṃ ca sādṛśyaṃ padārtheṣu pṛthak pṛthak / ekasmin sa vinaṣṭe 'pi yato 'nyatraiva dṛśyate //
[2,2.118]	kuto bhasmatvamāptasya naratvaṃ punariṣyate / ekatve nāsti mānaṃ ca śrutirapyāha sādaram //
[2,2.119]	bhinnāśca bhinnadharmāśca padārthā akhilā api / svaiḥ svairdharmairabhinnāśca svarūpairapi sarvaśaḥ //
[2,2.120]	anivṛttavināśāstu dharmā ubhayarūpakāḥ / na kenacidabhinno 'to bhagavān svaguṇairvinā //
[2,2.121]	iti vyutpattirapi hi sādṛśyenaiva gamyate / sarveṣu yugapacchabdaḥ sadṛśeṣu pravartate //
[2,2.122]	tathāpi prāptitastvekavacanācca viśeṣataḥ / abhīṣyāvagatiśca syācchaktiḥ sādṛśyagā yataḥ //
[2,2.123]	tādṛśo 'yaṃ ca tacchabda iti jñāpayati sphuṭam / jātitaścet kathaṃ tāsu tatra cedanavasthitiḥ //
[2,2.124]	tathaiva vyaktivijñānaṃ vyaktitvābhāvadūṣitam / yadi taccāsti tasyāpi viśeṣeṣvanavasthitiḥ //
[2,2.125]	kathaṃ svarūpatvamapi jñāyate 'nugataṃ yadi / ekavyutpattiparyantamanavasthādidūṣitam / kalpanāgauravāt tena yuktā nānugakalpanā //
[2,2.126]	aupādhikaviśiṣṭādyamapi tadvastu kiṃ tataḥ / anyat tadeva cedagnimattvaṃ kiṃ tatra bhaṇyate //
[2,2.127]	agnisaṃyogamātraṃ ced bhavet tat siddhasādhanam / bhūdharasyāgnisaṃyogo yadi ṣaṣṭhayartha eva kaḥ //
[2,2.128]	samavāyo yadi hy asya caikatvāt siddhasādhanam / yadyasyaupādhiko bhedaḥ kuta ekatvamiṣyate //
[2,2.129]	nānirvācyaṃ hi teneṣyamata aupādhikānyayoḥ / satyatvāt ko viśeṣaḥ syānmāyāvādyanyathā bhavet //
[2,2.130]	upādhijanyaṃ tadgamyamiti vaupādhikaṃ bhavet / ubhayatrāpyanantāḥ syuḥ samavāyā itastataḥ / bhinnatvaṃ caiva teṣvasti ko viśeṣa upādhige //
[2,2.131]	avidyamāna evānyaḥ samavāyo 'dhigamyate / upādhinā tadgamakamanumānaṃ na mā bhavet //
[2,2.132]	evamevāsataḥ sattasamavāyo janirmatā / tatrāpi hyuktadoṣāṇāṃ naiva kiñcinnivārakam //
[2,2.133]	asmatpakṣe viśeṣasya sarvatrāṅgīkṛtatvataḥ / nāsti doṣaḥ kvacid bhāvo hyabhāvaśca sa eva hi //
[2,2.134]	abhāvasya ca dharmāḥ syurbhāvāsteṣāṃ ca te 'khilāḥ / pratyakṣamānataḥ sarvametanno vāraṇakṣamam / sarve bhāvā abhāvāśca padārthāstena sarvadā //
[2,2.135]	tathāpi prathamaṃ buddheryo niṣedhasya gocaraḥ / so 'bhāvo vidhibuddhestu gocaraḥ prathamaṃ paraḥ //
[2,2.136]	tasmāt pradhvastabhedādi sadityevāvagamyate / astyabhāvo 'sti ca dhvaṃso dehābhāvaśca bhasmatā //
[2,2.137]	ityādi yujyate sarvaṃ pratyakṣādipramāṇataḥ / anyonyābhāvabhedau ca pṛthaktavaṃ ca pṛthak pṛthak //
[2,2.138]	yat kalpayanti taccaiva kalpanāgauravād gatam / paryāyatvena te śabdā jñāyante sarva eva hi //
[2,2.139]	bhedasya tu svarūpatve ye vadanti ca śūnyatām / adbhutatāste yato 'nyasya pratiyogitvamiṣyate //
[2,2.140]	pratiyogino hi bhedo 'yaṃ natu svasmāt kathañcana / vibhāgenālpataiva syāt kuta eva ca śūnyatā //
[2,2.141]	na śūnyānāṃ hi saṃyogād bhāvo vastuna iṣyate / vidāraṇārtho dhātuśca vibhāgaguṇavācakaḥ //
[2,2.142]	avidāraṇe 'pi hyāsyasya bhinnāvoṣṭhau tu tasya ca / ata unmattavākyatvānmāyāvādo 'bhyupekṣitaḥ //
[2,2.143]	na cāmandasadānandasyandyanantaguṇārṇavaḥ / īśvaro 'ṣṭaguṇatvena prameyo 'pramitatvataḥ //
[2,2.144]	mayyanantaguṇe 'nante guṇato 'nantavigrahe / anantaguṇamāhātmyaśaktijñānamahārṇavaḥ //
[2,2.145]	nārāyaṇaḥ paro 'śeṣacetanebhyaḥ paraṃ padam / ityādivedatadvākyairanantaiścāvasīyate //
[2,2.146]	anantaguṇatā viṣṇoḥ kathameva hyapodyate / yadyanantaviśeṣāśca tajjñānādernivāritāḥ //
[2,2.147]	kathaṃ tattadviṣayatā sārvajñyārthaṃ vidhīyate / aupādhikaviśeṣastu pūrvameva nirākṛtaḥ //
[2,2.148]	svaprakāśatvamapi tu yairjñānasya nivāritam / kathaṃ sarvajñatā tasya svajñānādhigamaṃ vinā //
[2,2.149]	jñānaṃ viśvādhigaṃ tvekaṃ tajjñānaviṣayaṃ param / iti jñānadvayenaiva sarvavit parameśvaraḥ //
[2,2.150]	iti cedeṣa evārthastajjñānāvasito yadi / svaprakāśatvameva syājjñānaṃ hyetad viśeṣaṇam //
[2,2.151]	jñānāntareṇa cedatra bhavedevānavasthitiḥ / svaprakāśatvametasmād durnivāryaṃ samāpatet //
[2,2.152]	sukhavān duḥkhavāṃśca syāditi vyāptiśca no bhavet / nirduḥkhatvaṃ mahānandaḥ śrutyaiveśasya bhaṇyate //
[2,2.153]	yo 'śanāyāpipāse ca śokādīṃścātivartate / ānandaṃ brahmaṇo vidvān vipāpmetyādikā ca sā //
[2,2.154]	īśvarasya tatheṣṭatvaṃ duḥkhitvopādhirityapi / ukte kimuttaraṃ brūyācchrutyanādaratatparaḥ //
[2,2.155]	nacātmaduḥkhitecchā syādata etannivāryate / sahadarśanamātreṇa śrutīnāmapalāpakaḥ //
[2,2.156]	yajñāder api pāpasya hetutvaṃ hiṃsayā yuteḥ / nānumāti kathaṃ tatra yadyupādhirniṣiddhatā //
[2,2.157]	aduḥkhitvena cānuktiḥ kathaṃ nopādhitāṃ vrajet / aduḥkhamitarat sarvaṃ jīvā eva tu duḥkhinaḥ / teṣāṃ duḥkhaprahāṇāya śrutireṣā pravartate //
[2,2.158]	iti śrutirhi paramā śrutyuktir yadi kāraṇam / kiṃ kāryamanumānena gaḷastanasamena hi //
[2,2.159]	anumānena yadyarthaḥ śrutidṛṣṭo vyapodyate / pūrvoktena prakāreṇa neśvaro dharma eva ca / syāt tatphalaṃ ca tenātra śrutireva pramā bhavet //
[2,2.160]	īśasyānumayā siddheḥ śrutirdhamirpramā bhavet / tayā sarvaguṇaiḥ pūrṇa ukta īśo yatastataḥ //
[2,2.161]	anānandānumā tasya dharmigrāhivirodhataḥ / na pramāṇaṃ bhavet tasmānnānumātropayoginī //
[2,2.162]	nityecchatvāt pareśasya paramāṇusadātvataḥ / adṛṣṭakālayoścaiva bhāvāt kāryaṃ sadā bhavet //
[2,2.163]	na hi kālavibhedo 'sti tatpakṣe 'smanmate hareḥ / viśeṣakāla evaitatsṛṣṭayādīcchā sadātanā //
[2,2.164]	viśeṣāścaiva kālasya harericchāvaśāḥ sadā / sarve nimeṣā iti hi śrutirevāha sādaram //
[2,2.165]	udīrayati kālākhyaśaktimityasya vāgapi / kālasya kālagatvena na virodho 'pi kaścana //
[2,2.166]	asaṅkhayātaviśeṣatvādicchāyā api sarvadā / īśo deśaś ca kālaś ca svagatā eva sarvadā //
[2,2.167]	īśādhīnau ca tau nityaṃ tadādhārau ca tadgatau / iti śrutirapi prāha kāle svoddiṣṭa eva tu //
[2,2.168]	tatkālasṛṣṭimevāto vāñchatīśaḥ sadaiva hi / syāt kālaḥ sa tadaiveti kālasya svagatatvataḥ //
[2,2.169]	svabhāvādeva hīcchaiṣā devasyaiva iti śruteḥ / svabhāvo 'pi pareśecchāvaśa ityuditaḥ purā //
[2,2.170]	nityā anityāśca tatastadadhīnā iti śrutiḥ / rūpasparśādihetubhyaḥ paramāṇoranityatā //
[2,2.171]	anumeyā śrutīnāṃ ca viruddhatvānna tanmatam / upādeyamataścāyamaviruddhaḥ samanvayaḥ //
[2,2.172]	vaibhāṣikāśca sautrāntāḥ svarasakṣaṇikaṃ jagat / aṇūnāṃ samudāyaṃ ca kālakarmanimittataḥ //
[2,2.173]	utpattikāle yuktānāmātmānaṃ ca kṣaṇasthitim / nityaṃ santānameteṣāṃ pañcaskandhātmanā sthitam //
[2,2.174]	saṃskārarūpavijñānasañjñāduḥkhātmanā sthitiḥ / duḥkhābhāvaṃ sukhaṃ cāhurarūpajñānasantatim //
[2,2.175]	mokṣaṃ sa samudāyo hi naikasmādeva yujyate / nobhayoścobhayatvaṃ yat samudāyavyapekṣayā //
[2,2.176]	ato 'nyonyāśrayatvena samudāyo na yujyate / anyonyāpekṣayā puṃsaḥ samudāyatvavedanam //
[2,2.177]	syāt tatsadātanatve 'pi tacca sāmīpyahetukam / iti cet kāryasambhūtimātravyāpṛtikāraṇam //
[2,2.178]	natu kāryaviśeṣeṣu vyāpṛtaṃ kāraṇaṃ bhavet / ato 'rthendriyasaṃyogirūpakāraṇatātmanaḥ / saṃyogirūparāhityānnaiva tajjñānatāpi hi //
[2,2.179]	viśaṣaṣakāryajanakaṃ yadi kāraṇamiṣyate / kutaḥ samānarūpatvaṃ kāryāṇāmapi sarvaśaḥ //
[2,2.180]	ato 'niyatyā yatkiñcid yasya kasyāpi kāraṇam / adṛṣṭasyāpi tasyaiva viśeṣāpādakaṃ kutaḥ //
[2,2.181]	yasya kasyāpi yatkiñcid viśeṣamupapādayet / kāryaṃ ca kāraṇaṃ caiva yatkiñcid yasya kasyacit //
[2,2.182]	bhavenniyāmakābhāvādidamasyaiva kāraṇam / iti nityavināśitve kena mānena gamyate //
[2,2.183]	idaṃ na jāyate 'muṣmādityatrāpi na kāraṇam / vināśotpattayaścaiva na dṛśyante sadātanāḥ //
[2,2.184]	dṛśyate pratyabhijñātaḥ sthiratvaṃ sarvavastuṣu / phalādīnāṃ viśeṣeṇa sarvatrāpyanumīyate //
[2,2.185]	sattvena kṣaṇikatvaṃ cedākāśasyāviśeṣataḥ / aviśeṣo 'khilasyāpi sattvāt kiṃ nānumīyate //
[2,2.186]	yadyākāśasya sattvaṃ na kuta eva narādiṣu / sadharmipratiyogitvamākāśasyāvagamyate //
[2,2.187]	tau vinā na hy abhāvaś ca kvaciddṛṣṭaḥ kadācana / adharmipratiyogitvamākāśasyāvagamyate //
[2,2.188]	svīkāratyāgato 'dṛṣṭadṛṣṭayoḥ sarvavastuṣu / guṇānunmatta evāsau vidadhātyadhikaṃ punaḥ //
[2,2.189]	uttarotpattimātreṇa vināśāt pūvarvastunaḥ / na saṃskārārpakatvaṃ ca yujyate kasyacit kvacit //
[2,2.190]	ato jñātaṃ mayetyādi na jñeyamanumā kutaḥ / ekatvamanubhūtisthaṃ tyaktavā nirmānakā bhidā / kuta ātmādikeṣu syād balyevānubhavo yataḥ //
[2,2.191]	kāryakāraṇayoścaikakālīnatvaṃ vinā katham / pūrvasaṃskārayogī syāduttaro niyamena ca //
[2,2.192]	sambaddha eva saṃskāramanyatrādattate 'khilāḥ / asambaddhaḥ kathaṃ pūrva uttare vāsanākaraḥ //
[2,2.193]	ekakālatayā yogaṃ vinā saṃskārataḥ katham / kṣaṇamātramavasthānaṃ svīkṛtaṃ sarvavastuṣu //
[2,2.194]	pūrvamadhyāparakalārahitaḥ kṣaṇa iṣyate / pūrvabhāvabhavaṃ kāryamuta tannāśasambhavam //
[2,2.195]	yaugapadyaṃ sati bhavedutpādyānāmaśeṣataḥ / vināśe cenna tatkāryaṃ kāryotpattau ca kā pramā //
[2,2.196]	abhedena viśeṣeṇa dehadīpaphalādiṣu / viśeṣadarśanaṃ yuktamasmākamanubhūtitaḥ //
[2,2.197]	viśeṣadarśanaṃ mānaṃ yadi na sthairyadṛk kutaḥ / diksukhe ca khadṛṣṭāntād bhāvau saccet kvacid bhaved //
[2,2.198]	viśvaṃ pratyakṣagaṃ tyaktavā tayoryo 'numitaṃ vadet / māyāvādivadevāsāvupekṣyo bhūtimicchatā //
[2,2.199]	sarvapramāṇasiddhaṃ yad buddherbhedena sarvadā / kathaṃ nu tasya buddhitvaṃ viśvamanyacca kimpramam //
[2,2.200]	sarvaloko bibhetyañjo yasmādanubhavāt sadā / tasyāpalāpinaḥ kiṃ na niṣpramāṇakavādinaḥ //
[2,2.201]	so 'haṃ tadidamevāhaṃ sukhī sad gaganaṃ diśaḥ / satyā ityādyanubhavāḥ sadā tatpratipakṣagāḥ //
[2,2.202]	ato nirmānamakhilapramāṇapratipakṣagam / durmataṃ ko nu gṛhṇīyād vināsuratatiṃ kvacit //
[2,2.203]	aparaḥ śūnyamakhilaṃ manovācāmagocaram / nirviśeṣaṃ svayambhātaṃ nirlepamajarāmaram //
[2,2.204]	aśeṣadoṣarahitamanantaṃ deśakālataḥ / vastutaśca tadasmīti nityopāsāparokṣitam / rāgādidoṣarahitaṃ tadbhāvaṃ yoginaṃ nayet //
[2,2.205]	tasyaivānādisaṃvṛttyā nānābhedātmakaṃ jagat / sadivābhāti satyatvaṃ sāṃvṛtaṃ tasya ceṣyate //
[2,2.206]	pāramārthikasattvaṃ tu śūnyādanyasya na kvacit / sāṃvṛtenaiva satyena vyavahāro 'khilo bhavet //
[2,2.207]	śūnyāt saṃvṛtiyogena viśvametat pravartate / sṛṣṭikāle punaścānte stimitaṃ śūnyatāṃ vrajet / iti brūte tamuddiśya jagāda jagatāṃ guruḥ //
[2,2.208]	nāsato jagato bhāvo na hi dṛṣṭāsato janiḥ / sataḥ kvacit pramāṇaṃ ca dṛṣṭirevākhilād varam //
[2,2.209]	yadyevaṃ saptamarasānmadhurādiva pīnatā / bhavejjanasya mārjārṛṅgaṃ goriva ghātakam //
[2,2.210]	kāryārthī kāraṇaṃ sacca nopādadyāt kathañcana / na pravarteta ceṣyāya śūnyādeveṣyasambhavāt //
[2,2.211]	deśakālādiniyamo niṃha śūnyāt sato bhavet / puruṣecchānusāreṇa yadi kiñcit prajāyate //
[2,2.212]	kiṃ nānumīyate tadvad vastutvāt puruṣād bhavaḥ / sarvasyāpi nacābhāvo viśvaṃ saditi gamyate //
[2,2.213]	yato 'nubhavarodhe tu vacanaṃ vādinaḥ kutaḥ / svapnabhrāntivadevedaṃ saṃvṛttyaivopalabhyate //
[2,2.214]	yadi sattvena kiñcātra bhramo naiva nivartate / anāderasya viśvasya nivṛttiryadi ceṣyate / nivṛttiśca nivarteta tasyā bhrāntitvasambhavāt //
[2,2.215]	dṛṣṭasya bhrāntitā cet syādadṛṣṭe na bhramaḥ kutaḥ / gavāmaśṛṅgibhāvena na hi syācchaśaśṛṅgitā //
[2,2.216]	asmākaṃ tu pramāṇena prasādādīśvarasya ca / uktabhaṅgayā'gamānāṃ ca prāmāṇyād yujyate 'khilam //
[2,2.217]	dṛśyatvād vimaṃta mithyā svapnavaccediyaṃ ca mā / mithyā cet sādhyasiddhirna vyabhicāro na ced bhavet //
