[2,2.218]	sādhakatvamasatyasya sādhyaṃ vipratipattitaḥ / tasya cetyanavasthā syāt sattvaṃ cāsyānubhūtitaḥ //
[2,2.219]	anubhūtivirodhena mithyātve mā na kācana / atītānāgatau kālāvapi naḥ sākṣigocarau / tatsambandhitayā sattvamapi dṛṣṭasya sākṣigam //
[2,2.220]	dṛḍhadṛṣṭaṃ tu yad dṛṣṭaṃ dṛṣṭābhāsastato 'param / bhrānteḥ saṃvṛtisatyasya viśeṣo 'vyabhicāravān / tenāpyaṅgīkṛtaḥ samyak sa naḥ satyatvameva hi //
[2,2.221]	vijñānād vyabhicāro 'sya kadācit syāditi pramā / naiva dṛṣṭā pramā sā ca na bhavet svavirodhataḥ //
[2,2.222]	bhedo viśeṣyadharmyādigrahaṇāpekṣayā yadi / anyonyāśrayatāhetordurgāhya iti yanna tat //
[2,2.223]	svarūpaṃ vastuno bhedo yanna tasya grahe grahaḥ / anyathāsyāmunā bheda iti vaktuṃ na yujyate //
[2,2.224]	agṛhīto yadā bhedastadā svasmāditi grahaḥ / syāt pratītivirodhācca na hi kaścit tathā vadet //
[2,2.225]	dharmitvapratiyogitvatadbhedā yugapad yadi / viśeṣaṇaṃ viśeṣyaṃ ca tadbhāvaścaiva gṛhyate //
[2,2.226]	ko virodhaḥ svarūpeṇa gṛhīto bheda eva tu / asyāmuṣmāditi punarviśeṣeṇaiva gṛhyate //
[2,2.227]	kiñca bhedaḥ kathaṃ grāhya iti yaḥ paripṛcchati / dharmyādibhedagrahaṇāt tenokto 'nyonyasaṃśrayaḥ //
[2,2.228]	anyatvāgrahaṇe proktaḥ kathamanyonyasaṃśrayaḥ / anyatvaṃ yadi siddhaṃ syāt kathamanyonyasaṃśrayaḥ //
[2,2.229]	etādṛśasya vaktārāvubhau jātyuttarākarau / māyī mādhyamikaścaiva tadupekṣyau bubhūṣubhiḥ //
[2,2.230]	yacchūnyavādinaḥ śūnyaṃ tadeva brahma māyinaḥ / na hi lakṣaṇabhedo 'sti nirviśeṣatvatastayoḥ //
[2,2.231]	anṛtādivirodhitvamubhayośca svalakṣaṇam / svavākyābhāvasaṃvādānna kṛtyaṃ prativādinaḥ //
[2,2.232]	tatpakṣa iti vaidharmyānna svapnādivadityajaḥ / aprayatnānnirācakre ceti dṛṣṭiviruddhatām / niṣpramāṇatvamapyasya sūcayāmāsa viśvakṛt //
[2,2.233]	jñānamevaikamakhilajñeyākāraṃ prabhāsate / tatra santatibhedaśca svabhedo bheda eva ca / kalpitāḥ pratibhāsante nānāsaṃvṛtibhūmiṣu //
[2,2.234]	ityetadapi no yuktaṃ na hi jñānatayā jagat / bhāsate 'nubhavasyaiva viruddhatvādapeśalam //
[2,2.235]	tanmataṃ kṣaṇikatvācca jñānasya sthirarūpataḥ / jñeyasyoktaprakāreṇa sarvaśrutivirodhataḥ / anubhūtiviruddhatvādapi pakṣā ime 'śivāḥ //
[2,2.236]	āha kṣapaṇako viśvaṃ sadasad dvayamadvayam / dvayādvayamatatsarvaṃ saptabhaṅgisadātanam //
[2,2.237]	naitat padārtha ekasmin yuktaṃ dṛṣṭivirodhataḥ / bhāvābhāvatayā viśvaṃ yena rūpeṇa mīyate / tadrūpameva taditi niyamaḥ kena vāryate //
[2,2.238]	tattaddoṣanivṛttyarthaṃ svīkṛtā tattadātmanā / yadi tairakhilairdeṣairlipyate caladarśanaḥ //
[2,2.239]	atihāya pramāṇāptaṃ niyamaṃ sadasattayā / aśeṣamāviruddhaṃ ca nirmānaṃ vyāhataṃ sadā //
[2,2.240]	sarvaprakāraṃ vadato dṛṣṭahāniramagrahaḥ / svavyāhatatvamityādyā doṣāḥ sarve bhavanti hi //
[2,2.241]	vakti svaprabhamātmānaṃ dehamānaṃ tadapyalam / duṣyaṃ nānāśarīreṣu praveśādanyathābhavāt //
[2,2.242]	anyathābhāvi yad vastu tadanityamiti sthitiḥ / tanmate tadanityatvaṃ pudgalasyānivāritam //
[2,2.243]	nānityatāsmatpakṣe tu caitanyāderviśeṣiṇaḥ / lakṣaṇasya nivṛttau tu syānna taccetane kvacit //
[2,2.244]	otaprotātmakatvaṃ tu paṭe dehe 'ṅgasaṃsthitiḥ / ityādilakṣaṇasyaiva nivṛttau syādanityatā //
[2,2.245]	bhautikaṃ tveva rūpādi vyāptaṃ nāśena no mate / naivaṃ tasyānyathābhāvo yasyānityatvamīritam //
[2,2.246]	rūpādiyuktasya tathā jagannāśitvasiddhaye / vyāptyā tayānyathābhāvādātmano 'nityatā bhavet //
[2,2.247]	nityordhvagatirapyeṣā yā muktiriti kathyate / alokākāśamāptasya kathaṃ na vikṛtiśca sā //
[2,2.248]	kīdṛśaścānyathābhāvo nāśahetutayeṣyate / saṃsthānāpagamaścet sa na hi bhūsāgarādiṣu //
[2,2.249]	yaḥ kaścidanyathābhāvo yadi muktiśca tādṛśī / dehamāne vikāraḥ syāditi sthāsnūnanātmanaḥ //
[2,2.250]	āha hastyādideheṣu hyapi syādanyathābhāvaḥ / aṇudehasya jīvasya gajatve vikṛtirhi yā / dehavyāptyai viśeṣaḥ kastasyāḥ sthāsnutanau ca nuḥ //
[2,2.251]	gītāt puṣpaphalāvāptiḥ sparśāt kārśyaṃ rasāt sthitiḥ / api vṛkṣasya dṛśyanta iti nānātmatā bhavet / evañcātmākārtsnyamiti tata evāha vedavit //
[2,2.252]	sarvajñatvādikaiḥ sarvairguṇairyuktaṃ sadāśivam / jagadvicitraracanākartāraṃ doṣavarjitam //
[2,2.253]	āhuḥ pāśupatāstacca bahuśrutivirodhataḥ / nopādeyaṃ mataṃ hyasya devasya stuhi gartagam //
[2,2.254]	utpipeṣa śirastasya gṛṇīṣe satpatiṃ padam / yad viṣṇorupamaṃ hantuṃ rudramākṛṣṭate mayā //
[2,2.255]	dhanuryaṃ kāmaye taṃ tamugraṃ mā śiśnadevatāḥ / ghnañchiśnadevāneko 'sāvāsīnnārāyaṇaḥ paraḥ //
[2,2.256]	tasmād rudraḥ samprasādaścābhūtāṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ makham / yajñena yajñamayajantābadhnan puruṣaṃ paśum //
[2,2.257]	yo bhūtānāmadhipatī rudrastanticaro vṛṣā / ityādiśrutisāmarthyāt pāratantryaṃ janirmṛtiḥ //
[2,2.258]	parādhīnaparaprāptirajñatvaṃ praḷaye 'bhavaḥ / pratīyante sadoṣatvānneśaḥ paśupatistataḥ //
[2,2.259]	aśarīratvatastasya sambandho jagatā kvacit / kartṛtvena na yujyeta dehino jñānadṛṣṭitaḥ //
[2,2.260]	na ca dehādivad viśvamasya syād bhogasambhavāt / adhiṣṭhāne sthitaḥ kartā kāryaṃ kurvan pratīyate / nāsyādhiṣṭhānayogo 'sti bhūtānāṃ praḷaye tadā //
[2,2.261]	adehaścedasārvajñaḥ śilākāṣṭhādivat sadā / dehī cedantavāneva yajñadattanidarśanāt //
[2,2.262]	nacaitadakhilaṃ viṣṇau śrutiprāmāṇyagauravāt / manobuddhayaṅgitāṃ viṣṇorlakṣayāmo ya eva saḥ //
[2,2.263]	sa eva deho vijñānamaiśvaryaṃ śaktirūrjitā / deho viṣṇorna te viṣṇo vāsudevo 'grato 'bhavat //
[2,2.264]	eko nārāyaṇastvāsīnna brahmā na ca śaṅkaraḥ / ajasya nābhāvadhyekamarpitaṃ mātrayā paraḥ //
[2,2.265]	saddehaḥ sukhagandhaśca jñānabhāḥ satparākramaḥ / jñānajñānaḥ sukhasukhaḥ sa viṣṇuḥ paramākṣaraḥ //
[2,2.266]	ānanda eka evāgra āsīnnārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ / priyaṃ tasya śire modapramodau ca bhujau hareḥ //
[2,2.267]	ānando madhyato brahma pucchaṃ nānyadabhūt kvacit / manaso 'syābhavad brahmā lalāṭādapi śaṅkaraḥ //
[2,2.268]	pakṣayorgaruḍaḥ śeṣo mukhādāsa sarasvatī / sahasraśīrṣā puruṣaḥ sahasrākṣaḥ sahasrapāt //
[2,2.269]	ityādiśrutisandarbhabalānnityaguṇātmanaḥ / viṣṇordehājjagat sarvamāvirāsīditīyate //
[2,2.270]	mānavattvād virodhaḥ ko nāmānaṃ kvacidiṣyate / avirodho virodhaśca mānenaiva hi gamyate //
[2,2.271]	ata uktaṃ samastaṃ ca vāsudevasya yujyate / śivādināmayuktāśca śrutayo viṣṇuvācakāḥ //
[2,2.272]	nāmāni sarvāṇi ca yameko yo devanāmadhāḥ / viṣṇunāmāni nānyasya sarvanāmā hariḥ svayam //
[2,2.273]	na nārāyaṇanāmāni tadanyeṣvapare harau / ityādiśrutayastatra mānaṃ coktaḥ samanvayaḥ //
[2,2.274]	purāṇāni purāṇādyairviruddhatvānna tat pramā / tadviruddheṣu no mānaṃ pūrvāparavirodhataḥ //
[2,2.275]	samabrāhmavirodhācca niyamād vaiṣṇaveṣvapi / mohārthamuktitaścaiva viṣṇureko guṇārṇavaḥ //
[2,2.276]	skandasūryagaṇeśādimatāni nyāyato 'mutaḥ / nirākṛtānyaśeṣeṇa siddhāntasyāviśeṣataḥ //
[2,2.277]	nirākṛtau viśeṣasya bhāvācchaktimataṃ pṛthak / dūṣyate mahatī devī hrīṅkarī sarvakāraṇam / tripurābhairavītyādināmabhiḥ sābhidhīyate //
[2,2.278]	tasyāḥ sadāśivādyāśca jāyante devamānuṣāḥ / bhūtabhautikamapyetaditi tannopapadyate //
[2,2.279]	dṛṣṭā pumbhyaḥ sadā sṛṣṭiḥ strīpumbhyo vā viśeṣataḥ / kevalābhyo na hi strībhyastata utpattyasambhavāt //
[2,2.280]	nārcyaṃ mahāvāmamataṃ vāmairanyadudīryate / śivopasarjanā śaktiḥ sasarjedaṃ samantataḥ //
[2,2.281]	iti taccopapannaṃ na śivasyākaraṇatvataḥ / adehatvādapi hyanye brūyuḥ sarvajñamīśvaram //
[2,2.282]	aṇuvāmā na tadyuktamīśavādapraveśanāt / sārvajñyādiguṇairyuktaṃ gurukalpanayā dvayam //
[2,2.283]	na yujyate hyatastvīśa eka eva prayojakaḥ / uktadoṣaśca tatpakṣa iti naivātra dūṣyate //
[2,2.284]	śrutismṛtītihāsānāṃ sāmastyena virodhataḥ / satāṃ jugupsitatvācca nāṅgīkāryaṃ hi tanmatam //
[2,2.285]	pañcarātraniṣedhārthametānyācakṣate yadi / sūtrāṇyativiruddhaṃ tad yata āha sa bhārate //
[2,2.286]	pañcarātrasya kṛtsnasya vaktā nārāyaṇaḥ svayam / jñāneṣveteṣu rājendra sarveṣvetad viśiṣṭate //
[2,2.287]	pañcarātravido ye tu yathākramaparā nṛpa / ekāntabhāvopagatā vāsudevaṃ viśanti te //
[2,2.288]	iti gītā ca tacchāstrasaṅkṣepa iti hīritam / vedena pañcarātreṇa bhaktayā yajñena caiva hi //
[2,2.289]	dṛśyo 'haṃ nānyathā dṛśyo varṣakoṭiśatairapi / iti vārāhavacanaṃ ślokā iti vacaḥ śrutau //
[2,2.290]	vedaiśca pañcarātraiśca dhyeyo nārāyaṇaḥ paraḥ / pañcarātraṃ ca vedāśca vidyaikaiva dvidheyate //
[2,2.291]	ityādivedavacanaiḥ pañcarātramapodyate / kathamevātra doṣaḥ ka utpattirjño 'ta ityapi //
[2,2.292]	ihaivoktā nacābhūtabhāvastatrāpi kathyate / anādikarmaṇā baddho jīvaḥ saṃsāramaṇḍale //
[2,2.293]	vāsudevecchayā nityaṃ bhramatīti hi tadvacaḥ / na hi saṃsārasāditvaṃ pañcarātroditaṃ kvacit //
[2,2.294]	jīvābhimāniśeṣasya nāmnā saṅkarṣaṇasya tu / vāsudevājjaniḥ proktā pradyumnasya tatastathā //
[2,2.295]	mano 'bhimāninaḥ kāmasyaivaṃ sākṣāddhareḥ kvacit / saṅkarṣaṇādināmnaiva nityācintyoruśaktitaḥ / vyūha ukto 'nyathānūdya kathaṃ duṣṭatvamucyate //
[2,2.296]	yadi vidyāccaturvedānitivad vedapūraṇam / pañcarātrāditi kuto dveṣaḥ śāṇḍilyavartane //
[2,2.297]	ataḥ paramaśāstrorudveṣāduditamāsuraiḥ / dūṣaṇaṃ pañcarātrasya vīkṣāyāmapi na kṣamam //
[2,2.298]	ato 'śeṣajagaddhātā nirdoṣoruguṇārṇavaḥ / nārāyaṇaḥ śrutigaṇatātparyādavasīyate //
[2,2.299]	andhaṃ tamaḥ praviśanti ye tvavidyāmupāsate / tato bhūya ivāpsyanti ye tasyā naiva nindakāḥ //
[2,2.300]	tato vidyāmavidyāṃ ca yo jānātyubhayaṃ saha / doṣajñānādatītyaitān vidyayāmṛtamaśnute //
<iti śrīmadānandatīrthabhagavatpādācāryaviracite śrīmadbrahmasūtrānuvyākhyāne dvitīyādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ ||>
{2,3}
[2,3.1]	athāśeṣasamāmnāyavirodhāpākṛtiṃ prabhuḥ / kariṣyannadhidaivādhibhūtajīvaparātmanām //
[2,3.2]	svarūpanirṇayāyaiva vacanānāṃ parasparam / pādenānenāvirodhaṃ darśayatyamitadyutiḥ //
[2,3.3]	anubhūtiyuktibahuvāgvailomyaṃ ca tato 'dhikam / etat sarvaṃ sataḥ sāmyaṃ dvāravaiyarthyameva ca //
[2,3.4]	dṛṣṭayuktayanusāritvamuktānyārthāvirodhataḥ / prasiddhanāmasvīkāre bahuvākyānuvatirtā //
[2,3.5]	lokadṛṣṭānusāritvaṃ jīvasāmyamanāditā / tatra tatra parijñānaṃ guṇasāmyaśrutī tathā //
[2,3.6]	utpattimattvaṃ svaguṇānanubhūtyalpakalpane / nānāśrutiśca vaicitṛyaṃ yuktayaḥ pūrvapakṣagāḥ //
[2,3.7]	vyavasthānupapattiśca svātantryamanusāritā / mukhyatā śaktimattvaṃ ca vairūpyaṃ sarvasaṅgrahaḥ //
[2,3.8]	gatyādirīśaśaktiśca sarvamānavirodhitā / abhīṣyāsiddhisuvyaktī śāstrasiddhivirparyayaḥ / viśeṣakāraṇaṃ ceti siddhāntasyaiva sādhakāḥ //
[2,3.9]	prakṛtiḥ puruṣaḥ kālo devāstadabhimāninaḥ / mahadādyāśca jāyante parādhīnaviśeṣitā / idaṃ sarvaṃ sasarjeti janimattvamihoditam //
[2,3.10]	avakāśamātramākāśaḥ kathamutpadyate 'nyathā / yadyanākāśatā pūrvaṃ kiṃ mūrtanibiḍaṃ jagat //
[2,3.11]	mūtarsampūrṇatā caiva yadyanākāśatā bhavet / mūrtadravyāṇi cākāśe sthitānyeva hi sarvadā //
[2,3.12]	ata ākāśaśabdoktastaddevo 'tra vināyakaḥ / dehotpattyā samutpanna iti śrutyābhidhīyate //
[2,3.13]	bhūtamapyasitaṃ divyadṛṣṭigocarameva tu / utpadyate 'vyākṛtaṃ hi gaganaṃ sākṣigocaram / pradeśa iti vijñeyaṃ nityaṃ notpadyate hi tat //
[2,3.14]	tathāpi pūrvasambandhaparatantraviśeṣayuk / khamevotpattimannāma śrutiśabdavivakṣitam //
[2,3.15]	prakṛtiḥ puruṣaḥ kāla ityete ca samastaśaḥ / īśādhīnaviśeṣeṇa janyā ityeva kīrtitāḥ //
[2,3.16]	kālapravāha evaiko nityo natu viśeṣavān / puruṣāvyaktakālānāṃ ramaivaikābhimāninī //
[2,3.17]	sisṛkṣutvaviśeṣaṃ tat sākṣād bhagavadicchayā / prāptaiva sṛṣṭetyuditā pradhānaṃ vikṛterapi //
[2,3.18]	pumāṃso dehasambandhāt sṛṣṭimanta itīritāḥ / evaṃ praḷayakāle 'pi pratibhātaparāvaraḥ //
[2,3.19]	mukhyāvāyurnityasamaḥ śarīrotpattikāraṇāt / parādhīnaviśeṣeṇa janimāneva śabditaḥ //
[2,3.20]	naiva kiñcit tato janmavarjitaṃ paramādṛte / parādhīnaviśeṣatve janmanaḥ sthūlatābhavaḥ //
[2,3.21]	pūrvaśabdavilopaśca yadi janmeti kīrtyate / ramāyā naiva janmāsti caitanyasyāpi kevalam //
[2,3.22]	pradhanasya ca vedasya vedasyāpīśvarecchayā / vyaktirnāma viśeṣo 'sti tasmāt tadvaśataiva hi //
[2,3.23]	utpattiratra kathitā svatantratvāt parātmanaḥ / naivotpattiḥ kathamapi na svatantraṃ tato 'param //
[2,3.24]	acchedyasyāpi jīvasya vibhāgaṃ bahudhā hariḥ / kṛtvā bhogān pradāyaiva caikyamāpādayet punaḥ //
[2,3.25]	ata īśavaśaṃ sarvaṃ cetanācetanaṃ jagat / avibhāgaṃ vibhāgāya yadā nayati keśavaḥ / kimaśakyaṃ pareśasya tadeti hyabhidhīyate //
[2,3.26]	evaṃ sthite 'pi jīvaikyaṃ kecidāhuḥ parātmanā / tad yo 'hamitipūrvābhiḥ śrutibhiścānumābalāt //
[2,3.27]	na tad yuktaṃ yato viṣṇuḥ pṛthagevābhidhīyate / prajñānetro 'loka iti muktau bhedo 'bhidhīyate / etamānandamityanyā paramaṃ sāmyamityapi //
[2,3.28]	idaṃ jñānamapāśritya mama sādharmyamāgatāḥ / sarge 'pi nopajāyante praḷaye na vyathanti ca //
[2,3.29]	upasampadya tajjyotiḥ svarūpeṇābhipadyate / tatra paryeti jakṣaṃśca krīḍannapi sadā sukhī //
[2,3.30]	ācakṣva me mokṣaṃ dhīrā yaṃ pravadanti tam / ityakta āha vāgdevī paraṃ mokṣaṃ prajāpateḥ //
[2,3.31]	śākhāṃ śākhāṃ mahānadyaḥ saṃyānti paritaḥsravāḥ / dhānāpūpā māṃsakāmāḥ sadā pāyasakardamāḥ //
[2,3.32]	yasminnagnimukhā devāḥ sendrāḥ sahamarudgaṇāḥ / ījire kratubhiḥ śreṣṭhaistadakṣaramupāsate //
[2,3.33]	praviśanti paraṃ devaṃ muktāstatraiva bhoginaḥ / nirgacchanti yathākāmaṃ pareśenaiva coditāḥ //
[2,3.34]	bhedadṛṣṭayābhimānena niḥsaṅgenāpi kamarṇā / kartṛtvāt saguṇaṃ brahma puruṣaṃ puruṣarṣabham //
[2,3.35]	sa saṅgatya punaḥ kāle kāleneśvaramūrtitā / jāte 'guṇavyatikare yathāpūrvaṃ prajāyate //
[2,3.36]	ṛcāṃ tvaḥ poṣamāste ca pareṇa preritāḥ sadā / yatkāmastat sṛjatyaddhaiṣātmanā tat sṛjatyapi //
[2,3.37]	sahaiva brahmaṇā kāmān bhuṅkate nistīrṇatadguṇaḥ / duḥkhādīṃśca parityajya jagadvayāpāravarjitaḥ //
[2,3.38]	bhuṅkte bhogān sahaivoccānityādyāgamamānataḥ / muktasya bhedāvagateḥ kathameva hyabhinnatā //
[2,3.39]	jīveśayornānumā ca tadabhedaṃ pramāpayet / mithyaiva bhedo vimato bhedatvāccandrabhedavat / iti cet sādhyadharmo 'yaṃ sannasan vā navobhayam //
[2,3.40]	yadi sannapasiddhāntaḥ sa evāsannitīrite / nobhayaṃ cenna siddhaṃ taditi mānasya dūṣaṇam //
[2,3.41]	na ca mānāntareṇaitacchakyaṃ sādhayituṃ kvacit / anumānena cet saiva hyanavasthā bhaviṣyati //
[2,3.42]	nacāgamastadartho 'sti nāsadāsīnna tad vadet / pariśeṣādanirvācyaṃ yadi siddhayet parātmanaḥ //
[2,3.43]	anirvācyatvameva syāt pariśiṣṭo hyasau tadā / nacānya āgamastatra sadasatpratiyogini //
[2,3.44]	na ca pratyakṣamātrāsti nacārthāpattiriṣyate / bādhāyogāt sata iti bādhābhāvata eva hi //
[2,3.45]	viṣayasya kuto bādho vidyamānaṃ hi bādhyate / na hi vandhyāsuto vadhyo yajñadatto hi vadhyate //
[2,3.46]	bādhāyogaḥ sata iti vyāptireṣā kva dṛśyate / kaścāyaṃ bādha uddiṣṭo na hi nāśo 'sato bhavet / nivṛttiścāpravṛttasya kathamevopapadyate //
[2,3.47]	nāsīdasti bhaviṣyacca taditi jñānameyatā / yadi bādhastadāsattvaṃ tenaivāṅgīkṛtaṃ punaḥ //
[2,3.48]	pratītirnāsata iti vadannaṅgīkaroti tām / niṣedho hyapratītasya kathañcinnopapadyate //
[2,3.49]	na copamā bhavedatra pratyakṣāt sattvameva ca / śāstragamyapareśānād bhedaḥ svātmana īyate //
[2,3.50]	anubhūtivirodhena kathamekatvamucyate / kiñcitkartā ca duḥkhīti sarvairevānubhūyate //
[2,3.51]	sarvajño bhagavān viṣṇuḥ sarvaśaktiriti śrutaḥ / anubhūtāddhi bhedena śrutireṣā vadatyamum //
[2,3.52]	upajīvyaviruddhaṃ tu kathamaikyaṃ śrutirvadet / aprāmāṇyaṃ yadā bhedavācakasya bhaviṣyati //
[2,3.53]	sa eva dharmiṇo grāhī tadabhedaḥ kathaṃ bhavet / yat svarūpagrahe mānaṃ taddharme na kathaṃ bhavet //
[2,3.54]	ekavijñānavijñaptyā dvayaṃ mānaṃ bhaviṣyati / na cedekamamānaṃ tad dvayamapyatra no bhavet //
[2,3.55]	dharmigrāhivirodhastu tasmānmānasya dūṣaṇam / nopajīvyo hyabhedo 'tra kvacid bhedaśruterbalāt //
[2,3.56]	na ca mānāntaropeyaṃ brahma tad bhavati kvacit / yena mānena cāpeyaṃ bhedastenāvagamyate //
[2,3.57]	sarvajñānamayaiveśo yadyupeyaḥ kathañcana / sarvajñathvaguṇenaiva tayā bhedo 'vagamyate //
[2,3.58]	na duḥkhānubhavaḥ kvāpi mithyānubhavatāṃ vrajet / na hi bādhaḥ kvacid dṛṣṭo duḥkhādyanubhavasya tu //
[2,3.59]	yadi duḥkhānubhūtiśca bhrāntirityavasīyate / aduḥkhitāśrutiḥ kena na bhrāntiriti gamyate //
[2,3.60]	śrutisvarūpamarthaśca mānenaivāvasīyate / taccenmānaṃ gṛhītaṃ te kiṃ duḥkhānubhave bhramaḥ //
[2,3.61]	na ca bādhaviśeṣo 'sti yadabādhitameva tat / bādho yadyanubhūte 'rthe kathaṃ nirṇaya īyate //
[2,3.62]	ko 'pi hy artho na niścetuṃ śakyate bhramavādinā / bhramatvamabhramatvaṃ ca yadaivānubhavopagam / ekasya bhramatā tatra parasyābhramatā kutaḥ //
[2,3.63]	bhramatvamabhramatvaṃ ca sarvaṃ vedyaṃ hi sākṣiṇā / sa cet sākṣī kvacid duṣyaḥ kathaṃ nirṇaya īyate //
[2,3.64]	viśeṣā sarva evaite sākṣipratyayagocarāḥ / ūrīkṛtya ca tān sarvān vyavahāraḥ pravartate / sākṣiṇo vyavasāyī tu vyavahāro 'bhidhīyate //
[2,3.65]	tasmāt sarvaprasiddhasya vyavahārasya siddhaye / sākṣī nirdoṣa evaikaḥ sadāṅgīkārya eva naḥ //
[2,3.66]	śuddhaḥ sākṣī yadā siddho duḥkhitvaṃ vāryate katham / upajīvyapramāṇaṃ tad bhedagrāhakameva hi / ato jīveśayorbhedaḥ śrutisāmarthyasusthiraḥ //
[2,3.67]	tathāpi tu cidānandapūrvāstatsadṛśā guṇāḥ / sārasvarūpamasyāpi muktāvapyavaśiṣyate //
[2,3.68]	ato 'bhedavadevaitāḥ śrutayaḥ pravadanti hi / paurāṇāni ca vākyāni sādṛśyābhedasaṃśrayāt //
[2,3.69]	sādṛśyācca pradhānatvāt svātantryādapicābhidām / āhurīśena jīvasya na svarūpābhidāṃ kvacit //
[2,3.70]	sthānaikyamaikamatyaṃ ca muktasya tu viśiṣṭate / sādṛśyaṃ ca viśeṣeṇa jaḍānāṃ dvayameva tu / bhavet sādṛśyamatyalpaṃ tṛtīyaṃ paramātmanā //
[2,3.71]	īśarūpakriyāṇāṃ ca guṇānāmapi sarvaśaḥ / tathaivāvayavānāṃ tatsvarūpaikyaṃ tu mukhyataḥ //
[2,3.72]	yathodakaṃ durge vṛṣṭaṃ parvateṣu vidhāvati / evaṃ dharmān pṛthak paśyaṃstānevānuvidhāvati / iti śruternobhayaṃ ca bhedābhedākhyamiṣyate //
[2,3.73]	ekamevādvitīyaṃ neha nānāsti kiñcana / mṛtyoḥ sa mṛtyumāpnoti ya iha nāneva paśyati //
[2,3.74]	iti śrutāvivetyasmād bhedābhedanirākṛtiḥ / ivobhaye ca sādṛśya iti vāk śabdanirṇaye //
[2,3.75]	bhedasya muktau vacanādapi tatpakṣanigrahaḥ / cetanatvādisādṛśyaṃ yadyabheda itīṣyate / aṅgīkṛtaṃ tadasmābhirna svarūpaikatā kvacit //
[2,3.76]	na kenacidabhedo 'sti bhedābhedo 'pivā kvacit / samudāyamṛte viṣṇoḥ svaguṇādīn vināpi vā //
[2,3.77]	iti śruterna tasyāsti bhedābhedo 'pi kenacit / abhedaśrutayo' ṃśatvāt sādṛśyaṃ cāṃśatāsya tu //
[2,3.78]	aṃśastu dvividho jñeyaḥ svarūpāṃśo 'nya eva ca / vibhinnāṃśo 'lpaśaktiḥ syāt kiñcitsādṛśyamātrayuk //
[2,3.79]	aṃśino yattu sāmarthyaṃ yat svarūpaṃ yathā sthitiḥ / sa eva cet svarūpāṃśaḥ prādurbhāvā hareryathā //
[2,3.80]	sūryamaṇḍalamānyekastatprakāśābhimānavān / sūryo 'tha saptamābdheśca bāhyodasya ca vāripaḥ //
[2,3.81]	kaṭhinatvena mervādeḥ pṛthivyā api devatā / dharādevyevamevaiko bhagavān viṣṇuravyayaḥ / nānāvatārarūpeṇa sthitaḥ pūrṇaguṇaḥ sadā //
[2,3.82]	viṇmūtrākṣyādimāninyo yathāpabhraṣṭadevatāḥ / sūryādibhyastathaivāyaṃ saṃsārī paramāt pṛthak //
[2,3.83]	dehadoṣaiśca duṣṭatvādapabhraṣṭākhyadevatāḥ / anyāḥ sūryādidevebhyo hyanugrāhyāśca taiḥ sadā //
[2,3.84]	evameva parād viṣṇoḥ pṛthak saṃsāriṇo matāḥ / anugrāhyāśca tenaiva tatprasādācca mokṣiṇaḥ //
[2,3.85]	na tu matsyādirūpāṇāmanugrāhyatvamiṣyate / guṇairaśeṣaiḥ pūrṇatvānmukhyābhedo 'parairnaca //
[2,3.86]	aṃśābhāsāśca sarve 'pi parasyāṃśā na mukhyataḥ / yathaiṣā puruṣe cchāyā etasminnetadātatam //
[2,3.87]	na tu pumpādavat pādā jīvā ete parātmanaḥ / pūrṇāstasya guṇā eva prādurbhāvatayā sthitāḥ / evaṃ jagāda paramaśrutirnārāyaṇaṃ param //
[2,3.88]	akṣayo bhagavān viṣṇurlakṣmyāvāso laye sthitaḥ / muktaiḥ sadā cintyamāno brahmādyaistāratamyagaiḥ //
[2,3.89]	prakṛtiḥ puruṣaḥ kālo vedāśceti catuṣyayam / nityaṃ svarūpato viṣṇorviśeṣāvāptimātrataḥ / utpattimāditi proktaṃ lakṣmīstadabhimāninī //
[2,3.90]	tato jātaḥ pumān nāma brahmāsyāṃ vāsudevataḥ / sūtrātmā prāṇanāmā ca devyau prakṛtimāninī //
[2,3.91]	tato rūpaṃ mahān nāma brahmaṇo 'haṅkṛtiḥ śivaḥ / brahmaṇo buddhināmnomā tata indro mano 'bhidhaḥ / skandaśca tata evānye sarve devāḥ prajajñire //
[2,3.92]	tatra pūrvatanaḥ śreyān guṇaiḥ sarvaiḥ samastaśaḥ / tebhyaśca bhagavān viṣṇustadadhīnā ime sadā //
[2,3.93]	janmasthitilayājñānaniyatijñānasaṃsṛtiḥ / mokṣaśca tadadhīnatvameteṣāṃ naiva hīyate //
[2,3.94]	muktāvapi sa evaikaḥ svatantraḥ pūrṇasadguṇaḥ / iti śrutyupapattibhyāṃ pāde 'smin prabhuṇoditam //
<iti śrīmadānandatīrthabhagavatpādācāryaviracite śrīmadbrahmasūtrānuvyākhyāne dvitīyādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ ||>
{2,4}
[2,4.1]	śrutyarthaḥ śrutiyuktibhyāṃ viruddha iva dṛśyate / yatra tannirṇayaṃ devaḥ suviśiṣṭopapattibhiḥ / karotyanena pādena tatra spaṣṭārthavacchrutiḥ //
[2,4.2]	viśeṣaśrutivairūpyaṃ māhātmyaṃ vyaktasadguṇāḥ / dṛṣṭāyuktiḥ samānatvaṃ kartṛśaktirvimiśratā //
[2,4.3]	yuktayaḥ pūrvapakṣeṣu sunirṇītāsatu tādṛśāḥ / yuktayo nirṇayasyaiva svayaṃ bhagavatoditāḥ //
<iti śrīmadānandatīrthabhagavatpādācāryaviracite śrīmadbrahmasūtrānuvyākhyāne dvitīyo 'dhyāyaḥ ||>
{3,1}
[3,1.1]	svābhāvikānyathānāmasahābhāvānyathoktayaḥ / aviśeṣo viśeṣau ca sahabhāvo vimiśratā //
[3,1.2]	viruddhoktiḥ sahasthānaṃ vaiyarthyaṃ cānyathāgatiḥ / yuktayaḥ pūrvapakṣasya guṇādhikyārthatobhavau //
[3,1.3]	upapattirdvirūpatvamādhikyamanurūpatā / yogyatā prabalatvaṃ ca vibhāgaḥ kāraṇābhavaḥ / kḷptiranyāgatiścaiva siddhāntasyaiva sādhakāḥ //
[3,1.4]	bījāpūruṣayonīnāṃ saṅgātiniyamojkhitim / athaśabdena bhagavānāha kāraṇataśca tām //
<iti śrīmadānandatīrthabhagavatpādācāryaviracite śrīmadbrahmasūtrānuvyākhyāne tṛtīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pādaḥ ||>
{3,2}
[3,2.1]	paścādadṛṣṭayavijñānakāladuḥkhapṛthagbhavāḥ / sthānabhedo viruddhatvaṃ nyāyasāmyaṃ svatobhavaḥ //
[3,2.2]	guṇasāmyamayogaśca tarkabādho vilomatā / nānābhāvaḥ pralobhaśca pūrvapakṣagāḥ //
[3,2.3]	aśakyakartṛtāśaktiḥ svato 'bodhastadeva ca / amānakḷptisanmānavyavasthātyalpatābhavāḥ //
[3,2.4]	viśeṣadṛṣṭivākye ca puṃśaktiḥ sunidarśanam / alaukikatvamādhikyaṃ svātantryaṃ nirṇayapramāḥ //
[3,2.5]	vāsanāḥ sarvavastūnāmanādyanubhavāgatāḥ / santyevāśeṣajīvānāmanādimanasi sthitāḥ //
[3,2.6]	triguṇātmakaṃ mano 'styeva yāvanmuktiḥ sadātanam / tatraivāśeṣasaṃskārāḥ sañcīyante sadaiva ca //
[3,2.7]	sūkṣmatvena laye sacca prākṛtairupacīyate / sṛṣṭikāle yadā tanna kutaḥ saṃsārasaṃsthitiḥ //
[3,2.8]	saṃskārairbhagavāneva sṛṣṭvā nānāvidhaṃ jagat / svapnakāle darśayati bhrāntirjāgrattvameva hi //
[3,2.9]	adṛṣṭe cāśrute bhāve na bhāva upajāyate / adṛṣṭādaśrutād bhāvānna bhāva upajāyate //
[3,2.10]	iti śrutipurāṇoktiranāditvāttu yujyate / kadācid darśanāyogyaṃ yat tatrāpi vibhāgataḥ //
[3,2.11]	dṛṣṭaṃ samānādhikaraṇaṃ dṛśyate ca sa ca bhramaḥ / vāsanāmātramūlatvājjāgradvat spaṣṭatā na ca //
[3,2.12]	bhedo 'bhedo 'thavā dvandvamiti praśno na yujyate / draṣṭuḥ svapnasya dṛṣṭatvād bhedasyaivākhilairjanaiḥ //
[3,2.13]	praśnadoṣā hi catvāraḥ svavyāhatirasaṅgatiḥ / siddhārthatā ca vaiphalyaṃ na taiḥ syāt tattvanirṇayaḥ //
[3,2.14]	tattvanirṇayavailomyaṃ syād vāde 'pi hi nigrahaḥ / udbhāvanīyameva syānna kathāvasitirbhavet //
[3,2.15]	vijigīṣukathāyāṃ tu kathāvasitikāraṇam / parihāre 'pi siddhatvaṃ dūṣaṇaṃ prativādinaḥ / pratijñāyāṃ tadanyasya siddhataiva hi sādhakā //
[3,2.16]	āśrayavyāśrayāsiddhī sādhyasiddhiśca dūṣaṇam / keṣāñcin na ca te doṣā vyāptau satyāṃ kathañcana //
[3,2.17]	doṣo vyāhatirevāsti nṛśṛṅgāstitvasādhane / yatra vyāhatatā nāsti ko 'tisaṅgo 'sya sādhane //
[3,2.18]	pratyakṣāgamamūlāstu nyāyāḥ sarve bhavanti hi / nyāyābhāsā amūlāḥ syurnyāyasyānyasya tau punaḥ //
[3,2.19]	adṛṣṭe vyabhicāre tu sādhakaṃ taditi sphuṭam / jñāyate sākṣiṇaivādvā mānabādhe na tad bhavet //
[3,2.20]	yat sākṣiṇaiva mānatvaṃ mānānāmavasīyate / amānasya tu mānatvaṃ mānasatvāccalaṃ bhavet //
[3,2.21]	utsargato 'pi yat prāptamapavādavivarjitam / vyabhicāryapavādena mānameva bhaviṣyati //
[3,2.22]	ato hi bhojanādīnāmiṣṭasādhanatānumā / mānaṃ vyavahṛtau nityaṃ vyabhicāro hi tatra ca //
[3,2.23]	vyāptatve vyāśrayatvaṃ tu kathameva hi dūṣaṇam / rohiṇyudaya āsannaḥ kṛttikābhyuditā yataḥ / ityukte sādhanaṃ no kiṃ na hyājñaivātra sādhakā //
[3,2.24]	anyat sadasatorviśvamiti ca vyāhateramā / asiddhasādhane doṣaḥ ko vyāptiryadi vidyate //
[3,2.25]	vyāptiśca vyatirekeṇa tatra taiścaiva gamyate / aprasiddhasya sādhyasya sādhakatvaṃ yadeṣyate / liṅgasyoktau viśeṣo 'yaṃ kena mānena gamyate //
[3,2.26]	sādhanaṃ paramāṇvāderyadāsiddhasya ceṣyate / yathānubhavamevaitannāṅgīkāryaṃ kutastadā //
[3,2.27]	yatra nātiprasaṅgo 'sti mānaṃ na ca viparyate / kliṣṭakalpanayaivātra sādhyamityatidurvacaḥ //
[3,2.28]	pariśeṣo mithaḥsiddhiḥ cakrakasvāśrayādayaḥ / asiddhasādhakatvena pañcāvayavatāṃ vinā / aṅgīkāryāḥ samastaistanniyamaḥ kiṃnibandhanaḥ //
[3,2.29]	siddasādhanatāyāṃ ca na kathāvasitirbhavet / vyabhicāro hetvasiddhirekapakṣe 'pi dūṣaṇam //
[3,2.30]	sādhyasādhanavaikalyaṃ dṛṣṭāntasya viśeṣaṇe / vaiyathyarmekāsiddhau ca viśiṣṭāsiddhireva hi //
[3,2.31]	aprayojakatā tatra prathamapraśnadūṣaṇam / siddhapraśnādikaṃ yat tadādhikyāntagartaṃ bhavet //
[3,2.32]	arthāpattyupamābhāvā anumāntargatāḥ kvacit / pratyakṣāntargato 'bhāvaḥ sukhāderniyamena ca //
[3,2.33]	anyatra khaḍiti prāptaḥ prārambhādyāśca yuktayaḥ / āgamārthāvasityarthā niyatavyāptayo 'khilāḥ //
[3,2.34]	vākyaṃ prakaraṇaṃ sthānaṃ samākhyā ca tathāvidhāḥ / kurupāṇḍavavat teṣāmupapatteḥ pṛthag vacaḥ //
[3,2.35]	svanyāyaiḥ sādhanaṃ kāryaṃ paranyāyaistu dūṣaṇam / svanyāyairdūṣaṇaṃ ca syāt sādhitaiḥ prativādinaḥ //
[3,2.36]	prasaṅgārthatayā proktā na siddhāntasya dūṣakāḥ / chalaṃ jātiriti dvedhā vyāhatyantaramiṣyate / jātiḥ svavyāhatirjñeyā chalamarthāntarottaram //
[3,2.37]	evaṃ saṃśodhitanyāyasadāgamavirodhataḥ / nānirvācyamiha proktaṃ māyāmātrapadena hi //
[3,2.38]	vilakṣaṇaṃ sadasatoriti hi vyāhataṃ svataḥ / pratiyogitvamapyasya brahmaṇo 'ṅgīkṛtaṃ bhavet //
[3,2.39]	mithyā cet pratiyogitvaṃ vailakṣaṇyaṃ tato na hi / avilakṣaṇatvaṃ satyaṃ syānmithyātvaṃ brahmaṇastataḥ //
[3,2.40]	anirvācyasya sattvaṃ vā yadi dharmā na kecana / brahmaṇo naiva jijñāsyaṃ jijñāsā dharmanirṇayaḥ //
[3,2.41]	idamitthamiti jñānaṃ jijñāsāyāḥ prayojanam / itthambhāvo hi dharmo 'sya na cenna pratiyogitā //
[3,2.42]	itthambhāvātmakān dharmānāhuśca śrutayo 'khilāḥ / adṛśyatvādayo 'pyasya guṇā hi prabhuṇoditāḥ //
[3,2.43]	yadi syustādṛśā dharmāḥ sarvajñatvādayo na kim / anyāpekṣā yadi syuṣṭe sattaivaṃ deśakālagā //
[3,2.44]	deśakālānapekṣā hi na sattā kvāpi dṛśyate / sarvadharmojjñitasyāsya kiṃ śāstreṇādhigamyate //
[3,2.45]	mithyādharmavidhātuśca vedasyaivāpramāṇatā / aprāptāṃ bhrāntimāpādya kiṃ vedo mānatāṃ vrajet //
[3,2.46]	na hi vedaṃ vinā brahma vedyaṃ dharmāśca tadgatāḥ / vedavedyasya mithyātvaṃ yadi naikyasya tat katham //
[3,2.47]	dharmāropo 'pi sāmānyadharmādīnāṃ hi daśarne / idantadādidharmitve dharmo 'nyaḥ kalpyate 'tra hi //
[3,2.48]	sarvadharmavihīnasya dharmāropaḥ kva dṛśyate / tadarthaṃ yadi dharmāṇāmāropaḥ sānavasthitiḥ //
[3,2.49]	īśatajjñānavedākṣajānumāmātṛpūrviṇaḥ / bhrāntirviśvasya yenaiva mānābhāsena kalpyate 'tra hi //
[3,2.50]	tanmātrasyānyathā bhāvāt kiṃ na syād viśvasatyatā / yenedaṃ kalpyate bhrāntaṃ bhrāntistasyaiva kiṃ na sā //
[3,2.51]	bhrāntatve tasya viśvāderīśādyabhrāntameva hi / bhaveyurbhrāntayo nṛṇāṃ naiveśādeḥ kathañcana //
[3,2.52]	satyatvamakṣajaprāptaṃ yadi bhrāntamitīṣyate / prāmāṇyamāgamasyāpi pratyakṣādanyataḥ kutaḥ //
[3,2.53]	sākṣipratyakṣato hyeva mānānāṃ mānateyate / sākṣiṇaḥ svaprakāśatvamanavasthā tato na hi //
[3,2.54]	tātkālikaṃ pramāṇatvamakṣajasya yadā bhavet / aikyāgamasya kiṃ na syāt tasyāpyetādṛśaṃ yadi / aikyaprāmāṇyamithyātvaṃ yadā viśvasya satyatā //
[3,2.55]	aikyāgamasya mānatvaṃ yadyabādhyamitīṣyate / akṣajasyāpi mānatvaṃ nābādhyaṃ kimitīṣyate //
[3,2.56]	advaitahānisāmānyānna viśeṣaśca kaścana / yadi svatastvaṃ prāmāṇye viśvasattā kathaṃ na te //
[3,2.57]	prāmāṇyasya ca maryādā kālato vyāhatā bhavet / kālāntare 'pyamānaṃ cedidānīṃ mānatā kutaḥ //
[3,2.58]	mithyātvamānaṃ mokṣe 'pi mānaṃ kiṃ neti bhaṇyatām / mānatve 'dvaitahāniḥ syādamānatve 'pyamokṣatā //
[3,2.59]	viśvasya punarāpattirmithyāmānaṃ yadā na mā / asti cenmuktayavasthā ca dvaitāpattirato 'nyathā //
[3,2.60]	amuktatvaṃ tathā kāle kālādhīnā hi muktatā / kāla evāgamo 'pyāha muktiṃ kālanivartane / mukterapi nivṛttiḥ syāt saṃsāritvamato bhavet //
[3,2.61]	kva ca pratyakṣataḥ prāptamanumāgamabādhitam / dehātmatvaṃ yadi na tat prāptaṃ pratyakṣataḥ kvacit / mama deha iti hyeva na deho 'hamiti pramā //
[3,2.62]	upacāraśca kṛṣṇo 'hamiti kardamalepane / vastrasya yadvadevaṃ syād yadyupādhikṛtaṃ tadā / svataḥ śuklatvavat kārṣṇyaṃ na mameti pratīyate //
[3,2.63]	kathaṃ ca bhedo dehāderātmano na pramīyate / jātamātrā mṛgā gāvo hastinaḥ pakṣiṇo khaṣāḥ / bhayābhayasvabhogādau kāraṇāni vijānate //
[3,2.64]	asmṛtau pūrvadehasya vijñānaṃ tat kathaṃ bhavet / anvayavyatirekāderanusandhānavismṛtau //
[3,2.65]	yadā dehāntarajñānaṃ dehaikyāvasitiḥ kutaḥ / vyāptatvādātmano dehe vyavahāreṣvapāṭavāt //
[3,2.66]	bhedajñāne 'pi cāṅgāravahnivat svāviviktavat / bhavanti vyavahārāśca na hi pratyakṣagānapi //
[3,2.67]	arthān yathānubhavataḥ pratipādayituṃ kṣamāḥ / lokāstato hi pratyakṣasiddhaṃ nānyena kenacit //
[3,2.68]	śakyaṃ vārayituṃ kvāpi taccennottaragocaram / kathamevottaraḥ kālastadgo mokṣaśca gamyate //
[3,2.69]	āgamo 'pi hi sāmānye siddhe pratyakṣataḥ punaḥ / viśeṣaṃ gamayedeva kathaṃ śaktigraho 'nyathā //
[3,2.70]	atītānāgatārtheṣu jāte śaktigrahe 'khilam / viśeṣaṃ jñāpayed vākyaṃ na tadajñātaśaktike //
[3,2.71]	śaktiśced vartamāne syānnātītānāgataṃ vadet / yadi śaktigraho 'nyatra kathaṃ sa syāt tadagrahe //
[3,2.72]	sāmānyaṃ dṛṣṭamevāsāvanyatra gamayed yadi / sāmānyavarjitaṃ vastusvarūpaṃ gamayet katham //
[3,2.73]	na svarūpatvasāmānyaṃ kenāpyaṅgīkṛtaṃ kvacit / svarūpaṃ cedanugataṃ vyāvṛttaṃ tatra kiṃ bhavet //
[3,2.74]	sarvānugatadharmāṇāmante hi svatvamiṣyate / kiṃ vyāvṛttamiti praśne svarūpamiti kevalam / syāduttaraṃ tato 'nyaccet tadeva svayameva naḥ //
[3,2.75]	evaṃ vyāvṛttarūpe 'pi yadā śaktigraho bhavet / tasya sāmānyato jñānaṃ vinā sa ca bhavet kutaḥ //
[3,2.76]	ato viśeṣasāmānyarūpaṃ sarvamapīṣyate / vyāvṛttaṃ yacca sāmānyaṃ tadeva syād viśeṣataḥ //
[3,2.77]	nacaikadharmatā tena padārthānāṃ parasparam / dharmāṇāṃ bhedadṛṣṭayaiva tatsādṛśyasya darśanāt //
[3,2.78]	ataḥ sarvapadārthāśca sāmānyāt sākṣigocarāḥ / sarvamityeva vijñānaṃ sarveṣāṃ kathamanyathā //
[3,2.79]	kiñcitsādṛśyavijñānādakhilasyāpi vastunaḥ / śabdaśaktigrahaśca syāt tattatsādṛśyamānataḥ //
[3,2.80]	pratyakṣaṃ mānasaṃ caiva yadātītārthagocaram / tadā smṛtipramāṇatvamatītatvaviśeṣitam //
[3,2.81]	ādhikyamanubhūtāttu yadātītatvamiṣyate / mānatā ca kathaṃ na syāt smṛterbādhaśca nātrahi //
[3,2.82]	mānatvaṃ pratyabhijñāyā api sarvānubhūtigam / atītavartamānatvadharmiṇī sā ca dṛśyate //
[3,2.83]	na ca sā smṛtimātrārdhā tadidantvagrahaikataḥ / ato na vatarmānaikaniyamaḥ syād grahe 'kṣaje //
[3,2.84]	na ca pramāṇato 'nyā syāt pramitirnāma kutracit / mānābhāvād gauravācca kalpanāyāḥ kimetayā //
[3,2.85]	mayaitajjñātamiti tu sākṣigaṃ jñānagocaram / jñānameva tato 'nyā na pramitirnāma dṛśyate //
[3,2.86]	mānāmātṛprameyāṇāṃ taducchittirnahi kvacit / svapnānāmapi caiteṣāṃ na bādho dṛśyate kvacit //
[3,2.87]	jāgrattvamātramatraikamanyathā dṛśyate sphuṭam / ato mithyā na ca svapno jāgradvajjāgradeva ca //
[3,2.88]	ātmavat kvacidātmā ca syādeva bhramagocaraḥ / etāvatā na mithyāsau svapne jāgarite tathā //
[3,2.89]	yadyātmanyanyathā dṛśyaṃ bhrāntamatrāpi tad bhavet / abādhitānuvṛttestu svapnāderbhrāntatā kutaḥ //
[3,2.90]	na ca kācit pramā viśvabhrāntatve sarvameva ca / abhrāntatve pramāṇaṃ tu kathaṃ tadbhrāntitā bhavet //
[3,2.91]	kiñca bhrāntatvavādī sa bhrāntatvaṃ svamatasya ca / aṅgīkaroti niyataṃ tatra sampratipannatā / vādinostena cābhrāntaṃ viśvameva bhaviṣyati //
[3,2.92]	bhrāntitvabhrāntatā cet syāt kathaṃ nābhrāntisatyatā / aśeṣadoṣaduṣyaṃ tanmataṃ heyaṃ bubhūṣibhiḥ //
[3,2.93]	yena svamataheyatvaṃ svayamaṅgīkṛtaṃ sadā / bhrāntitvād durghaṭatvasya bhūṣaṇatvācca kevalam //
[3,2.94]	unmatto 'pi kathaṃ tasya mataṃ svīkartumicchati / īśaśakteracintyatvānmahonmattaiḥ pravartitam //
[3,2.95]	ataḥ prajñātra māyoktā jaivyupādānameva sā / nimittamaiśvarī mukhyaṃ nirmitaṃ trātameva ca //
[3,2.96]	tābhyāṃ saha pṛthak caiva māyāmātramitīryate / ubhābhyāṃ mātamaiśvaryā trātaṃ saha pṛthak tataḥ //
[3,2.97]	prajñātmakaṃ mano yena manorūpāśca vāsanāḥ / dhīrbhīriti manastvevetyāha ca śrutirañjasā //
[3,2.98]	cidacinmiśramevaitanmano yāvacca saṃsṛtiḥ / tenāvasthā imāḥ sarvā jīvaḥ paśyati sarvadā //
[3,2.99]	manovikārā viṣayāḥ svāpnā yad bahyavanna te / sthūlā bhavantyatasteṣāṃ spaṣṭatā na tathā kvacit //
[3,2.100]	kvacit spaṣṭā api syuṣye vāsanā mānasī ca sā / īśecchayāntardadhāti vyajyate ca punastayā //
[3,2.101]	sṛṣṭvaiva vāsānabhiśca prapañcaṃ svāpnamīśvaraḥ / vāsanāmātratāṃ tasya nītvāntardhāpayatyajaḥ //
[3,2.102]	suṣuptimohabodhāṃśca svavaśastadvaśaṃ sadā / jīvaṃ nayati deveśo nānyaḥ kartāsya kaścana //
[3,2.103]	na sthānabhedato 'pyasya bhedaḥ kaścit pareśituḥ / sarvatrāśeṣadoṣojkhapūrṇakalyāṇacidguṇaḥ //
[3,2.104]	tadviruddhaṃ tu yat tatra mānaṃ naiva bhavet kvacit / mahātātparyarodhena kathaṃ tanmānamatra tu //
[3,2.105]	duḥkhāpyayasukhāvāptihetutvenaiva vedavāk / bhavenmānaṃ tadīśānāt prasannādeva nānyathā //
[3,2.106]	prasannatā guṇotkarṣajñānādeva hi kevalam / nirdoṣatāparijñānādapi nānyena kenacit //
[3,2.107]	yo māmaśeṣadoṣojkhaṃ guṇasarvasvabṛṃhitam / jānātyasmai prasanno 'haṃ dadyāṃ muktiṃ nacānyathā //
[3,2.108]	yo māmaśeṣābhyadhikaṃ vijānāti sa eva mām / vijānātyakhilāṃstasya dadyāṃ kāmān paraṃ padam //
[3,2.109]	yo māmevamasammūḍhaḥ kiṃ mā nindanti śatravaḥ / ityādivedasmṛtigavākyairevāvasīyate //
[3,2.110]	lokataśca prasādena muktiḥ sa guṇavedanāt / mahātātparyamukhyasya virodhādata eva hi //
[3,2.111]	doṣitvanirguṇatvālpaguṇatvādi kathañcana / nārthaḥ śrutipurāṇādestadviruddho 'khilasya ca / arthaḥ svayaṃ vinirṇīto vāsudevena sādaram //
[3,2.112]	iti guhyatamaṃ śāstramidamuktaṃ mayānagha / etad buddhvā buddhimān syāt kṛtakṛtyaśca bhārata //
[3,2.113]	ityato 'khilasacchāstraviruddhatvena nānumā / vartate tatra teneśo nirṇīto 'khilasadguṇaḥ //
[3,2.114]	na ca cittvādabhinnatvaṃ jīvasyeśavadāpyate / yata ābhāsatāmeva śrutirasya vadatyalam //
[3,2.115]	yathaiṣā puruṣe cchāyā etasminnetadātatam / chāyā yathā puṃsadṛśā pumādhīnā ca dṛśyate / evamevātmakāḥ sarve brahmādyāḥ paramātmanaḥ //
[3,2.116]	sattāpratītikāryeṣu pumadhīno yatheyate / ābhāsa eva puruṣā muktāśca paramātmanaḥ //
[3,2.117]	chāyā viṣṇo ramā tasyāśchāyā dhātā viśeṣakau / tasyendrakāmau ca tayostayoranye 'khilā api //
[3,2.118]	harerbrahmāsya gīstasyā viśeṣāvindra etayoḥ / māraścābhāsakāḥ sarva etayostadadhīnataḥ //
[3,2.119]	sarve 'lpaśaktayaścaiva pūrṇaśaktiḥ paro hariḥ / cetanatve 'pi bhinnāste tasmādetena sarvadā / ityādiśrutivākyebhyo jñāyate bheda eva hi //
[3,2.120]	ābhāsatvaṃ hi nirṇītaṃ jīvasya paramātmanaḥ / tanna yuktaṃ yadābhāsa upādhyāyatta īyate //
[3,2.121]	upādhyāyattatābhāvādābhāsatvavirodhataḥ / cetanatvena cāṃśatvāt samudāyaikyamāpatet //
[3,2.122]	ataḥ pṛthaktavamuditaṃ samudāyāṃśayorbhavet / īśākhyā samudāye syādīśarūpeṣvivoditā //
[3,2.123]	ato dehādyupādhīnāmapāye samatā bhavet / īśarūpairathābhāsā mukhyataḥ sūryakādivat //
[3,2.124]	yadā tadopādhyāyattarūpāṇāṃ nāśitā bhavet / ityāśaṅkānivṛttyarthamāha vedādhipaḥ prabhuḥ / ata evopametyeva cānyābhāsaviśeṣitām //
[3,2.125]	yaduktaṃ tadadhīnatvaṃ sarvāvasthāsvaśeṣataḥ / jīvasya sadṛśatvaṃ ca cittvamātraṃ nacāparam //
[3,2.126]	tāvanmātreṇa cābhāso rūpameṣāṃ cidātmanām / nopādhyadhīnatādyaiśca nātisāmyaṃ nidarśane //
[3,2.127]	kiñcitsukhādisādṛśyamapīśenesurānṛte / tata ābhāsate nityaṃ tadvadābhāsate 'pi ca //
[3,2.128]	bhānamastitvamapicaivāsamantād yatastataḥ / jīva ābhāsa uddiṣṭaḥ sadaiva paramātmanaḥ //
[3,2.129]	na jalāyattasūryādipratibimbopamatvataḥ / tadadhīnatvameveti kiñcit sādṛśyameva ca / samprakāśayataḥ sūtragatāvakhilamānataḥ //
[3,2.130]	jīveśabhedadṛṣṭayaiva samudāyaikatā kutaḥ / aśeṣadoṣarāhityaṃ sarvaśaktitvato hareḥ //
[3,2.131]	sarvopeteti kathitamata aikyaṃ kva doṣiṇā / aśeṣaśaktiyuktaścet svātantryād doṣavān katham //
[3,2.132]	anusandhānarahitamaikyaṃ cedekatā na tat / cetanaikye 'nusandhānaṃ pramāṇaṃ naiva cāparam //
[3,2.133]	anusandhānarahitasamudāyaikyameva cet / cetaneṣvastu tannāmamātrameva yatastataḥ //
[3,2.134]	muktau syādanusandhānaṃ cenmithyājñānitā bhavet / sarvajña ekatāṃ nānusandhatte naiva sā yataḥ //
[3,2.135]	paścāt syādanusandhānaṃ cenmithyājñānitā bhavet / vidyamānānusandhānaṃ na cedajñatvamāpatet //
[3,2.136]	asadaikyaṃ bhavet paścād yadi syāt saptamo rasaḥ / samudāyaikyametasmād dūrato 'pākṛtaṃ sadā //
[3,2.137]	ato 'śeṣaguṇonnaddhaṃ nirdoṣaṃ yāvadeva hi / tāvadeveśvaro nāma tatra bhedo 'pi na kvacit //
[3,2.138]	neha nānāsti kimapi harayo 'yamayaṃ hi saḥ / ityādiśrutimānena jīvāṃśāḥ sarva eva ca //
[3,2.139]	niyamenānusandhānavanto yadyekatā svataḥ / aṃśino 'śeṣasandhānamatyalpasyāpi vidyate //
[3,2.140]	bhuvi jātena cāṃśena sukhaduḥkhādi tadgatam / anubhūyate viśeṣastu kaścidīśakṛto bhavet //
[3,2.141]	īśasyācintyaśaktitvānnāśakyaṃ kvāpi vidyate / seśatānupapannaiva yadi jīvaikatāsya hi / anīśasyeśatetyeva viruddhaṃ sarvamānataḥ //
[3,2.142]	īśatvenaiva vijñātamanīśatvena cecchrutiḥ / anīśatvena vijñātamīśatvenāthavā diśet //
[3,2.143]	upajīvyavirodhena naiva mānatvameṣyati / ata eveśatāsiddherna kiñcicchakyamasya ca //
[3,2.144]	īśatve 'nīśabhedena śrutyā samyak prakāśite / ayuktamapi cānyatra yuktaṃ bhavati tadbalāt //
[3,2.145]	ato 'nyatrāpi yad dṛṣṭaṃ tadīśenaiva kalpyate / śrutyābhāsāptamapi nahīśatvaparipanthi yat //
[3,2.146]	īśo 'nīśo jaganmithyā duḥkhī mukto bhidā na hi / iti pratijñāvyāghātaḥ sarvadoṣādhikādhikaḥ //
[3,2.147]	iti hi brahmatarkoktiratiheyamato 'khilaiḥ / bubhūṣubhirmatamidaṃ jīveśābhedavādinaḥ //
[3,2.148]	nāyuktamīśituḥ kiñcidīśatvasyāvirodhi yat / yadīśitvavirodhi syāt tadevāyuktamañjasā //
[3,2.149]	īśitvasyāvirodhena yojayitvākhilāḥ pramāḥ / siddheśitvena cāyuktamapi hīśe na yojayet //
[3,2.150]	mānataḥ prāptamakhilaṃ nāmānaṃ yojayet kvacit / iti hi brahmatarkoktirato yuktamihoditam //
[3,2.151]	sa cāprākṛtarūpatvādarūpaḥ svaguṇaśatmakam / rūpamasya śiraḥpāṇipādādyātmakamiṣyate //
[3,2.152]	ato nānityatā naiva śrutidvayavirodhitā / yathā hi taijasasyaiva prakāśasyojkhitāvapi / ātmaiva jyotirityāha jīvasyeśaṃ śrutistathā //
[3,2.153]	tadbhaktitāratamyena tāratamyaṃ vimuktigam / brahmādīnāṃ ca sarveṣāmānandāderyathākramam //
[3,2.154]	pratibimbavadapyeṣāmānando 'nyaguṇā yathā / nārāyaṇaguṇādhīnaścātyalpastadapekṣayā //
[3,2.155]	tasmād bhinnaśca satatamanyajjñānaṃ parasya ca / anyajjñānaṃ tu jīvānāmanya ānanda īśatā //
[3,2.156]	mukhyeśatā pareśasya gauṇī jīvasya sā yataḥ / iti śruteḥ sṛṣṭināśau tadadhīnāvitīrite / svabhāvatvāt sthiternaitadapekṣeti na yujyate //
[3,2.157]	yataḥ svabhāvo 'khila īśāyatto 'khilasya ca / avyakto 'pi svaktayaiva bhaktānāṃ dṛśyate hariḥ //
[3,2.158]	tadabhinnā guṇā nityamapi sarve viśeṣataḥ / guṇatvena guṇitvena bhoktṛbhogyatayā sthitāḥ //
[3,2.159]	viśeṣātmatayā teṣāṃ nityaśaktayātmanā tathā / nityasthiterna dharmāṇāṃ kriyādīnāmanityatā //
[3,2.160]	na viśeṣātmatā ceyamanityā śaktirūpatā / saiva yat saviśeṣā syād viśeṣo 'nyo nacāpyayam //
[3,2.161]	svanirvāhakatāhetostathāpi syād viśeṣataḥ / viśeṣatvena vijñāteḥ pramāṇairakhilairapi //
[3,2.162]	sasarja sañjahāreti viśeṣo hyavagamyate / śrutyaiva sa sa eveti tadabhedaśca gamyate //
[3,2.163]	bhedo yadi viśeṣasya sa bhedo bhedinā katham / bhinnaścedanavasthā syādabhinnaścet purā na kim //
[3,2.164]	viśeṣo 'bhinna eveti tena nābhyupagamyate / abhinno nivirśeṣaśced bhedastadbhedatā kutaḥ //
[3,2.165]	anenānena bhinno 'yamiti yat sa viśeṣataḥ / bheda evaiṣa bahudhā dṛśyate tat kimuttaram //
[3,2.166]	abhedabhedayoścaiva svarūpatvaṃ hi bhedinā / tayorapyaviśeṣatve paryāyatvaṃ hi śabdayoḥ //
[3,2.167]	abhedabhedaśabdau ca paryāyāviti ko vadet / bhedo 'nyonyamabhedaśca bhedinā ced viśeṣatā //
[3,2.168]	nirviśeṣe kathaṃ bhedo bhedinaikastathābhidā / punastayorvibhedaśca bhedimātratvato bhavet //
[3,2.169]	bhedinaścaiva bhedasya viśeṣo yadi gamyate / abhedābhedinoścaiva kiṃ bhedo 'bhedabhedayoḥ //
[3,2.170]	viśeṣeṇaiva sarvatra yadi vyavahṛtirbhavet / kalpanāgauravāyaiva kiṃ bhedaḥ kalpyate tadā //
[3,2.171]	aikyapratītyabhāvena bheda eva gavaśvayoḥ / sa eveti pratītau hi viśeṣo nāma bhaṇyate //
[3,2.172]	saccidāderaparyāyasiddhayarthaṃ māyināpi hi / aṅgīkāryo viśeṣo 'yaṃ yadyasatyaviśeṣaṇam / pṛthak pṛthag vārayituṃ śabdāntaramitīṣyate //
[3,2.173]	māyāviśeṣarāhityaviśeṣeṇa viśeṣitā / satyasyāpi bhavet sā ca tathā cedanavasthitiḥ //
[3,2.174]	yadi satye viśeṣo na na taduktirbhavet tadā / lakṣyate cet tena lakṣyamityapi syād viśeṣitā //
[3,2.175]	punaḥpunarlakṣaṇāyāmapi syādanavasthitiḥ / yadyabhāvaviśeṣitvaṃ syādaṅgīkṛtameva te //
[3,2.176]	asārvajñyādirāhityamapyevaṃ te bhaviṣyati / tadā sārvajñyameva syād bhāvārthatvānnañordvayoḥ //
[3,2.177]	yadi naitādṛśaṃ grāhyamasukhatvānivartanāt / asattvajñānatādeśca syādasattvādikaṃ tadā //
[3,2.178]	anṛtādivirodhitvaṃ yadyasyābhyupagamyate / anaiśvaryavirodhitvamapyevaṃ kiṃ nivāryate //
[3,2.179]	akhaṇḍakhaṇḍanādevaṃ viśeṣo'khaṇḍavādinā / khaṇḍitenāpi manasā svīkāryo'nanyathāgateḥ //
[3,2.180]	akhaṇḍakhaṇḍavādibhyāṃ khaṇḍākhaṇḍena caiva tat / mahādareṇa śirasi viśeṣo dhārya eva hi //
[3,2.181]	nidarśanatrayeṇāto bhagavānatyabhinnatām / guṇānāmādareṇāha tacca nābhihitānvayaḥ //
[3,2.182]	yadāśeṣaviśeṣāṇamuktiḥ sāmānyato bhavet / padaikenāpyuttareṇa viśeṣāvagatirbhavet //
[3,2.183]	yato 'śeṣaviśeṣāṇāṃ vastunāstyeva caikatā / ataḥ sāmānyato jñātaḥ padāntarabalāt punaḥ / bhaved viśeṣato jñānastena syādanvitoktitā //
[3,2.184]	svārtha evānvito yasmāt kenacit tadviśeṣataḥ / aneneti taduktayaiva jñāyate 'nubhavena hi //
[3,2.185]	yadyananvitamevaitat padaṃ svārthaṃ vadediha / tathānyānyapi sarvāṇi kaḥ kuryādanvayaṃ punaḥ //
[3,2.186]	vyāpāro na hi śabdasya paraḥ svārthaprakāśanāt / pumānapyekavāroktayā kṛtakṛtyo yadā bhavet //
[3,2.187]	anvayasya kathaṃ jñānaṃ śabdārthatvaṃ yadāsya na / yadaivānanvitārthasya vacanaṃ taiḥ padaibharvet //
[3,2.188]	ananvitaḥ syācchabdārtho na tadartho hi so 'nvayaḥ / nirākāṅkṣapadānyeva vākyamityucyate budhaiḥ //
[3,2.189]	tattadarthābhidhānena syānnirākāṅkṣatā ca sā //
[3,2.190]	apūrtestāvadarthānāmākāṅkṣā pūrvamiṣyate / karmakartṛkriyāṇāṃ tu pūrtau ko 'nyo 'nvayo bhavet //
[3,2.191]	apūrtiścet padairuktaiḥ kiṃ nṛśṛṅgeṇa pūryate / vyāpāraścet punasteṣāmanuktāvapi kiṃ na saḥ //
[3,2.192]	ukte buddhisthatāhetoryadi vyāpāra iṣyate / buddhisthatvāya yatnaṃ na kathaṃ kuryuḥ puraiva ca / puruṣādhīnatā teṣāṃ yadi paścācca sā samā //
[3,2.193]	pumānevānvayāyaiṣāṃ paścād yadi viceṣyate / ananvitābhidhānānāṃ sa evārthāntaroktiṣu / yatatāṃ śabdaśaktiścet tatra naivānvaye katham //
[3,2.194]	tatkalpanāgurutvādidoṣeto 'bhihitānvayaḥ / anubhūtiviruddhaśca tyājya eva manīṣibhiḥ //
[3,2.195]	kartṛśabde hyabhihite dharmasāmānyavedanāt / viśeṣadharmamanvicchan kimityeva hi pṛcchati //
[3,2.196]	guṇakriyādidharmāṇāṃ viśeṣe kathite punaḥ / nirākāṅkṣo bhaved yasmācchabdā anvitavācakāḥ //
[3,2.197]	ato 'nantaguṇātmaiko bhagavāneka eva tu / ucyate sarvavedaiśca te cākhilavilakṣaṇāḥ //
[3,2.198]	sarve sarvaguṇātmānaḥ sarvakartāra eva ca / tathāpi saviśeṣāśca vidvadyvutpattito 'pica //
[3,2.199]	taistaiḥ śabdaiśca bhaṇyante yujyate copadeśataḥ / anyānandādisādṛśyamānukūlyādinā param //
[3,2.200]	pūrṇatvādi mahat teṣāṃ vailakṣaṇyaṃ śrutau śrutam / pūrṇe 'śeṣaniyantā ca sukhādutama ekakalaḥ //
[3,2.201]	guṇorusamudāyo 'yaṃ vāsudevaḥ sa niṣkaḷaḥ / vāsudevaśrutiḥ saiṣā guṇān vakti hareḥ parān //
[3,2.202]	sa evāśeṣajīvasthanissaṅkhayānādikālikān / dharmādharmān sadā paśyan svecchayā bodhayatyajaḥ //
[3,2.203]	kāṃścit teṣāṃ phalaṃ caiva dadāti svayamacyutaḥ / na te viśeṣaṃ kamapi preraṇādikamucyate / kuryuḥ kadāpi tenāyaṃ svatantro 'nupacārataḥ //
[3,2.204]	karmāṇi tāni ca pṛthak cetanānyeva sarvaśaḥ / acetanaśarīrāṇi svakarmaphalabhāñci ca //
[3,2.205]	pratyekaṃ teṣu cānantakarmāṇyevaṃvidhāni ca / tāni caivamitīśasya nissīmā śaktiruttamā //
[3,2.206]	ekaiva brahmahatyā hi varāhahariṇoditā / brahmapārastavenaiva niṣkrāntā rājadehataḥ //
[3,2.207]	stotrasya tasya māhātmyād vyādhatvaṃ gamitā punaḥ / prāpya jñānaṃ paraṃ cāpa tathānyānyapi sarvadā //
[3,2.208]	anantānyuditānyevaṃ prabhuṇā kapilena hi / saṃsāre pacyamānāni karmāṇyapi pṛthak pṛthak //
[3,2.209]	tasmādanantamāhātmyaguṇapūgo janārdanaḥ / bhaktyā paramayā'rādhya iti pādārtha īryate //
<iti śrīmadānandatīrthabhagavatpādācāryaviracite śrīmadbrahmasūtrānuvyākhyāne tṛtīyādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ ||>
{3,3}
[3,3.1]	vairāgyato bhaktidārḍhyaṃ tenopāsā yadā bhavet / āparokṣyaṃ bhaved viṣṇoriti pādakramo bhavet //
[3,3.2]	yuktito jñātavedārtho nirasya samayān parān / parasparavirodhaṃ ca praṇudyāśeṣavākyagam //
[3,3.3]	adhyātmapraṇavo bhūtvā tasya sannihitatvataḥ / bahuyuktivirodhānāṃ bhānāt tatsahitaśruteḥ //
[3,3.4]	virodhaṃ ca nirākṛtya śrutīnāṃ prāṇatastvagān / parihṛtya virodhāṃśca tatprasādānurañjitaḥ //
[3,3.5]	dehakartṛtvamīśasya jñātvā tatpitṛtāsmṛteḥ / viśeṣasnehamāpādya sarvakartṛtvato 'dhikam //
[3,3.6]	niṣpādya bahumānaṃ ca tadanyatrātiduḥkhataḥ / utpādyādhikavairāgyaṃ tadguṇādhikyavedanāt //
[3,3.7]	sarvasya tadvaśatvācca dārḍhyaṃ bhakteravāpya ca / yatetopāsanāyaiva viśiṣṭācāryasampadā //
[3,3.8]	kartavyā brahmajijñāsetyukte kimiti saṃśaye / ata ityudite 'pyasya viśeṣānuktitaḥ punaḥ //
[3,3.9]	sṛṣṭibandhanamokṣādikartṛtvasya śrutatvataḥ / yato mokṣādidātāsāvato jijñāsya eva vaḥ / ityāha tat paraṃ brahma vyāsākhyaṃ jñānaraśmimat //
[3,3.10]	yenaiva bandhamokṣaḥ syāt sa ca jijñāsayā gataḥ / suprasanno bhavedīśo jijñāsāto 'sya muktidā //
[3,3.11]	mokṣādidatvamīśasya kathamevāvagamyate / iti cecchāstrayonitvācchāstragamyo hi mokṣadaḥ //
[3,3.12]	pratyakṣāvasitebhyaḥ syād yadi mokṣaḥ kathañcana / kimityanādisaṃsāramagnāḥ sarvā imāḥ prajāḥ //
[3,3.13]	yasmānniyamato duḥkhahāniḥ pratyakṣato bhavet / dhāvantyeva tamuddiśya rājādyamakhilāḥ prajāḥ //
[3,3.14]	anumānagamyato mokṣo yadi tasyānumaiva hi / dṛṣṭapūruṣavanmokṣadātṛtāṃ vinivārayet //
[3,3.15]	tacchāstragamya evaiko mokṣado bhavati dhruvam / śāstragamyaśca nānyo 'sti mokṣadatvena keśavāt //
[3,3.16]	mokṣado hi svatantraḥ syāt paratantraḥ svayaṃ sṛtau / vartamānaḥ kathaṃ śaktaḥ paramokṣāya kevalam //
[3,3.17]	anyāśrayeṇa yadyeṣa dadyānmokṣaṃ sa eva hi / tenānanusṛto mokṣaṃ na dadyādanyavākyataḥ / atastadarthamapi sa jñeyo viṣṇurmumukṣibhiḥ //
[3,3.18]	yamevaiṣa iti śrutyā tameveti ca sādaram / śāstrayonitvamasyaiva jñāyate vedavādibhiḥ //
[3,3.19]	ya enaṃ viduramṛtā ityuktastu samudragaḥ / tadeva brahma paramamiti śrutyāvadhāritaḥ //
[3,3.20]	yataḥ prasūteti tataḥ sṛṣṭimāha tato hariḥ / śāstrayonirnacānyo 'sti mukhyatastviti gamyate //
[3,3.21]	śāstrayonitvametasya jñāyate hi samanvayāt / samiti hyupasargeṇa paramukhyāthartocyate //
[3,3.22]	evaṃ paramamukhyārtho nārāyaṇa iti śruteḥ / nirdhāraṇāya nāśabdamiti vedapatirjagau //
[3,3.23]	kathaṃ samanvayo jñeyaḥ svalpaśākhāvidāṃ nṛṇām / vedā hyanantā iti hi śrutirāhāpyanantatām //
[3,3.24]	anantavedanirṇītirmahāpraḷayavāridheḥ / uttāraṇopametyasmānna jñeyo 'tra samanvayaḥ //
[3,3.25]	iti śaṅkāpanodārthaṃ sa āha karuṇākaraḥ / aśakyottaraṇatve 'pi hyāgamāpāravāridheḥ / nirṇīyate mayaivāyaṃ romakūpalayodinā //
[3,3.26]	yadyapyaśeṣavedārtho durgamo 'khilamānavaiḥ / majjñānāvyākṛtākāśe prāpnoti paramāṇutām //
[3,3.27]	iti prakāśayan viśvapatirāha prameyatām / nikhilasyāpi vedasya gatisāmānyamañjasā //
[3,3.28]	ko nāma gatisāmānyamanantāgamasampadaḥ / jñānasūryamṛte brūyāt tamekaṃ bādarāyaṇam //
[3,3.29]	anyo 'pyalpamatiḥ śākhācatuṣpañcagataṃ vasu / jānannānumitatvena brūyāt tasya prasādataḥ //
[3,3.30]	iti mukhyatayāśeṣagatisāmānyavit prabhuḥ / pratijajñe dṛḍhaṃ yasmād devānāmapi pūryate //
[3,3.31]	ato nikhilavedānāṃ siddha evaṃ samanvayaḥ / iti sujñāpitārtho 'pi pṛthak cāha samanvayam //
[3,3.32]	tatra prathamato 'nyatra prasiddhānāṃ samanvayaḥ / śabdānāṃ vācya evātra mahāmalleśabhaṅgavat //
[3,3.33]	ito 'tyabhyadhikatve 'pi turyapādoditasya tu / mahāsamanvaye tasmin nādhikāro 'khilasya hi //
[3,3.34]	brahmaivādhikṛtastatra mukhyato 'nye yathākramam / durgamatvācca naivātra prāthamyenodito 'ñjasā //
[3,3.35]	ato 'nyatra prasiddhānāṃ śabdānāṃ nirṇayāya tu / pravṛttaḥ prathamaṃ devastatrānandādayo guṇāḥ / īśasyaiveti nirṇītāḥ śrutiyuktisamāśrayāt //
[3,3.36]	devatāntaragāḥ sarve śabdavṛttinimittataḥ / viṣṇumeva vadantyaddhā tatsaṅgādupacārataḥ //
[3,3.37]	anyadevān vadantīha viśeṣaguṇavaktṛtaḥ / viṣṇumeva paraṃ brūyurevamanye 'pyaśeṣataḥ //
[3,3.38]	ityanyatraprasiddhoruśabdarāśeraśeṣataḥ / jñāte samanvaye viṣṇau liṅgairhyeṣa samanvayaḥ //
[3,3.39]	teṣāmanyagatatve tu na syāt samyak samanvayaḥ / ityevāśeṣaliṅgānāṃ brahmaṇyeva samanvayam //
[3,3.40]	āhobhayagatatvaṃ ca syādato liṅgaśabdayoḥ / iti saṃśayanuttyarthamubhayatra pratītitaḥ //
[3,3.41]	śabdānāṃ vartamānānāṃ saliṅgānāṃ viśeṣataḥ / samanvayo harāveva yannaivānyatra mukhyataḥ //
[3,3.42]	śabdā liṅgāni ca yato naivānyatra svatantratā / asvatantreṣu śabdasya vṛttiheturna mukhyataḥ //
[3,3.43]	yato 'to yadadhīnāste śabdārthatvamupāgatāḥ / atyalpenaiva śabdasya vṛttihetuguṇena tu //
[3,3.44]	ayo yathā dāhakatvaṃ sa eveśaḥ svatantrataḥ / mukhyaśabdārtha iti hi svīkartavyo manīṣibhiḥ //
[3,3.45]	ityāhaivañca śabdānāṃ nārāyaṇasamanvaye / siddhe 'pyaśeṣaśabdānāṃ na kathañcana yujyate //
[3,3.46]	virodhāvavaratvāderapi prāptiryato bhavet / iti cedavaratvādi dvividhaṃ hyupalabhyate //
[3,3.47]	parasyāvaratāheturyaḥ svayaṃ para eva san / so 'pi hyavaraśabdārtho yathā rājā jayī bhavet //
[3,3.48]	anyo 'varatvānubhavī tayoḥ pūrvo 'sti keśave / dvitīyo jīva evāsti svātantrānnaca dūṣaṇam //
[3,3.49]	harerevamaśeṣeṇa sarvaśabdasamanvaye / ukte virodhahīnasya syāt samanvayatā yataḥ / ato 'śeṣavirodhānāṃ kṛteśena nirākṛtiḥ //
[3,3.50]	samanvayāvirodhābhyāṃ sañjāte vastunirṇaye / kiṃ mayā kāryamityeva syād buddhiradhikāriṇaḥ //
[3,3.51]	tatra bhaktividhānārthamabhaktānarthasantatau / uktāyāṃ bhaktidārḍhyāya prokte 'śeṣaguṇoccaye / vaktavyopāsanā nityaṃ kartavyetyādareṇa hi //
[3,3.52]	sopāsanā ca dvividhā śāstrābhyāsasvarūpiṇī / dhyānarūpā parā caiva tadaṅgaṃ dhāraṇādikam //
[3,3.53]	tathobhayātmakaṃ caiva pāde 'smin bādarāyaṇaḥ / āhopāsanamaddhava vistarācchrutipūrvakam //
[3,3.54]	pṛthagdṛṣṭiraśakyatvamanirṇītiḥ samuccayaḥ / viśeṣadarśanaṃ kāryalopo nānoktirāśutā //
[3,3.55]	vibhramo 'pākṛtirliṅgamanavasthāviśeṣitā / aprayojanatā cātiprasaṅgo 'dūrasaṃśrayaḥ //
[3,3.56]	viśiṣṭakāraṇaṃ ceṣyā dṛṣṭavairūpyamunnatiḥ / anuktiraprayatnatvaṃ dṛḍhabandhaparābhavau //
[3,3.57]	puṃsāmyaṃ prāptasantyāgaḥ kāraṇānirṇayo bhramaḥ / viśeṣadarśitā'lāpo guṇasāmyaṃ pṛthagdṛśiḥ //
[3,3.58]	agamyavartma sandhānamiṣṭaṃ phalamakalpanā / śuddhavairūpyamaṅgatvamaviśeṣadṛśiḥ kriyā //
[3,3.59]	yuktayaḥ pūrvapakṣasthāḥ sujñeyatvaṃ vidhikriyā / māhātmyamalpaśaktitvaṃ yathāyogyaphalaṃ bhavaḥ //
[3,3.60]	phalasāmyaṃ viśeṣaśca guṇādhikyaṃ pradhānatā / yathāśaktikriyā sandhiḥ pramāṇabalamānatiḥ //
[3,3.61]	kāraṇaṃ kāryavaiśeṣyaṃ svabhāvo vastudūṣaṇam / pratikriyāvirodhaśca pratisandhiranūnatā //
[3,3.62]	saṃskārapāṭavaṃ svecchāniyatirvastuvaibhavam / viśeṣoktiramānatvaṃ prādhānyaṃ prītirāgamaḥ //
[3,3.63]	susthiratvaṃ kṛtaprāptiranādiguṇavistaraḥ / sādhanottamatā nānādṛṣṭiḥ śiṣṭiranūnatā //
[3,3.64]	avighnatvavirodhau ca guṇavaiśeṣyamāgamaḥ / siddhāntanirṇaye hyetā yuktayo 'vyāhatāḥ sadā //
[3,3.65]	yathāśaktayakhilān vedān vijñāyopāsanaṃ bhavet / tatrākhilasya vijñaptiḥ samyag brahmaṇa eva hi //
[3,3.66]	tadanyeṣāṃ yathāyogyamakhilajñaptiriṣyate / tāvatopāsane yogyo bhavedevākhilaḥ pumān //
[3,3.67]	mahattvasya paraṃ pāraṃ viditvaiva janārdanaḥ / stoṣyatāmeti tuṣṭatvamiti nāstyeva nārada //
[3,3.68]	kintu niścalayā bhaktayā hyātmajñānānurūpataḥ / yaḥ stoṣyati sadā bhaktastuṣyastasya sadā hariḥ //
[3,3.69]	ityādivākyasandarbhād yathāyogyākhilajñatā / ātmajñānānurūpatvaṃ yathāśakti vicāraṇāt //
[3,3.70]	vedaḥ kṛtsno 'dhigantavyaḥ svādhyāyādhyayanaṃ bhavet / ityādivākyavaiyarthyamanyathā na nivāryate //
[3,3.71]	adyāpi tena devādyāḥ śṛṇvate manvate sadā / dhyāyanti ca yathāyogaṃ tathāpyā vastunirṇayāt / śravaṇaṃ mananaṃ caiva kartavyaṃ sarvathaiva hi //
[3,3.72]	matiśrutidhyānakālaviśeṣaṃ gururuttamaḥ / vetti tasyoktimārgeṇa kurvataḥ syāddhi darśanam //
[3,3.73]	śravaṇaṃ dṛṣṭatattvasya mananaṃ dhyānameva ca / viśeṣānandasamprāptyā anyasyaitāni dṛṣṭaye //
[3,3.74]	yadi tādṛg gururnāsti nirṇītaśravaṇādikam / tatsiddhāntānusāreṇa nirṇayajñāt samācaret //
[3,3.75]	śravaṇādi vinā naiva kṣaṇaṃ tiṣṭhedapi kvacit / atyaśakye tu nidrādau punareva samārabhet //
[3,3.76]	abhāve nirṇayajñasya sacchāstrāṇyeva sarvadā / śṛṇuyād yadi sajjñānaprācuryamupalabhyate //
[3,3.77]	mahadbhayo viṣṇubhaktebhyo yathāśakti ca saṃśayān / chindyāt svato 'dhikābhāve svayameva samabhyaset //
[3,3.78]	aśeṣaguṇapūrṇatvaṃ sarvadoṣasamujkhitiḥ / viṣṇoranyacca tattantramiti samyag vinirṇayaḥ //
[3,3.79]	svatantratvaṃ sadā tasya tasya bhedaśca sarvataḥ / adoṣatvasya siddhayarthaṃ yadabhede tadanvayaḥ //
[3,3.80]	tattantratvaṃ ca muktānāmapi tadguṇapūrtaye / muktānāmapi bhedaśca na hi bhinnamabhinnatām / gacchad dṛṣṭaṃ kvacit tasyāpyabhāvo 'nubhavopagaḥ //
[3,3.81]	pūrvābhede doṣavattvamīśasyetyatibhinnatā / nārāyaṇena muktānāmapi samyagiti sthitiḥ //
[3,3.82]	bhedābhede 'pyabhedena doṣāṇāmapi sambhavaḥ / nirdoṣatvaṃ ramāyāśca tadanantaratā tathā //
[3,3.83]	brahmā sarasvatī vīndraśeṣarudrāśca tatsriyaḥ / śakrakāmau tadanye ca kramānmuktāvapīti ca //
[3,3.84]	satsiddhānta iti jñeyo nirṇīto hariṇā svayam / etadvirodhi yat sarvaṃ tamase 'ndhāya kevalam //
[3,3.85]	andhaṃ tamo viśantīti prāha śrutiratisphuṭam / ityeva śrutayo 'śeṣāḥ pañcarātramathākhilam //
[3,3.86]	mūlarāmāyaṇaṃ caiva bhārataṃ smṛtayo 'khilāḥ / vaiṣṇavāni purāṇāni sāṅkhayayogau parāvapi //
[3,3.87]	brahmatarkaśca mīmāṃsetyanantaḥ śabdasāgaraḥ / anantara yuktayaścaiva pratyakṣāgamamūlakāḥ //
[3,3.88]	pratyakṣamaiśvaraṃ caiva ramādīnāmaśeṣataḥ / muktānāmapyamuktānāmetamevārthamuttamam //
[3,3.89]	anyāvakāśarahitaṃ prakāśayati sādaram / etadeva ca sacchāstraṃ duḥśāstraṃ tu tataḥ param //
[3,3.90]	sacchāstramabhyasennityaṃ duḥśāstraṃ ca parityajet / asaṃśayena tattvasya nirṇaye brahmadarśanam //
[3,3.91]	samyagviṣamavijñānatāratamyānusārataḥ / phalaṃ bhavet tāratamyāt sukhaduḥkhātmakaṃ nṛṇām //
[3,3.92]	samyak cādhikavijñānāt sukhādhikyaṃ bhavennṛṇām / ato yathātmaśaktayaiva śravaṇaṃ mananaṃ tathā //
[3,3.93]	viṣayeṣu ca saṃsargācchāśvatasya ca saṃśayāt / manasā cānyadākāṅkṣāt paraṃ na pratipādyate //
[3,3.94]	iti bhāratavākyaṃ hi tenaitaddoṣavarjitaḥ / sadopāsanayā yukto vāsudevaṃ prapaśyati //
[3,3.95]	doṣā anādisambaddhāste muktiparipanthinaḥ / santyeva prāyaśaḥ puṃsu tena mokṣo na jāyate //
[3,3.96]	sarve ta ete jīveṣu dṛśyante tāratamyataḥ / ṛjūnāmeka evāsti paramotsāhavarjanam / sa guṇālpatvamātratvānnarjatvena viruddhayate //
[3,3.97]	ato viṣṇau parā bhaktistadbhakteṣu ramādiṣu / tāratamyena kartavyā puruṣārthamabhīpsitā //
[3,3.98]	svādaraḥ sarvajantūnāṃ saṃsiddho hi svabhāvataḥ / tato 'dhikaḥ svottameṣu tadādhikyānusārataḥ //
[3,3.99]	kartavyo vāsudevāntaṃ sarvathā śubhamicchatā / na kadācit tyajet taṃ ca krameṇainaṃ vivardhayet //
[3,3.100]	sameṣu svātmavat snehaḥ satsvanyatra tato dayā / kāryaivamāparokṣyeṇa dṛśyate kṣipramīśvaraḥ //
[3,3.101]	tat tamo 'ndhaṃ vrajed viṣṇusamatvaṃ yo 'nupaśyati / ramābrahmaśivādīnāmapi muktau kathañcana //
[3,3.102]	kimutādhikyadṛṣṭestad guṇābhāvamaterapi / doṣavetturabhedasya draṣṭurdraṣṭustathobhayoḥ //
[3,3.103]	ityāha sacchrutistena samproktaguṇasaṃyutam / upāsīta hariṃ dṛṣṭvā muktistenaiva jāyate //
[3,3.104]	dveṣād yanmuktikathanaṃ śrutivākyavirodhi yat / ripavo ye tu rāmasya vimukhatvānnirāmiṇaḥ / abhidrohapade nityamandhe tamasi te sthitāḥ //
[3,3.105]	haridviṣastamo yānti ye caiva tadabhedinaḥ / tannirguṇatvavettārastasya doṣavido 'pi ca //
[3,3.106]	ityādiśrutisandarbhād dveṣiṇastama īyate / hiraṇyakaśipuścāpi bhagavannindayā tamaḥ / vidhikṣuratyagāt sūno prahlādasyānubhāvataḥ //
[3,3.107]	yadanindat pitā mahyaṃ tvadbhakte mayi cāghavān / tasmāt pitā me pūyeta durantād dustarādaghāt //
[3,3.108]	nindāṃ bhagavataḥ śṛṇvaṃstatparasya janasya vā / tato nāpaiti yaḥ so 'pi yātyaghaḥ sukṛtāccyutaḥ //
[3,3.109]	avajānanti māṃ mūḍhā mānuṣīṃ tanumāśritam / paraṃ bhāvamajānanto mama bhūtamaheśvaram //
[3,3.110]	moghāśā moghakarmāṇo moghajñānā vicetasaḥ / rākṣasīmāsurīṃ caiva prakṛtiṃ mohanīṃ śritāḥ //
[3,3.111]	māmātmaparadeheṣu pradviṣanto 'bhyasūyakāḥ / tānahaṃ dviṣataḥ krūrān saṃsāreṣu narādhamān / kṣipāmyajasramaśubhānāsurīṣveva yoniṣu //
[3,3.112]	āsurīṃ yonimāpannā mūḍhā janmani janmani / māmaprāpyaiva kaunteya tato yāntyadhamāṃ gatim //
[3,3.113]	yo dviṣṭād vibudhaśreṣṭhaṃ devaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ prabhum / kathaṃ sa na bhaved dveṣya ālokāntasya kasyacit //
[3,3.114]	yo dviṣṭād vibudhaśreṣṭhaṃ devaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ prabhum / majjanti pitarastasya narake śāśvatīḥ samāḥ / ityādivākyasandohād dveṣiṇastama eva tu //
[3,3.115]	naiva mokṣa iti prāhurlokāyatamate sthitāḥ / bhogaḥ śarīraparyantaṃ bhasmībhāvastato bhavet //
[3,3.116]	iti tat kena mānena dṛṣṭaṃ pratyakṣavādinā / na hi pratyakṣamānena mokṣābhāvo 'vasīyate //
[3,3.117]	ghaṭate muktidṛṣṭistu puruṣeṇa mahīyasā / neti vakturmahattvaṃ tu kathañcana na vidyate //
[3,3.118]	sādhayan sarvasāmānyaṃ kathameva viśeṣavān / dṛśyante puruṣā loke parāvaravido 'pica //
[3,3.119]	aparokṣadṛśo yoganiṣṭhāścāmalacakṣuṣaḥ / pratyakṣaṃ devatāṃ dṛṣṭvā tatprasādāptabhūtayaḥ //
[3,3.120]	jñānavijñānapārajñā niṣiddhayante kathaṃ nṛbhiḥ / dṛśyate cātimāhātmyaṃ teṣāmatimahaujasām //
[3,3.121]	yadi te 'pi niṣiddhayante kiṃ noktiste niṣiddhayate / yaduktavākyaprāmāṇyaṃ pratyakṣeṇopalabhyate //
[3,3.122]	varādayo 'pi taddattāḥ sadā satyā bhavanti hi / aprāmāṇyaṃ tadukteśca vṛthāvācāvasīyate //
[3,3.123]	na hi prayojanaṃ kiñcit paralokanivāraṇāt / vṛthāvācaṃ vṛthā hanyād yadi tasya kimuttaram / svajīvanavirodhāya vadan kiṃ nāma buddhimān //
[3,3.124]	prāmāṇye saṃśayaḥ kiṃ syāt tayoḥ puruṣayorapi / svajīvanaviruddhoktirajño dṛṣṭasya cāpi saḥ //
[3,3.125]	yaścātīndriyadevoktiśrotā dṛṣṭaparāvaraḥ / atītānāgataṃ sarvaṃ lokānubhavamāpayan / ataḥ pratyakṣagamyatvād vedamātvasya ca sphuṭam //
[3,3.126]	yadyāgamasya no mātvamakṣajasya tathā bhavet / yadyakṣajasya mātvaṃ syādāgamasya kathaṃ na tat / lokavākyād viśeṣaścāvyabhicāreṇa siddhayati //
[3,3.127]	asti mokṣo 'pi dharmeṇa yathārthajñānato 'pi ca / prāmāṇyamanumāyāśca jinasyāptatvasādhane //
[3,3.128]	tadvākyād dharmasajjñānavijñaptirbhavatīti ca / dharmo 'hiṃsāparo nānyo jñānaṃ pudgaladarśanam //
[3,3.129]	iti jaināḥ kathaṃ tat syāt pramāṇamanumānataḥ / viṣayān prati sthitaṃ hyakṣaṃ pratyakṣamiti gīyate / pratyakṣaśabdānusārādanumeti prakītirtā //
[3,3.130]	ā samantād gamayati dharmādharmau paraṃ padam / yaccāpyatīndriyaṃ tvanyat tenāsāvāgamaḥ smṛtaḥ //
[3,3.131]	etena kāreṇenaiva tattanmānatvamiṣyate / svarūpaṃ hi tadeteṣāmanyathāsiddhimānataḥ //
[3,3.132]	ato 'numā kathaṃ dharmaṃ pudgalaṃ cāpi darśayet / svarūpaṃ pudgalasyoktā doṣā ānandameva ca / na manyate pudgalaṃ sa duḥkhābhāvaḥ sukhaṃ tviti //
[3,3.133]	mātrābhogātirekeṇa sukhādhikyasya darśanāt / sukhasyābhāvatā kena na ca syāt kiṃ viparyayaḥ //
[3,3.134]	yadi bhāvo 'pi kaścit syāt tasyaivābhāvatā kutaḥ / yadi sarve 'pyabhāvāḥ syuranyonyamiti bhāvatā //
[3,3.135]	abhāvābhāvatā yat syāt kiṃ naśchinnaṃ tadā bhavet / bhāvatvaṃ vidhirūpatvaṃ niṣedhatvamabhāvatā //
[3,3.136]	niṣedhasya niṣedho 'pi bhāva eva balād bhavet / prathamapratipattistu bhāvabhāvaniyāmikā //
[3,3.137]	na ca pudgalavijñānaṃ mokṣadaṃ bhavati kvacit / asvātantryāt pudgalasya jñāto 'pi sukhado na hi //
[3,3.138]	na hi duḥkhiparijñānād duḥkhitvaṃ vinivartate / yadi pudgalavijñānādaduḥkhī syāt kathañcana / dehavānapi nāduḥkhī kiṃ jñānāduttaraṃ sadā //
[3,3.139]	īśakḷptyanusāreṇa syāt kālādīśavādinaḥ / karmahetutvamapi tu niścaitanyānnahi kvacit //
[3,3.140]	aśeṣaduḥkhavilaye nedānīṃ kāraṇaṃ yathā / tathottaraṃ ca naiva syād dṛṣṭipūrvānumā yataḥ //
[3,3.141]	śaktasyānyasya vijñānaṃ tatprītijanakaṃ yadi / tayaiva bandhahāniḥ syāditi kiṃ nāma dūṣaṇam //
[3,3.142]	svajñānād bandhahānistu dṛśyate kasya kutracit / ahiṃsāyāśca dharmatvaṃ kena mānena gamyate / hiṃsāyā eva dharmatvamityukte syāt kimuttaram //
[3,3.143]	dharmasya sukhahetutvamapi kenāvagamyate / hatyayā mokṣahetutvaṃ kuto mānānnivāryate //
[3,3.144]	na ca śūnyaparijñānācchūnyabhāvanayāpi ca / mokṣaḥ kathañcana bhaved yadīdānīṃ kathaṃ na saḥ //
[3,3.145]	paraprasādanecchostu viḷambo nāma yujyate / pumicchādhīnatā no ced viḷambaḥ kiṅkṛto bhavet //
[3,3.146]	anyatrāpi viḷambāstu syurīśecchānimittataḥ / anyathā kāraṇaṃ cet syāt kiṃ kāryaṃ nopajāyate / kāraṇe sati kāryasya bhāvaḥ suniyato 'sya hi //
[3,3.147]	vijñānavādinaścaiva vijñānādvaitavedanāt / vijñānabhāvanāccaiva mokṣo na ghaṭate kvacit //
[3,3.148]	antarjñānasya bāhye ca kṣaṇikatvasya vedanāt / bhāvanāccoktamārgeṇa mānābhāvānna mucyate //
[3,3.149]	prakṛteḥ puruṣasyāpi viveko muktisādhanam / iti śaṅkayā na caitasmin mānamīśāprasādataḥ //
[3,3.150]	śrutayaḥ smṛtayaścaiva yadīśasya prasādataḥ / vadanti niyamānmuktiṃ tamṛte 'taḥ kuto bhavet //
[3,3.151]	kaṇādayogākṣapādā apīśasya prasādataḥ / muktiṃ bruvāṇā apyāhurbhogādeva ca karmaṇām / kṣayaṃ prāhuḥ kutaścaitat prasanne jagadīśvare //
[3,3.152]	bhidyate hṛdayagranthiśchidyante sarvasaṃśayāḥ / kṣīyante cāsya karmāṇi tasmin dṛṣṭe parāvare //
[3,3.153]	bhidyate hṛdayagranthiśchidyante sarvasaṃśayāḥ / kṣīyante cāsya karmāṇi dṛṣṭa evātmanīśvare / iti śrutipurāṇādivacanebhyo 'nyathāgateḥ //
[3,3.154]	na ca pāśupatādyuktaśivādīnāmanugrahāt / nānyaḥ panthā iti hyuktaṃ puruṣajñānataḥ śrutau //
[3,3.155]	sarve nimeṣā jajñire vidyutaḥ puruṣādataḥ / evaṃ puruṣaśabdaśca prayukto 'bdhiśaye harau //
[3,3.156]	na tasyeśe kaścana tasya nāma mahad yaśaḥ / iti cādhipatistasya pratiṣiddhaḥ svayaṃ śrutau //
[3,3.157]	viśvataḥ paramāṃ nityaṃ viśvaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ harim / iti sarvādhikatvoktayā samo 'pi vinivāritaḥ / samādhikasya rāhityānnopacārapumānasau //
[3,3.158]	puruṣa evedaṃ sarvaṃ yad bhūtaṃ yacca bhavyam / utāmṛtatvasyeśāno yadannenātirohati //
[3,3.159]	muktāmuktapareśatvamiti tasyāha sā śrutiḥ / amṛteśānavacanāt sarvasyeśānatoditā //
[3,3.160]	yadi sarvatvamuditamuteśa iti tad vṛthā / utaśabdo vadedeṣa hīśatvasya samuccayam //
[3,3.161]	puruṣeṇedaṃ vyāptamiti brāhmaṇaṃ cāha taṃ prati / etāvānasya mahimeti mahimno vaco hi tat //
[3,3.162]	so 'mṛtasyābhayasyeśo martyamannaṃ yadatyagāt / ityamuktādhipatyaṃ tu pūrvārdhoktamanūdya ca //
[3,3.163]	utāmṛtasyeśa iti vidhatte muktigeśatām / ato viṣṇuparijñānādeva muktirnacānyataḥ / tad yatheti śruteścaiva tataḥ karmakṣayo bhavet //
[3,3.164]	yathaidhāṃsi samiddho 'gnirbhasmasāt kurute 'rjuna / jñānāgniḥ sarvakarmāṇi bhasmasāt kurute tathā //
[3,3.165]	sarvadharmān parityajya māmekaṃ śaraṇaṃ vraja / ahaṃ tvā sarvapāpebhyo mokṣayiṣyāmi mā śucaḥ / ityādibhagavadvākyairuktārthaścāvasīyate //
[3,3.166]	nityanaimittikaṃ karma kurvannanyat parityajan / mucyate saṃsṛteścaitadapyetena nirākṛtam / vidyaivetīmamevārthaṃ svayamevāha vedarāṭ //
[3,3.167]	vinā karma na mokṣaḥ syājjñānenetyapi sā śrutiḥ / nānyaḥ panthā iti hyeva nivārayati sādaram //
[3,3.168]	anyathopāsanamapi tamevamitivādinī / nivārayatyādareṇa na pratīka iti prabhuḥ //
[3,3.169]	andhaṃ tamaḥ praviśanti ye 'vidyāmupāsate / iti śrutivirodhācca nānyathopāsanaṃ bhavet //
[3,3.170]	na cāpyekatvavijñānāduktanyāyena mucyate / iti sarvaṃ pravijñāya sarvaistarkasadāgamaiḥ / upāsīta hariṃ nityaṃ guṇaireva svayogataḥ //
[3,3.171]	brahmā sarvaiguṇaiścaiva kriyāsāmānyataśca gīḥ / guṇasāmānyato rudro dravyasāmānyataḥ pare //
[3,3.172]	adhikāraviśeṣeṇa bhaktijñānasukhādibhiḥ / viśeṣo devatādīnāṃ mokṣe caiva viśeṣataḥ //
[3,3.173]	na tāvatā virodho 'sti nirdoṣatvāt samastaśaḥ / ābhāsatvāt pareṣāṃ tadavarāṇāṃ ca sarvaśaḥ //
[3,3.174]	yato 'varāṇāṃ sarve 'pi guṇāḥ sarvāḥ kriyā api / niyamenaiva pūrveṣāṃ suprasādanibandhanāḥ / ataḥ sacchiṣyavat teṣāṃ naiverṣyādiḥ kathañcana //
[3,3.175]	na ca saṃsāridevānāṃ kāleyattāpare ime / sūtre hyārabdhamātrasya bhogenaiva kṣayo dhruvaḥ //
[3,3.176]	anārabdhakārye bhogena tvitare iti coditaḥ / paunaruktayena tenaite uktārthe iti niścayaḥ //
[3,3.177]	uṣāḥ svāhā ca parjanyo mitro 'gnirvaruṇo vidhuḥ / pravaho 'niruddha indrome rudro vāṇī ca mārutaḥ / uttarottaratastvete guṇaiḥ sarvaiśca muktigāḥ //
[3,3.178]	sūryadharmau yathā somo manurdakṣo bṛhaspatiḥ / śacī ratiścāniruddhasamāstārā ca mitravat //
[3,3.179]	somavacchatarūpā tu prasūtirvahnivad virāṭ / parjanyavad vāruṇī ca tathā sañjñā ca rohiṇī //
[3,3.180]	dharmī ca mitravattvena prāvahī parikīrtitā / mitrapajarnyamadhyasthāvaśvinau vighnavittapau //
[3,3.181]	bhṛguragnisamo mitratanmadhye brahmaputrakāḥ / varuṇāgnyantarā tatra nāradaḥ prāya indravat //
[3,3.182]	kāmaḥ suparṇī comāvad vīndro rudravadīritaḥ / niṛtirmitrasadṛśo viśvāmitraḥ kasūnuvat //
[3,3.183]	vaivasvato manuścāśvipaścādanye tato 'varāḥ / cyavanocathyavainyāśca śaśabinduśca haihayaḥ / tadvacca viprarājanyaviśeṣo 'trāpi kaścana //
[3,3.184]	tadvat priyavrataścāpi tadanyāḥ śatadevatāḥ / pajarnyamitrāntarāḷe tadanye tu tato 'varāḥ //
[3,3.185]	etebhyo 'bhyadhikā śrīrastu sadā muktā viśeṣataḥ / tatsamo nāsti paramo harireva nacāparaḥ //
[3,3.186]	saṃhitāyāṃ bṛhatyāṃ tu svayaṃ bhagavatoditam / tadetadakhilaṃ prāṇa āhaṅkārika eva ca / indrādanantaro dṛṣṭirapi yogyānusārataḥ //
[3,3.187]	samyag guruprasādaśca mukhyato dṛṣṭikāraṇam / śravaṇādi ca kartavyaṃ nānyathā darśanaṃ kvacit //
[3,3.188]	guṇādhikaṃ guruṃ prāpya taddhīnaṃ nāpnuyāt kvacit / viparyayastu kartavyaḥ sarvathā muktimicchatā //
[3,3.189]	same vikalpa eva syāt pūrvānujñā ca sarvathā / taduttamaguruprāptyai pūrvānujñā na mṛgyate //
[3,3.190]	gurubarrahmākhilānāṃ ca vidyā caiva sarasvatī / devatā bhagavān viṣṇuḥ sarveṣāmaviśeṣataḥ //
[3,3.191]	tatprasādena muktiḥ syānnānyathā tu kathañcana / svottamāstu krameṇaiva sarveṣāṃ guravaḥ śrutāḥ / upadeśo brahmaṇastu sarveṣāmeva muktaye //
[3,3.192]	sādhanebhyo 'dhikā bhaktirnaivānyat tādṛśaṃ kvacit / bhaktiścaiva harāveva mukhyānyatra yathākramam //
[3,3.193]	svādhikā tveva sarvatra svottameṣu krameṇa ca / anuvartate ca sā bhaktirmuktāvānandarūpiṇī / tatpūrvakopāsanaivaṃ kartavyā muktaye guṇaiḥ //
<iti śrīmadānandatīrthabhagavatpādācāryaviracite śrīmadbrahmasūtrānuvyākhyāne tṛtīyādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ ||>
{3,4}
[3,4.1]	evamutpannanirdoṣabhagavaddarśanāt sadā / apekṣitaphalaprāptirārabdhasyānatikramāt //
[3,4.2]	devarṣimānuṣādīnāṃ tattajjātyanusārataḥ / jaiminyuktaṃ mānuṣāṇāṃ tadviśeṣāśca kecana //
[3,4.3]	sāmānyaṃ bhagavatproktaṃ devādīnāṃ viśeṣataḥ / balavadvirodhisadbhāve jaiminyādyuktiriṣyate //
[3,4.4]	vikarmalepo naivāsti samyagdṛṣṭimatāṃ kvacit / guṇahāniśca naivāsti brahmaṇastvavikarmataḥ //
[3,4.5]	devānāmapi na prāyaḥ kḷptasya tu kathañcana / prāptahrāso bhavet kvāpi mahatā tu vikarmaṇā / tathāpi tat kḷptameva tasmānna niyamojkhitiḥ //
[3,4.6]	candrasugrīvayoścaiva svoccadāraparigrahāt / prāptahānirabhūnnaiva kḷptahāniḥ yathañcana //
[3,4.7]	hrāso 'pi mānuṣādīnāmānandasya vikarmaṇā / bhavenmuktau viśeṣeṇa svoccānāmaparādhataḥ //
[3,4.8]	jñānottarasya pāpasya caturthe 'lepa ucyate / aśucitvādikaṃ tasya na bhavediti tatphalam / atra jñānaphalasyaiva mukterniyatatocyate //
[3,4.9]	prārabdhakarmajasyaiva viṣabhakṣānmṛteriva / prāptasyāpyanivartyasya kiñcid bhuktasya saṃvidā / upamarda iha prokto devādīnāṃ yathākramam //
[3,4.10]	sarvātmanā tvabhogo hi prārabdhasyaiva karmaṇaḥ / na brahmadarśino 'pi syāt phalahrāsastu vidyate //
[3,4.11]	sarvātmanā phalahrāso yadi nārabdhakarmaṇaḥ / syāt kāmyavidhivaiyarthyamityuktaniyamo bhavet / evamadyāpi samproktaṃ tantrabhāgavate sphuṭam //
[3,4.12]	tāratamyaṃ phale no ced brahmādīnāṃ kathaṃ śrutiḥ / avṛjino 'kāmahata iti muktiṃ nigadya ca / ānandatāratamyaṃ ca teṣāṃ brūyāt pṛthak pṛthak //
[3,4.13]	saṃsāra eva cedetat tāratamyaṃ na mukhyataḥ / akāmahataśabdārtho 'vṛjinatvaṃ ca no bhavet //
[3,4.14]	kāmasya yatrāptāḥ kāmāstatra māmamṛtaṃ kṛdhi / iti yallakṣaṇaṃ mukteḥ śrutirāha balīyasī //
[3,4.15]	kāmāhatiḥ kuto 'nyatra prāptakāmasya sā bhavet / aprayatnena kāmānāmavāptiḥ sā yadā bhavet / tadaivākāmahatatā kuta evānyathā bhavet //
[3,4.16]	cetanasya tvasuptasya kutra dṛṣṭā hyakāmatā / avyaktireva kāmānāṃ na nāśo mohasuptayoḥ //
[3,4.17]	yatkāmaḥ svāpamāpnoti tadevotthāpitaḥ kutaḥ / avaśo 'pi vyāharati kutaḥ suptāvakāmatā //
[3,4.18]	sarvakāmānavāpnoti brahmaṇā saha muktigaḥ / paryeti tatra jakṣaṃśca krīḍan ratimavāpnuvan //
[3,4.19]	kāmānnī kāmarūpī sannimān lokāṃśca sañcaran / āste gāyan sāma mukta ityādiśrutisadbalāt //
[3,4.20]	akāmaḥ syāt kathaṃ muktaḥ kāmā ye 'sya hṛdi śritāḥ / ityantaḥkaraṇasthānāṃ kāmānāṃ mokṣameva hi / āha śrutirhṛdītyeva na ced vyarthaṃ viśeṣaṇam //
[3,4.21]	hṛdyeṣa teṣāṃ śrayaṇamiti pakṣo na bhāsate / muktānāṃ kāmitāmāha pṛthakchākhāsu yacchrutiḥ //
[3,4.22]	ato 'kāmahatatvaṃ tu muktānāmeva mukhyataḥ / mukhyārthasya vṛthā tyāgo māyināmeva bhūṣaṇam //
[3,4.23]	apāpatvamaduḥkhatvaṃ cāvṛjinatvamihoditam / apriyaṃ vṛjinaṃ duḥkhamakaṃ toda itīyarte //
[3,4.24]	tatkāraṇatvāt pāpaṃ vā vṛjinaṃ nāma kathyate / ityuktaḥ svayamīśena nāmārthaḥ śabdanirṇaye //
[3,4.25]	apāpatvaṃ ca naivāsti yāvatsaṃsāramasya hi / ārabdhapāpamastyeva duḥkhaṃ ca jñānino 'pi hi //
[3,4.26]	tasmāt tasmādakāmatvamiti cāśrutakalpanā / akāmahata ityukteḥ śrutahānirapi sphuṭā //
[3,4.27]	kutracit kāminaḥ puṃsaḥ kāmābhāvāt kvacit kvacit / indrādisukhabhogo 'stītyanubhūtirhi kupyati //
[3,4.28]	tasmādamuktasukhagaṃ tāratamyaṃ pṛthak pṛthak / uktvā yaśceti muktānāṃ tāratamyaṃ sukhe śrutiḥ / āheti peśalaṃ tacca caśabdādeva gamyate //
[3,4.29]	rāddhaḥ saṃsiddha ityeva mukta evāvagamyate / sādhunā viṣṇunā yukto muktaḥ sādhuyuvā mataḥ //
[3,4.30]	yauvanaṃ nityametasya muktasyeti yuvā sa ca / phalamadhyayanasyāptaṃ tenādhyāyaka īritaḥ //
[3,4.31]	nirhrāsānandasamprāptyā cāśiṣṭa iti gīyate / sthitasyānanyathā prāpterdṛḍhiṣṭha iti coditaḥ //
[3,4.32]	baliṣṭhaśca svabhāvena mukto bhavati kevalam / tasyeyaṃ pṛthivītyādi pūrvabhāvavyapekṣayā //
[3,4.33]	sa eka iti saṃsāragatamuktavā sukhaṃ punaḥ / śrotriyasyeti vadati muktācchataguṇātmatām //
[3,4.34]	saṃsāragācca saṃsāragatasyaiva śatādhikam / muktānmuktasya yuktaṃ syācchrutyuktamabhivīkṣitaḥ //
[3,4.35]	yuktaṃ ca sādhanādhikyāt sādhyādhikyaṃ surādiṣu / nādhikyaṃ yadi sādhye syāt prayatnaḥ sādhane kutaḥ //
[3,4.36]	yatnaśca dṛśyate teṣāṃ mahāneva mahātmanām / yatra sādhanabāhulyaṃ sādhyabāhulyamatra ca / dṛṣṭaṃ niyamato no cenna yatnaṃ kuryarañjasā //
[3,4.37]	kṛcchreṇa sādhanādeva na muktavadudīryate / daśakalpaṃ tapaścīrṇaṃ rudreṇa lavaṇārṇave / tyaktavā sukhāni sarvāṇi kliṣṭena lavaṇāmbhasā //
[3,4.38]	śakreṇa varṣakoṭiśca dhūmaḥ pīto 'tiduḥkhataḥ / varṣāyutaṃ ca sūryeṇa tapo 'vākchirasā kṛtam //
[3,4.39]	suduḥkhena sukhaṃ tyaktavā dharmeṇākāśaśāyinā / pītā mayīcayo varṣasāhasramatisādaram //
[3,4.40]	atikṛcchreṇa kurvanti yatnaṃ brahmavido 'pi hi / ityetadakhilaṃ mokṣaviśeṣābhāvataḥ katham //
[3,4.41]	daivī sampad vimokṣāya nibandhāyāsurī matā / iti mokṣaviśeṣaśca svayaṃ bhagavatoditaḥ //
[3,4.42]	tameva yūyaṃ bhajatātmavṛttibhirmanovacaḥkāyaguṇaiḥ svakarmabhiḥ / amāyinaḥ kāmadughāṅghripaṅkajaṃ yathādhikārāvasitārthasiddhaye //
[3,4.43]	akṣaṇvantaḥ karṇavantaḥ sakhāyo manojaveṣvasamā babhūvuḥ / ādaghnāsa upakakṣāsa u tve hradā iva snātvā u tve dadṛśre //
[3,4.44]	ityādīni ca vākyāni tāratamyaṃ vimuktigam / vyaktaṃ vadanti tat kena sāmyaṃ mukteṣu gamyate //
[3,4.45]	duḥkhādyabhāvasāmyaṃ ca sāmyavākyārtha īyate / bhaktayādiguṇasadbhāve hyatulyatvaṃ ca bhārate / uktaṃ sādhanavaiśeṣyamapi sarvatra kathyate //
[3,4.46]	durjñeyaṃ ghorarūpasya trailokyadhvaṃsinaḥ prabhoḥ / daivatairmunibhiḥ siddhairmahāyogibhireva ca //
[3,4.47]	nityayuktairmahābhāgairvimuktakleśasādhvasaiḥ / mahotsāhairmahādhairyaiḥ sattvasthairvyavasāyibhiḥ //
[3,4.48]	atītānāgatajñānaprabhavāpyayavedibhiḥ / śaucasvādhyāyasantoṣatapassatyadayānvitaiḥ //
[3,4.49]	kimu martyairbhayabhrāntidhvaṃsamoharujānvitaiḥ / alpāyurvīryadhīsattvavyavasāyaśrutivrataiḥ //
[3,4.50]	kastaṃ madāmadaṃ devaṃ madanyo jñātumarhati / brahmaiva kiñcijjānāti na tadanyo hi kaścana //
[3,4.51]	muktānāmapi siddhānāṃ nārāyaṇaparāyaṇaḥ / sudurlabhaḥ praśāntātmā koṭiṣvapi mahāmate //
[3,4.52]	iyaṃ visṛṣṭiryata ā babhūva yadi vā dadhe yadi vā na / yo asyādhyakṣaḥ parame vyoman tso aṅga veda yadi vā na veda //
[3,4.53]	yaḥ svātmamāyāvibhavaṃ svayaṃ gato nāhaṃ nabhasvāṃstamathāpare kutaḥ / brahmāpi yaṃ vetti naiveha samyaganye kuto devamunīndramartyāḥ //
[3,4.54]	namaste 'mitatattvāya dharmādīnāṃ ca sūtaye / nirguṇāya ca satkāṣṭhāṃ nāhaṃ vedāpare kutaḥ //
[3,4.55]	nāhaṃ parāyur ṛṣayo na marīcimukhyā jānanti yadviracitaṃ khalu sattvasaṅgāḥ / yanmāyayā muṣitacetasa īśadaityamartyādayaḥ kimuta śaśvadabhadravṛttāḥ //
[3,4.56]	ahaṃ mahendro nirṛtiḥ pracetāḥ somo 'gnirīśaḥ pavano 'rko viriñcaḥ / ādityaviśve vasavo 'tha sādhyā marudgaṇā rudragaṇāḥ sasiddhāḥ //
[3,4.57]	anye ca ye viśvasṛjo 'mareśā bhṛgvādayo 'spṛṣṭarajastamaskāḥ / yasyehitaṃ na viduḥ spṛṣṭṛmāyāḥ sattvapradhānā api kiṃ tato 'nye //
[3,4.58]	savarsyādau smṛto brahmā tasmād devādanantaraḥ / jānāti devapravaraṃ bhūyaścāto 'dhikaṃ nṛpa //
[3,4.59]	na tvāmatiśayiṣyanti muktāvapi kathañcana / madbhaktiyogājjñānācca sarvānatiśayiṣyasi //
[3,4.60]	yathā bhaktiviśeṣo 'tra dṛśyate puruṣottame / tathā muktiviśeṣo 'pi jñānināṃ liṅgabhedane //
[3,4.61]	sāyujyaṃ samanuprāptā api devādayo 'khilāḥ / tāratamyāddhi tiṣṭhanti tāratamyaṃ hi sādhane //
[3,4.62]	manuṣyāṇāṃ sahasreṣu kaścid yatati siddhaye / yatatāmapi siddhānāṃ kaścinmāṃ vetti tattvataḥ //
[3,4.63]	ya imaṃ paramaṃ guhyaṃ madbhakteṣvabhidhāsyati / bhaktiṃ mayi parāṃ kṛtvā māmevaiṣyatyasaṃśayaḥ //
[3,4.64]	na ca tasmānmanuṣyeṣu kaścinme priyakṛttamaḥ / bhavitā na ca me tasmādanyaḥ priyataro bhuvi //
[3,4.65]	adhyeṣyate ca ya imaṃ dharmyaṃ saṃvādamāvayoḥ / jñānayajñena tenāhamiṣṭaḥ syāmiti me matiḥ //
[3,4.66]	śraddhāvānanasūyuśca śṛṇuyādapi yo naraḥ / so 'pi muktaḥ śubhān lokān prāpnuyāt puṇyakarmaṇām //
[3,4.67]	dhyānenātmani paśyanti kecidātmānamātmanā / anye sāṅkhayena yogena karmayogena cāpare //
[3,4.68]	anye tvevamajānantaḥ śrutvānyebhya upāsate / te 'pi cātitarantyeva mṛtyuṃ śrutiparāyaṇāḥ //
[3,4.69]	susūkṣmairapyaśeṣaiśca viśeṣaiḥ saha paśyati / svātmānaṃ bhagavān viṣṇuḥ sarvarūpo 'pi sarvadā //
[3,4.70]	savartra cānyadapyevaṃ tenādṛṣṭaṃ na hi kvacit / sarvatra sarvadaiveśaṃ paśyatyeva ramāpi tu //
[3,4.71]	natu sarvairviśeṣaistaṃ paśyantyapyanyato 'dhikam / svātmānamanyaccāśeṣaṃ paśyatyeva hi sarvadā //
[3,4.72]	brahmā tu sarvagaṃ paśyed guṇānapyato 'dhikam / natu sarveṣu kāleṣu tathā paśyatyamuktigaḥ //
[3,4.73]	muktastu sarvadā paśyet sarvagatvena cāpi tu / na ramāvad viśeṣāṇāṃ darśanaṃ śaknuyāt kvacit //
[3,4.74]	svātmānamanyacca sadā viśeṣairakhilairapi / paśyantyañjastathā vāṇī viśoṣāṃstāvato natu / traiguṇyāt parataḥ paśyed vyāptaṃ śataguṇaṃ harim //
[3,4.75]	giriśo garuḍaścaiva tamomātragataṃ harim / paśyed viśeṣānapi hi vāṇīdṛṣṭān na paśyati //
[3,4.76]	umā suparṇī ca mahattattvaṃ yāvat prapaśyati / rudradṛṣṭān viśeṣāṃśca naiva paśyet kadācana //
[3,4.77]	svarūpamanyarūpaṃ ca muktā devāḥ samastaśaḥ / jānantīndraśca kāmaśca brahma yāvadahaṅkṛtiḥ //
[3,4.78]	paśyanto manudakṣādyā buddhitattvasthitaṃ harim / paśyanti somasūryau tu manasthaṃ parameśvaram //
[3,4.79]	anye bhūtasthitaṃ viṣṇuṃ devāḥ paśyanti sarvadā / bahusāhasravarṣeṇa mahattattve kvacit kvacit //
[3,4.80]	anye caiva yathāyogyamaṇḍāntarvartinaṃ harim / śvetadvīpapatiṃ caiva hṛdyevānye tu kecana / kadācideva tatrāpi kecit paśyanti keśavam //
[3,4.81]	umā yāvadanantāṃśān pūrvadṛṣṭebhya eva tu / viśeṣān vāsudevasya paścāduktā vicakṣate //
[3,4.82]	śakrakāmādayaścaiva viśeṣān brahmaṇi sthitān / umādibhiḥ prabuddhebhyaḥ śatāṃśāneva cakṣate //
[3,4.83]	ityādivedasmṛtigavacanebhyo yathārthataḥ / tāratamyaṃ vimuktānāṃ sādhanānāṃ ca dṛśyate //
[3,4.84]	sādhyasādhanavairūpyamadṛṣṭaṃ kena kalpyate / vaiṣamyaṃ nirghṛṇatvaṃ ca tena syātāṃ parasya ca / sāpekṣatvāditi ca tau vidyādhīśena vāritau //
[3,4.85]	tāratamyāt sādhanānāṃ sādhyatādṛktavamīśataḥ / avaiṣamyādihetuḥ syāt sadaiva parameśvare //
[3,4.86]	svātantrye vidyamāne 'pi sādhanādau pareśituḥ / apekṣyānādivaicitṛyaṃ na doṣa iti tadvacaḥ / nānāditvāditi hyuktamupapadyata ityapi //
[3,4.87]	apekṣyopāyavaiṣamyamupeyasya tathā sthitiḥ / mayā kayā viruddhā syād rājādāvapi dṛśyate //
[3,4.88]	tyāgo dṛṣṭasya cādṛṣṭakalpaneti suduṣkarau / māyibhyo 'nyena kenāpi tat kimanyaiśca vādibhiḥ //
[3,4.89]	māyino 'trānugamyante śrutahānyaśrutagrahau / apyatra māyināṃ liṅge tat ke doṣāstato 'dhikāḥ //
[3,4.90]	niśśeṣagatadoṣāṇāṃ bahubhirjanmabhiḥ punaḥ / syādāparokṣyaṃ hi harerdveṣerṣyādistataḥ kutaḥ //
[3,4.91]	bhaveyuryadi cerṣyādyāḥ sameṣvapi kuto na te / tapyamānāḥ samān dṛṣṭvā dveṣerṣyādiyutā api / dṛśyante bahavo loke doṣā evātra kāraṇam //
[3,4.92]	yadi nirdoṣatā tatra kimādhikyena dūṣyate / yadyanyadarśanābhāvādīrṣyādirvinivāryate / adarśanādaratyādiḥ kathaṃ tena nivāryate //
[3,4.93]	brahmaṇo 'pyaratirdṛṣṭvā pūrvamekākinaḥ śrutau / naiva reme sa caikākī tasamānna ramate kvacit / dvitīyamaicchat tenāsāviti śrutaya ūdire //
[3,4.94]	yadīcchā tatra naivāstītyeva tat kalpyate mṛṣā / śrutyuktanirdoṣataiva kiṃ nāṅgīkriyate svayam //
[3,4.95]	tāratamyaṃ ca kāmaṃ ca śrutamevātihāya tu / aśrutā samatā kena kalpyate yuktimāninā //
[3,4.96]	kiṃ tanmānaṃ samatve te muktānāmupalabhyate / vṛthāyamāgrahaḥ kena śrutahānyaśrutagrahe //
[3,4.97]	mokṣe 'pi tāratamyetaścetanatvāt purā yathā / ityukta uttaraṃ kiṃ te kalpanāmātravādinaḥ //
[3,4.98]	na ca duḥkhādikaṃ kalpyaṃ nirduḥkhatvaśruterbalāt / śokaṃ taratyātmavettā tīrṇaḥ sarvānaduḥkhabhāk //
[3,4.99]	yenānandyeva bhavati na śocati kadācana / kilbiṣaspṛt pituṣaṇiraraṃ hita iheśvaraḥ //
[3,4.100]	yaṃ yamantamabhiprepsuḥ sa saṅkalpād bhavediha / ityādiśrutayo mānaṃ nirduḥkhatvādisampadi //
[3,4.101]	ato duḥkhādyanumayā nāvakāśo 'tra labhyate / tāratamyānumā tena bhavennātiprasaṅginī //
[3,4.102]	śrutiyuktibalādevaṃ tāratamyaṃ vibhāvyate / muktāvapi tataḥ ke 'tra virodhaṃ kartumīśate //
[3,4.103]	anādiyogyatāṃ caiva kalivāṇīśvarāvadhim / ko nivārayituṃ śakto yuktayāgamabaloddhatām //
[3,4.104]	brahmaṇo 'nyatra ādhikyayuktaḥ kālo vivādavān / kālo hyayaṃ yathetyādi mānumāmānino bhavet //
[3,4.105]	anyaśabdo hariśrīsvasamebhyo 'nyavivakṣayā / prayukto naiva doṣāya rudrādiṣu ca yuktitaḥ //
[3,4.106]	uttamatvaṃ tu muktānāmapi na brahmaṇo bhavet / vyaktiḥ sukhasya tu bhavennatvādhikyaṃ sukhasya ca //
[3,4.107]	balajñānādhikatvaṃ ca tebhyo hi brahmaṇaḥ sadā / ādhikyasya tvanityatve na kiñcinmānamīyate //
[3,4.108]	śṛṇve vīra ugramugraṃ damāyannanyamanyamatinenīyamānaḥ / edhamānadviḷubhayasya rājā coṣkūyate viśa indro manuṣyān //
[3,4.109]	parā pūrveṣāṃ sakhyā vṛṇakti vitarturāṇo aparebhireti / anānubhūtīravadhūnvānaḥ pūrvītindraḥ śaradastartarīti //
[3,4.110]	divedive sadṛśīranyamardhaṃ kṛṣṇā asedhadapa sadmano jāḥ / ahan dāsā vṛṣabho vasnayantodavraje varcinaṃ śambaraṃ ca //
[3,4.111]	taṃ bhūtiriti devā upāsāñcakrire te babhūvustasmāddhāpyetarhi supto bhūbhrūrityeva praśvasityabhūtirityasurāste ha parābabhūvuḥ //
[3,4.112]	tad yathā peśaskarī peśaso mātrāmapādāyānyannavataraṃ kalyāṇataraṃ rūpaṃ tanuta evamevāyamātmedaṃ śarīraṃ nihatyāvidyāṃ gamayitavānyannavataraṃ kalyāṇataraṃ rūpaṃ kurute pitṛyaṃ pitṛyaṃ vā gāndharvaṃ vā daivaṃ vā prājāpatyaṃ vā brāhmaṃ vānyeṣāṃ vā bhūtānām //
[3,4.113]	prayānti paramāṃ siddhimaihikāmuṣmikīṃ drutam / yā na prāpyāsuraiḥ sarvairakṣayā kleśavarjitā / na tāṃ gatiṃ prapadyante vinā bhāgavatān narān //
[3,4.114]	avajānanti māṃ mūḍhā mānuṣīṃ tanumāśritam / paraṃ bhāvamajānanto mama bhūtamaheśvaram //
[3,4.115]	moghāśā moghakarmāṇo moghajñānā vicetasaḥ / rākṣasīmāsurīṃ caiva prakṛtiṃ mohanīṃ śritāḥ //
[3,4.116]	mahātmānastu māṃ pārtha daivīṃ prakṛtimāśritāḥ / bhajantyananyamanaso jñātvā bhūtādimavyayam //
[3,4.117]	abhayaṃ sattvasaṃśuddhirjñānayogavyavasthitiḥ / dānaṃ damaśca yajñaśca svādhyāyastapa ārjavam //
[3,4.118]	ahiṃsā satyamakrodhastyāgaḥ śāntirapaiśunam / dayā bhūteṣvalolutvaṃ mārdavaṃ hrīracāpalam //
[3,4.119]	tejaḥ kṣamā dhṛtiḥ śaucamadroho nātimānitā / bhavanti sampadaṃ daivīmabhijātasya bhārata //
[3,4.120]	ḍambho darpo 'timāśca krodhaḥ pāruṣyameva ca / ajñānaṃ cābhijātasya pārtha sampadamāsurīm //
[3,4.121]	māmātmaparadeheṣu pradviṣanto 'bhyasūyakāḥ / tānahaṃ dviṣataḥ krūrān saṃsāreṣu narādhamān / kṣipāmyajasramaśubhānāsurīṣveva yoniṣu //
[3,4.122]	āsurīṃ yonimāpannā mūḍhā janmani janmani / māmaprāpyaiva kaunteya tato yāntyadhamāṃ gatim //
[3,4.123]	dvividho bhūtasargo 'tra daiva āsura eva ca / viṣṇubhaktiparo daivo viparītastathā'suraḥ //
[3,4.124]	devānāṃ paramo dharmaḥ sadā yajñādikāḥ kriyāḥ / svādhyāyastattvaveditvaṃ viṣṇupūjāratiḥ smṛtiḥ //
[3,4.125]	daityānāṃ bāhuṣāḷitvaṃ mātsaryaṃ yuddhasatkriyā / nītiśāstrapraveditvaṃ śivapūjāratiḥ smṛtiḥ //
[3,4.126]	varṇāśramācāravattvaṃ svādhyāyo bhaktiracyute / śive sūrye tathā devyāṃ svabhāvo mānuṣaḥ smṛtaḥ //
[3,4.127]	anādivaiṣṇavā eva devatāstu svabhāvataḥ / viparītāstato daityāḥ sadaivānādikālataḥ //
[3,4.128]	mānuṣā miśramatayo vimiśragatayo 'pi ca / ityādivākyasandarbhe jñāyate 'nādiyogyatā //
[3,4.129]	yadyanādirviśeṣo na sāmprataṃ kathameva saḥ / adṛṣṭādeva cādṛṣṭaṃ svīkṛtaṃ savarvādibhiḥ //
[3,4.130]	ākasmiko viśeṣaścedadṛṣṭe kvacidiṣyate / sarvatrākasmikatvaṃ syānnādṛṣṭāpekṣatā bhavet / adṛṣṭāśced viśeṣo 'yamanāditvaṃ kuto na tat //
[3,4.131]	nacānyabhedavad viṣṇau bhedastaddarśināmapi / dṛśyate pratyabhijñaiva bahurūpeṣu dṛśyate //
[3,4.132]	bahutvaṃ ca viśeṣeṇa na bhedena kathañcana / pratyabhijñā ca yeṣāṃ na te 'pi tanmuṣyadṛṣṭayaḥ //
[3,4.133]	bhedaṃ naiva prapaśyanti bhedamanyebhya eva ca / paśyantyevaṃ haristeṣāṃ sandarśayati nānyathā //
