[3,4.134]	evaṃ bṛhatsaṃhitāyāṃ vacanaṃ na purāṇagam / lokadarśanavādyeva vedarodhāya śaknuyāt //
[3,4.135]	aparīkṣitadṛṣṭiśca parīkṣāpūrvadarśanam / niṣeddhuṃ śaknuvādyeva vedarodhāya śaknuyāt //
[3,4.136]	na ca niścitabhedasya darśane 'sti purāṇagam / vākyaṃ kvaciddhi sammugdhadarśanaṃ tatra gamyate //
[3,4.137]	aparīkṣitamevātra vedhādikamadhīśituḥ / parīkṣādarśane naiva dṛśyate kenacit kvacit //
[3,4.138]	nirdoṣameva taṃ brahmā dadarśāśeṣarūpiṇam / nirdoṣameva rudro 'drāṅ nirdoṣaṃ taṃ purandaraḥ //
[3,4.139]	nirdoṣāṇyasya rūpāṇi dṛṣṭānyevaṃ surottamaiḥ / anye sadoṣāḥ sarve 'pi nirdoṣo harirekalaḥ / iti barkuśruteścaiva sadoṣaṃ nāsya darśanam //
[3,4.140]	aviddho viddhavad viṣṇurajāto jātavanmṛṣā / abaddho baddhavaccaiva darśayatyamitadyutiḥ / iti paiṅgiśrutiścaiva prāha nirdoṣatāṃ hareḥ //
[3,4.141]	aparīkṣitadṛṣṭayaiva sadoṣo dṛśyate hariḥ / parīkṣādarśane naiva dṛśyo doṣo hareḥ kvacit / iti paiṅgiśrutiścāha pramāṇaṃ hi parīkṣitam //
[3,4.142]	na parīkṣānavasthā syāt sākṣisiddhe tvasaṃśayāt / mānase darśane doṣāḥ syurnavai sākṣidarśane / sudṛḍho nirṇayo yatra jñeyaṃ tat sākṣidarśanam //
[3,4.143]	icchā jñānaṃ sukhaṃ duḥkhabhayābhayakṛpādayaḥ / sākṣisiddhā na kaściddhi tatra saṃśayavān kvacit / yat kvacid vyabhicārī syād darśanaṃ mānasaṃ hi tat //
[3,4.144]	manaścakṣurdarśanāderapi yatraiva sākṣiṇā / prāmāṇyaṃ sugṛhītaṃ syāt tat parīkṣitadarśanam //
[3,4.145]	na jñānadṛṣṭimātreṇa prāmāṇyaṃ tasya dṛśyate / niyamena sukhādyeṣu prāmāṇyaṃ sākṣigocaram //
[3,4.146]	svaprāmāṇyaṃ sadā sākṣī paśyatyeva suniścayāt / jñānasya grāhakeṇaiva sākṣiṇā mānatāmiteḥ //
[3,4.147]	doṣābhāve pramāṇatvaṃ doṣābhāvasya sākṣiṇā / niścitatvaṃ kvaciccaiva svataḥ prāmāṇyamiṣyate //
[3,4.148]	ato na sarvamānānāṃ prāmāṇyaṃ niścitaṃ bhavet / sākṣiṇā niścitaṃ yatra tat prāmāṇyasvalakṣaṇam //
[3,4.149]	na hi kaścit sukhādyeṣu saṃśayaṃ kurute janaḥ / nacaivākhilamānāni niścinotyakhilo janaḥ //
[3,4.150]	tasmādanubhavārūḍhaṃ kimarthamupalapyate / doṣābhāvādikaṃ caiva sākṣī samyak prapaśyati //
[3,4.151]	tat parīkṣitamānena na doṣo viṣṇavi kvacit / aparīkṣitadṛṣṭistu kasminnarthe na vidyate //
[3,4.152]	tat pratyakṣaviruddhārthe nāgamasyāpi mānatā / upajīvyamakṣajaṃ yatra tadanyatra viparyayaḥ //
[3,4.153]	laukike vyavahāre 'tra pratyakṣasyopajīvyatā / avatārādidaṣṭau syādāgamasyopajīvyatā //
[3,4.154]	āgamena hi viṣṇutvaṃ jñātvā doṣo 'tra kalpyate / na cet syāt doṣavānanyaḥ śāstrasiddhaṃ hi lakṣaṇam //
[3,4.155]	kasyacid doṣavattvaṃ syāditimātre 'kṣajaṃ bhavet / na viṣṇordeṣavattve hi pratyakṣaṃ vartate svataḥ //
[3,4.156]	kecit paśyanti doṣānityatrāpi syānnacākṣajam / paurāṇaṃ vākyamevātra tacchrutyaiva viruddhayate //
[3,4.157]	purāṇasyopajīvyaśca veda eva nacāparaḥ / tadvirodhe kathaṃ mānaṃ tat tatra ca bhaviṣyati //
[3,4.158]	aparīkṣitadṛṣṭiśca kathamevākṣajaṃ bhavet / yadyevaṃ devadattādibhramaḥ kiṃ nākṣajaṃ bhavet //
[3,4.159]	yāvacchakti parīkṣāyāmupajīvyasya bādhane / doṣo nāśodhite doṣa upajīvyatvamasvalam //
[3,4.160]	bhrame 'pyabhramabhāgo 'sti tanmātramupajīvya hi / bādhakajñānavṛttiḥ syānnacaivaṃ suparīkṣite / sarvaṃ tadupajīvyaiva pramāṇaṃ vartate yataḥ //
[3,4.161]	kathaṃ brahmeti tajjñeyaṃ sarvajñatvādilakṣaṇam / vihāya yasmātkasmāccit svarūpasyaiva ced yadi //
[3,4.162]	upajīvyatvametasmād vyāvṛttaṃ yāvatā bhavet / tāvataivopajīvyatvaṃ svarapasyaiva na kvacit //
[3,4.163]	sarvalakṣaṇayuktaṃ tu svarūpaṃ yadi bhaṇyate / astu no naiva hāniḥ syāt svapakṣaścāyamañjasā //
[3,4.164]	yasmādanvita evārthaḥ śabdānāmapi sarvaśaḥ / viśeṣasāmanyatayā svarūpamakhilaṃ bhavet //
[3,4.165]	purovartitvapūrvāṇi devadattādikabhrame / vyāvartayanti tadrūpaṃ caitramātrad vinaiva hi //
[3,4.166]	brahmaṇo nirviśeṣatvād vyāvartayati kiṃ punaḥ / yasmātkasmāccidapyarthāt tāvaccet siddhasādhanam //
[3,4.167]	cinmātratvaṃ ca naiveṣyamaviśeṣatvavādinaḥ / tāvanmātraṃ yadīṣyaṃ syāt sarvajñatvaṃ kuto na tat //
[3,4.168]	cinmātrābhedasādhye 'pi siddhaṃ tat prativādinaḥ / svābhedāṅgīkṛtereva cittvaṃ svasyāpi yanmatam //
[3,4.169]	sarvāpekṣatayā sarvajñatvamityeva tannahi / iti ceccetanatvaṃ ca jñatvaṃ na jñeyavarjitam //
[3,4.170]	svajñeyatvaṃ ca naivāsau manyate saviśeṣataḥ / svaśabdo 'pi parāpekṣastasmād vyāvṛttireva hi / svaśabdārtha iti proktaḥ svarūpaṃ nāma kiṃ na cet //
[3,4.171]	rūpaśabdena pūrṇatvāt tacca sāmānyatāvacaḥ / na svarūpābhidhāyi syād vaiyarthyaṃ svaravasya yat //
[3,4.172]	cetanasya svabhāvo hi caitanyamiti gīyate / tasmād viśeṣabāhulyaṃ caitanyasya viśeṣataḥ //
[3,4.173]	na jñeyajñātṛhīnaṃ hi jñānaṃ nāma kvacid bhavet / jñeyajñānavihīnaśca jña ityatra ca na pramā //
[3,4.174]	jñātṛjñeyavihīnaṃ ca jñānaṃ ced bhoktṛbhojyataḥ / hīnaṃ bhojanameva syāt tāḍanaṃ kartṛtāḍyataḥ //
[3,4.175]	nityatvāt tādṛśaṃ ca syāditi cennityavāgapi / vācyavaktṛvihīnā syānnahi sā caiva tādṛśī //
[3,4.176]	draṣṭāro vedavāco hi santi vācyāni cāñjasā / nityo draṣṭā ca vācyaśca bhagavāneva ca svayam //
[3,4.177]	na hi vaktṛvihīnā ca vācyahīnāpi vāk kvacit / jñātṛjñeyavihīnaṃ ca jñānamevaṃ na tad bhavet //
[3,4.178]	na hi nityo 'pi vaktāsti vākyavācyavivarjitaḥ / jñānajñeyavihīnaśca jño 'pyevaṃ naiva vidyate //
[3,4.179]	kiñca sarvavilopaśca kena mānena gamyate / sarveṇa saha tad vākyāmarthaśca yadi gṛhyate / tadabhāvena sarvasya nāpalāpo bhavet tadā //
[3,4.180]	na gṛhyate ced tannyāyādapalāpo na hi kvacit / upapattivihīnasya vākyasyārtho na gamyate //
[3,4.181]	upakramādiliṅgānāṃ balīyo hyuttarottaram / śrutyādau pūrvapūrvaṃ ca brahmatarkavinirṇayāt //
[3,4.182]	pratyakṣamupapattiśca bahavaścāgamā yadā / viruddhayante nacārtho 'sti yatra liṅgavirodhitā //
[3,4.183]	sa evārthaḥ kathaṃ grāhya upapanne 'virodhinī / mukhyārthe vidyamāne tu kva sāvarjñyaṃ niṣiddhayate //
[3,4.184]	ataḥ sarvaguṇairyuktaṃ brahmāṅgīkāyarmeva hi / apalāpo 'pi sarvasya na kathañcana yujyate //
[3,4.185]	anādiyogyatā coktā tena grāhyaiva sarvathā / muktānāṃ tāratamyaṃ ca mānairuktairna cālyate //
[3,4.186]	jñānino 'pi yato nityaṃ kurvanti śubhameva hi / tāratamyaṃ tu muktau ca tenaivādhyavasīyate //
[3,4.187]	tāratamyaṃ na cenmuktau kutaḥ kuryuḥ śubhaṃ punaḥ / kṛcchreṇāpi tapo jñānaṃ karmāpyete caranti hi //
[3,4.188]	bibhyati smāśubhānnityaṃ sakāmāśca śubhe sadā / na ca svabhāva evāyaṃ bhayapūrvapravṛttitaḥ / kṛcchreṇācaraṇāccaiva śubhasyaiva punaḥ punaḥ //
[3,4.189]	tādṛśo 'pi svabhāvaścedajñasyāpi bhavet tathā / phalavattve pramāṇaṃ cet tatra jñasya samaṃ hi tat //
[3,4.190]	niṣkāmaṃ jñānapūrvaṃ ca nivṛttamiha cocyate / nivṛttaṃ sevamānastu brahmābhyeti sanātanam //
[3,4.191]	śubhenānandavṛddhi syādghrāsaścaivāśubhena hi / jñānino 'pi yatastena kartavyaṃ śubhameva taiḥ //
[3,4.192]	upāste sa ya ātmānaṃ kṣīyate nāsya karma ha / asmāddhayevātmano yadyat kāmayet sṛjate ca tat //
[3,4.193]	avidvān bahukarmāpi hyantavat phalamāpnuyāt / yadeva vidyayā kuryāt tadeva hyativīryavat / ityādivākyasāmarthyāt tāratamyaṃ vimuktigam //
[3,4.194]	nacātropāsakasyaiva phalamakṣayamucyate / na hi jñānaṃ vinā kvāpi phalasyākṣayatā bhavet / jñānadvāreṇa cet tasya nāsmatpakṣapratīpatā //
[3,4.195]	jñānottarasyaivamapi hyakṣayatvaṃ nacānyathā / pūrvabhāviśubhānāṃ hi jñānenaiva kṛtārthatā //
[3,4.196]	prārabdhānāṃ tu bhogena tajjñānottarakarmaṇām / muktāvanupraveśaḥ syādanyathā tatkṛtirnahi //
[3,4.197]	jñānāt pūrvāṇi sarvāṇi śubhāni jñānasiddhaye / akāmyāni niṣiddhāni jñānarodhāya bhuktaye //
[3,4.198]	yogyatāyā balād yacca śubhabāhulyamāditaḥ / jñānabāhulyamevaitat kuryānnānyasya kāraṇam //
[3,4.199]	jñānasya bhaktibhāgatvād bhaktirjñānamitīryate / jñānasyaiva viśeṣo yad bhaktirityabhidhīyate //
[3,4.200]	parokṣatvāparokṣatve viśeṣau jñānagau yathā / snehayogo 'pi tadvat syād viśeṣo jñānagocaraḥ //
[3,4.201]	ityābhiprāyataḥ prāyo jñānameva vimuktaye / vadanti śrutayaḥ so 'yaṃ viśeṣo 'pi hyudīryate //
[3,4.202]	bhaktirjñānamiti kvāpi na hi dveṣayutā dṛśiḥ / puruṣārthāya bhavati sarvaśrutivirodhataḥ //
[3,4.203]	cetanasya dvayaṃ bhogyaṃ saṃsāro muktireva ca / saṃsārastrividhastatra svargo madhyamadhastathā //
[3,4.204]	muktiśca dvividhā tatra sukhaṃ nityaṃ tathāparam / nityaduḥkhamiti jñeyaṃ sādhanaṃ saṃsṛtāvapi / kāmyaṃ karma niṣiddhaṃ ca sājñānamiti niścayaḥ //
[3,4.205]	dveṣo bhaktiśca muktau tu muktidvayavidhāyakam / iti paiṅgiśruterdveṣo naiva sanmuktikāraṇam //
[3,4.206]	asanmukteḥ kāraṇaṃ ca muktāvityatra keśavaḥ / muktiśabdodito mokṣaṃ svabhaktānāṃ karoti yat //
[3,4.207]	dveṣato 'pi vimuktiścenmahātātparyarodhanam / bhaktayā prasannato devānmuktirityeva tadguṇān / vadanti śrutayaḥ sarvāḥ purāṇānyāgamā api //
[3,4.208]	yadi dveṣeṇa muktiḥ syād vaktavyo doṣasañcayaḥ / smartavyo bhagavān nityamityarthenaiva hi kvacit / dveṣādiva guṇānāha purāṇe kruddhavākyavat //
[3,4.209]	yathā kruddhaḥ pitā putraṃ maretyākṣepapūrvakam / proktasyānyasya kṛtyarthaṃ vadatyevaṃ purāṇagam //
[3,4.210]	vākyaṃ śrutivirodhena svavirodhena cāñjasā / bahvāgamavirodhācca na dveṣānmuktivācakam //
[3,4.211]	tamo dveṣeṇa saṃyānti bhaktayā muktiṃ tathaiva ca / viṣṇau viṣṇuprasādena vilomatvena cāñjasā / iti ṣāḍguṇyavacanamapyuktārthaniyāmakam //
[3,4.212]	mahātātparyarodhe ca kathaṃ vākyaṃ pramāṇatām / yāti sarvārtharūpaṃ hi mahātātparyamiṣyate //
[3,4.213]	vācakatvaṃ hi tātparyaṃ yadarthā akhilā ravāḥ / so 'rthaḥ kathaṃ parityājya ekaśabdasya saṃśaye / ato vijñānabhaktibhyāṃ puruṣārthaḥ paro bhavet //
[3,4.214]	yasya deve parā bhaktiryathā deve tathā gurau / tasyaite kathitā hyarthāḥ prakāśante mahātmanaḥ //
[3,4.215]	bhaktyā jñānaṃ tato bhaktistato dṛṣṭistataśca sā / tato muktistato bhaktiḥ saiva syāt sukharūpiṇī //
[3,4.216]	bhaktayā prasanno bhagavān dadyājjñānamanākulam / tayaiva darśanaṃ yātaḥ pradadyānmuktimetayā //
[3,4.217]	nāhaṃ vedairna tapasā na dānena nacejyayā / śakya evaṃvidho draṣṭuṃ pradadyānmuktimetayā //
[3,4.218]	bhaktayā tvananyayā śakya ahamevaṃvidho 'rjuna / jñātuṃ draṣṭuṃ ca tattvena praveṣyuṃ ca parantapa //
[3,4.219]	ityādivākyataścaiva so 'yamuktārtha īyate / na ca prasādamāpnoti dveṣād bhaktyā tamāpnuyāt / iti dṛṣṭānusāritvamapyasminnartha īyate //
[3,4.220]	ye pṛthag vihitā viṣṇorguṇā vedena sādaram / ta eva dṛṣṭavailomyādaṅgīkāryā nacāparam //
[3,4.221]	anyad dṛṣṭānusāreṇa vāsudeve 'pi gṛhyate / doṣābhāvāśca ye vedairuditā avihāya tān //
[3,4.222]	anuktā apica grāhyā mahātātparyaśaktitaḥ / evaṃ bṛhatsaṃhitāvāk siddhānto hi tadīritaḥ //
[3,4.223]	tāratamyena tadbhakteṣvapi bhaktirviniścayāt / kartavyaiṣāpi tadbhaktirlokavedānusārataḥ //
[3,4.224]	yo hi bhaktaḥ pradhāne syāt tadīyeṣvapi bhaktimān / dṛśyate 'sau niyamato viparīto viparyaye //
[3,4.225]	vyabhicāro yadi kvāpi bhaktihrāso 'tra kalpyate / bhaktidoṣo hyasau yanna tadbhakteṣvapi bhaktimān //
[3,4.226]	tāratamyena teṣvaddhā bhaktirdṛṣṭānusārataḥ / viṣṇuprasādānusārāt kāryā doṣastadanyathā //
[3,4.227]	svaprītyanusṛtau prītirloke 'pyaddhaiva dṛśyate / tāratamyaparijñānamapyetenaiva sādhanam //
[3,4.228]	lakṣmīviriñcavāṇīśagirijendrāṅgirassutāḥ / sūryādayaśca kramaśo bhagavatprītigocarāḥ //
[3,4.229]	teṣu bhaktiḥ krameṇaiva kāryā nityaṃ mumukṣubhiḥ / sarve 'pi guravaścaite puruṣasya sadaiva hi //
[3,4.230]	tasmāt pūjyāśca namyāśca dhyeyāśca parito harim / iti ṣāḍguṇyavacanādapyeṣo 'rtho 'vasīyate //
[3,4.231]	haribhaktiḥ krameṇaiva tadīyeṣu harismṛtiḥ / haristutistatsmṛtiśca tatstutirharipūjanam //
[3,4.232]	tatpūjāvihitatyāga iti mukteḥ krameṇa hi / niyamāt sādhanānyeva nityasādhyāni cākhilaiḥ //
[3,4.233]	iti pravṛttavacanaṃ sādhanasya vinirṇaye / pravṛtte pañcarātre hi sādhanasyātiniścayaḥ //
[3,4.234]	haridveṣo na śubhada ;saddveṣatvād yathā guroḥ / kramād bhaktirhariprītikāraṇaṃ tatpriyaupagā / bhaktiryato yathā svasminnityādyā yuktiratra ca //
[3,4.235]	prādhānyatāratamyānusāriṇī bhaktiruttamā / prītidaiva hareryasmād bhaktiḥ sā svopagā yathā //
[3,4.236]	iti vā jñānakarmādiphalaṃ caiṣu kramopagam / svātantryatāratamyena phalaṃ hi phalināṃ bhavet //
[3,4.237]	aśubhaṃ tvaśubhe 'pyeṣāṃ svātantryāt prītito hareḥ / ājñayā cānyagaṃ naiva bhogāya bhavati kvacit //
[3,4.238]	puṇyamevāmumāpānoti na devān pāpamāpnuyāt / ityādiśrutayo mānamukte 'rthe yuktayo 'parāḥ //
[3,4.239]	upāsanādharmaphalaṃ yato dehāntare sthitiḥ / vāsudevājñayā caiva pūrvakarmānusārataḥ //
[3,4.240]	prerayanti hi te jīvān puṇyapāpeṣu nityaśaḥ / arāgadveṣataścaiva kathaṃ doṣānavāpnuyuḥ //
[3,4.241]	haryājñākaraṇādeva puṇyamebhiravāpyate / haripūjeti coddeśāt kathaṃ na śubhamāpnuyuḥ //
[3,4.242]	ato yathākramaṃ dharmajñānayoḥ phalamañjasā / sarvaprāṇigataṃ devāḥ prāpnuvantyā viriñcataḥ //
[3,4.243]	devā eva hi devānāṃ viśiṣṭā viniyāmakāḥ / brahmā tvakhiladevānāṃ narāṇāṃ ca niyāmakaḥ / ataḥ sarvaguṇāneṣa prāpanotyadhikamanyataḥ //
[3,4.244]	dravyasvātantryavijñānaprayatnairadhikaṃ phalam / devānāmanyagaṃ cāpi teṣu yad brahmaṇo hi tat //
[3,4.245]	bṛhattantroditaṃ vākyaṃ hariṇā phalanirṇaye / loke 'pyetādṛśaguṇaiḥ phalādhikyaṃ hi dṛśyate //
[3,4.246]	evañca kalipūrvāṇāmasurāṇāṃ mahat phalam / aśubheṣu sadaiva syānmithyājñānādikeṣu hi //
[3,4.247]	śubhāśubhaphalaṃ devā asurāśca samāpnuyuḥ / krameṇaiva yathāśakti yathā ye ye prayojakāḥ //
[3,4.248]	prerakā api pāpānāṃ na devāḥ pāpamāpnuyuḥ / iti prakāśikāyāṃ hi provāca harirañjasā //
[3,4.249]	yadyapyevaṃ surāṇāṃ ca daityānāṃ ca mahat phalam / śubhāśubhebhya evañca kartuśca syād yathoditam //
[3,4.250]	tasmānnirayamānuṣyasvargamuktyupabhoginaḥ / mānuṣottamamārabhya devāstu nirayaṃ vinā //
[3,4.251]	asurāstu vinā muktiṃ tamo 'ndhamapi cāpnuyuḥ / iti tattvavivekoktaṃ svayaṃ bhagavatā vacaḥ //
[3,4.252]	jñānadā apicācāryā viśeṣāt phalamāpnuyuḥ / muktāvaṣṭaguṇaṃ śiṣyād gururāpanoti śobhanam //
[3,4.253]	tadgururdviguṇaṃ tasmāt sārdhaṃ tāvat tato 'pare / devāḥ sahasraguṇitaṃ kramāt tasmād yathottaram //
[3,4.254]	brahmā mahaughaguṇitamevaṃ phalavinirṇayaḥ / ityāha bhagavāñchāstre guruvṛttābhidhe svayam / yuktaṃ ca tanna godātā gomātraphalamāpnuyāt //
[3,4.255]	ya imaṃ paramaṃ guhyaṃ madbhakteṣvabhidhāsyati / bhaktiṃ mayi parāṃ kṛtvā māmevaiṣyatyasaṃśayaḥ //
[3,4.256]	na ca tasmānmanuṣyeṣu kaścinme priyakṛttamaḥ / bhavitā na ca me tasmādanyaḥ priyataro bhuvi / ityāha bhagavānevamapi pātramapekṣyate //
[3,4.257]	evamevāvirodhena prārabdhasyaiva karmaṇaḥ / jñānaṃ dṛṣṭaphalaṃ proktaṃ muktiścehaiva labhyate //
<iti śrīmadānandatīrthabhagavatpādācāryaviracite śrīmadbrahmasūtrānuvyākhyāne tṛtīyo 'dhyāyaḥ ||>
{4,1}
[4,1.1]	samanvayāvirodhābhyāṃ siddhe vastuni sādhane / vicāriteṣvaśeṣeṣu sādhaneṣu viśeṣataḥ //
[4,1.2]	nityaśaḥ kāryamatyantamavaśyaṃ bhāvi sādhanam / cintyate prathamaṃ tatra śravaṇādisakṛtkriyā //
[4,1.3]	āvṛttirveti sandehe kartavyā'vṛttireva hi / upadeśo 'tat tvamasītyādirhyasakṛdeva yat //
[4,1.4]	liṅgāllātavyataḥ pūrvamṛjobarrahmatvataḥ śatāt / śuśrāvogratapā nāma yogyo rudrapadasya yaḥ //
[4,1.5]	sārddhaṃ parārddhaṃ viṣṇostu guṇān bhaktayā sadodyataḥ / tattribhāgamupāsāṃ ca cakre sambhṛtamānasaḥ //
[4,1.6]	daśamanvantaraṃ śakrapadayogyo garutmataḥ / padayogyāt sumanasaḥ sunando nāma cāśṛṇot / upāsāṃ cakra udyukto manvantaracatuṣyayam //
[4,1.7]	sūryācandramasoścaiva padayogyau sutejasau / surūpaḥ śāntarūpaśca manvantaracatuṣyayam / aśṛṇvatāṃ sumanaso manvantaramupāsatām //
[4,1.8]	tataḥ proktāstu te sarve bhaktayogratapaādayaḥ / apaśyan paramaṃ viṣṇuṃ tatprasādedhitāḥ sadā / ityuktaṃ viṣṇunā sākṣād granthe sattatvasañjñite //
[4,1.9]	ātmeti nāma kathitaṃ sākṣānnārāyaṇasya hi / ātmā brahma mahāṃstāraḥ parameśaḥ śuciśravāḥ //
[4,1.10]	viṣṇurnārāyaṇo 'nanta iti śrīpatirīryate / iti piṅgaśrutiścaiva tathaiva paramaśrutiḥ //
[4,1.11]	omātmā bhagavān viṣṇurātmānando 'kṣaraḥ svarāṭ / viśvatrātā nṛsiṃho 'jo nārāyaṇa urukramaḥ //
[4,1.12]	anasūyā tathaivātrerjajñe putrānakalmaṣān / dattaṃ durvāsasaṃ somamātmeśabrahmasambhavān //
[4,1.13]	iti bhāgavate caiva tasmādātmā janārdanaḥ / tasmādupāsyo viṣṇuriti jñātavyaḥ sajjanaiḥ sadā //
[4,1.14]	tathaivopāsate santastathaivopadiśanti ca / ādānārthatvataścāyamātmaśabdaḥ patiṃ vadet / svāmī me viṣṇurityeva nityadopāsyamañjasā //
[4,1.15]	svāmī viṣṇuriti dhyānaṃ viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyataḥ / kartavyaṃ sarvathaivaitanna kathañcana vismaret //
[4,1.16]	iti sattattvavacanaṃ ṣāḍguṇyavacanaṃ param / mama svāmī harirnityaṃ sarvasya patireva ca / iti dhyeyaḥ sarvadaiva bhagavān viṣṇuravyayaḥ //
[4,1.17]	pratīkaviṣayatvena na kāryā viṣṇubhāvanā / pratīkaṃ naiva viṣṇuryanmithyopāsā hyanathardā //
[4,1.18]	yo 'nyathā santamātmeśamanyathā pratipadyate / kiṃ tena na kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ coreṇātmāpahāriṇā //
[4,1.19]	yo 'nyathā santamātmānamanyathā pratipadyate / kiṃ tena na kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ coreṇeśāpahāriṇā //
[4,1.20]	yo 'nyathaiva sthitaṃ viṣṇumanyathā pratipadyate / kiṃ tena na kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ coreṇa brahmacāriṇā //
[4,1.21]	svātmānaṃ pratimāṃ vāpi devatāntarameva vā / cetanācetanaṃ vānyad dhyāyed yaḥ keśavastviti / kiṃ tena na kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ cāreṇeśāpahāriṇā //
[4,1.22]	yo 'nyad viṣṇuriti dhyāyejjānīyād vā hariṃ tathā / andhe tamasi majjet sa yatra naivotthitiḥ kvacit //
[4,1.23]	yo 'nyad viṣṇuriti dhyāyed viṣṇuranyaditi sma vā / anyathā dhyānadoṣeṇa mahātamasi majjati //
[4,1.24]	yo 'nyad viṣṇuriti dhyāyed viṣṇuranyaditi sma vā / mahātamasi magnasya tasya naivotthitiḥ kvacit //
[4,1.25]	yatkiñcidanyathā saṃsthamanyathā dhyātamañjasā / dhyāturmahādoṣakaraṃ kimu sarveśvaro hariḥ //
[4,1.26]	yatkiñcidanyathā saṃsthamanyathā jñātamañjasā / mahādoṣakaraṃ viṣṇuḥ kimu sarveśvareśvaraḥ //
[4,1.27]	yatkiñcidanyathā saṃsthamanyathā jñātamañjasā / anarthakāraṇaṃ loke kimu sarveśvareśvaraḥ //
[4,1.28]	na kiñcidanyathā jñeyaṃ dhyeyaṃ vā tena kutracit / kimu sarvottamo viṣṇurjñeyo nīcatayā kvacit //
[4,1.29]	tasmād vastu yathārūpaṃ jñeyaṃ dhyeyaṃ ca sarvadā / kāraṇaṃ puruṣārthasya nānyathā bhavati kvacit //
[4,1.30]	iti śrutipurāṇoktibalato na pratīkatā / dhyeyā viṣṇoḥ kvacid yasmānmithyājñānamanarthadam //
[4,1.31]	ityabhipretya na hi sa ityāha bhagavān prabhuḥ / pratīkasaṃsthitatvena dhyeyo viṣṇurnacānyathā //
[4,1.32]	brahmeti ca sadā dhyeyo bhagavān viṣṇurañjasā / utkṛṣṭo brahmaśabdārthaḥ pūrṇatvaṃ brahmatā yataḥ //
[4,1.33]	ādhivyādhinimittena vikṣiptamanaso 'pi tu / dhyeyaiva brahmatā nityaṃ viṣṇorbhaktayā nirantaram / iti prakāśikāyāṃ ca vacanaṃ viṣṇuneritam //
[4,1.34]	nātmeti sūtramīśasya jīvatvapratipādakam / ātmaśabdaṃ yato hetuṃ kṛtvā jīvaṃ nyavārayat / svaśabdāt prāṇabhṛccaiva nokta ityeva vedarāṭ //
[4,1.35]	yadyātmaśabdo jīve 'pi kathaṃ sa vinivārayet / ātmaśabdoditastasmād viṣṇureva nacāparaḥ //
[4,1.36]	ātmabrahmādayaḥ śabdāstamṛte viṣṇumavyayam / na vadanti yato nāptā kvāpi tairguṇapūrṇatā / nārāyaṇādhyātmagatamiti yad vaiṣṇavaṃ vacaḥ //
[4,1.37]	yadi jīveśayorvedapatiraikyaṃ ca manyate / ātmaśabdaṃ kathaṃ tasmānnivārayati yuktitaḥ //
[4,1.38]	bhedasya vyapadeśaṃ ca sthitiṃ cādanameva ca / bhedadārḍhye hetumāha satātparyaṃ jagatpatiḥ //
[4,1.39]	vyāvahārikabhedaścet kvāsāvavyāvahārikaḥ / vyāvahārikamityeva vacanaṃ vyāvahārikam //
[4,1.40]	uta neti vikalpe tu yadi syād vyāvahārikam / tasyāpi bādhyatā cet syād bhedaḥ syāt pāramārthikaḥ //
[4,1.41]	avyāvahārikatvaṃ ced bhedo 'yaṃ satyatāṃ gataḥ / ekasyāsatyatāyāṃ hi dvayoreva viruddhayoḥ / anyasya satyataiva syāditi kena nivāryate //
[4,1.42]	asatyaṃ noktamityukte satyamuktamiti prajāḥ / jānantyuktaṃ tu no satyamityukte 'satyatāmapi //
[4,1.43]	na svapne 'pi dvayaṃ mithyā tatraikaṃ satyameva hi / bhāvābhāvāvubhau tatra kathaṃ mithyā bhaviṣyataḥ //
[4,1.44]	bhāvasya hi niṣedhe tu nābhāvasya niṣedhanam / svavāco 'satyatā cet syāt tasmād bhedasya satyatā //
[4,1.45]	tasmājjīveśayorbheda uktanyāyena gamyate / etasmādātmaśabdo 'yaṃ paramātmābhidhā bhavet //
[4,1.46]	pratīkaviṣayatvena viṣṇudṛṣṭirna tad bhavet / pratīke viṣṇurityeva tasmāt kāryā hyupāsanā //
[4,1.47]	na ca viṣṇuḥ pratīkaṃ yat tasmānnātmetyupāsanā / iti pakṣo yadā brahmadṛṣṭiścātra viruddhayate / sa neti yuktistatrāpi sametyuktaviruddhatā //
[4,1.48]	yadyapyutkarṣamātreṇa hyatadbhave 'pyupāsanā / utkarṣa ātmano 'pi syāccetanatvādacetanāt / tasamādatattvaṃ nopāsyamiti vedavido matam //
[4,1.49]	utkarṣād brahmatādhyāne yadi syāt phalamañjasā / brahmaṇo nīcatādhyānādanarthaḥ kiṃ na jāyate //
[4,1.50]	acetanasya brahmatvadhyāne tuṣyirnahi kvacit / nīcasya svātmatādhyāne kupyati brahma lokavat //
[4,1.51]	caṇḍālo nṛpa ityukte nṛpaścaṇḍāla ityapi / ko viśeṣaḥ parijñāte nṛpeṇa syāt kathañcana //
[4,1.52]	purato naradevasya caṇḍālo yadi pūjyate / rājavat kiṃ na kopaḥ syād rājño loke hi paśyati //
[4,1.53]	rājñastu purataḥ prokte caṇḍālaṃ nṛpa ityapi / ātmānaṃ sa iti proktamitivaddhayeva kupyati //
[4,1.54]	abhede naitayordhyāne ko viśeṣo vacasyapi / ayaṃ rājā tvamityukte caṇḍāle 'tha nṛpe 'pi ca / caṇḍāla iti tu prokte samameva hi dūṣaṇam //
[4,1.55]	dhyāte tvekasya tadbhāve tadbhāvo 'nyasya kiṃ na tat / nacaiva tadavijñātaṃ sarvajñabrahmaṇā kvacit //
[4,1.56]	tasmādapeśalaṃ sarvamanyasya brahmatāvacaḥ / tasmād yathoktamārgeṇa brahmopāsyaṃ mumukṣubhiḥ //
[4,1.57]	tathopāsyāñjasā dṛṣṭaṃ brahma pāpaṃ ca bhasmasāt / karoti nikhilaṃ pūrvaṃ pāścāttyasyāpyasaṅgatām / karoti taddviṣaścaivaṃ puṇyanāśo 'pyasaṅgatā //
[4,1.58]	yadeva vidyayetyatra pūrvoktāddhi viśiṣṭate / pūrvaṃ svargādilabdhyarthaṃ vīryavattvena coditam / karma vidyāyutaṃ paścānmokṣe vīryapradaṃ tviti //
[4,1.59]	tato bhogena puṇyaṃ ca kṣapayitvetarat tathā / brahmadviḍ brahmadarśī ca tamomokṣāvavāpnutaḥ //
[4,1.60]	brahmāṇaṃ śatakālāttu pūrvamārabdhasaṅkṣayaḥ / brahmaṇastveva tāvattvaṃ pañcāśad brahmaṇastathā / rudrasya viṃśadeva syādindrasyārkādike daśa //
[4,1.61]	anyeṣāṃ brahmamātrasya tvanta ārabdhasaṅkṣayaḥ / brahmaṇaiva sahātaśca paraṃ nārāyaṇaṃ vrajet / iti sattattvavacanaṃ svayaṃ bhagavatoditam //
<iti śrīmadānandatīrthabhagavatpādācāryaviracite śrīmadbrahmasūtrānuvyākhyāne caturthādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pādaḥ ||>
{4,2}
[4,2.1]	devānāṃ ca manuṣyāṇāmetāvat samameva hi / utkrāntimārgau devānāṃ na prāyeṇa bhaviṣyataḥ //
[4,2.2]	karmakṣayasatathotkrāntirmārgo bhogaścatuṣyayam / phalaṃ mokṣa iti proktaḥ kramāt pādeṣu coditaḥ //
[4,2.3]	sraṣṭṛṣveva tu sṛjyānāṃ praveśo brahmaṇo laye / devānāṃ mārga uddiṣṭo nārcirādirnacotkramaḥ //
[4,2.4]	sraṣṭustu grāsabhūtasya dehastatra layaṃ vrajet / yataḥ sṛjyasya devasya naivotkrāntistato bhavet //
[4,2.5]	layāccaivārcirādīnāṃ lokānāmapi sarvaśaḥ / kathaṃ mārgo bhavet teṣāṃ viśatāmuttamaṃ svataḥ //
[4,2.6]	jātānāṃ mānuṣe loke devānāṃ ca kadācana / utkrāntimārgau bhavato na tadā muktiriṣyate //
[4,2.7]	anyeṣāmapi sākṣāttu muktiḥ prāpyāpi taṃ harim / sahaiva brahmaṇā bhūyāditi śāstrasya nirṇayaḥ //
[4,2.8]	kṣmāmbhonalānilaviyanmanaindriyārthabhūtādibhiḥ parivṛtaḥ pratisañjighṛkṣuḥ / avyākṛtaṃ viśati yarhi guṇatrayātmā kālaṃ paraṃ svamanubhūya paraḥ svayambhūḥ //
[4,2.9]	evaṃ paretya bhagavantamanupraviṣṭā ye yogino jitamarunmanaso virāgāḥ / tenaiva sākamamṛtaṃ puruṣaṃ purāṇaṃ brahma pradhānamupayāntyagatābhimānāḥ //
[4,2.10]	bhagavantamanuprāptā api tu brahmaṇā saha / paramaṃ mokṣamāyānti liṅgabhaṅgena yoginaḥ //
[4,2.11]	prāptā api paraṃ devaṃ sahaiva brahmaṇā punaḥ / ānandavyaktiyāyānti pūrṇāṃ liṅgasya bhaṅgataḥ //
[4,2.12]	iti śrutipurāṇoktibalād vijñāyate ca tat / bhogastu sarvadevānāṃ narādīnāṃ ca vidyate //
[4,2.13]	tatra praveśo devānāmuttarottarataḥ kramāt / ucyate dehagānāṃ ca vṛttīnāmevameva tu //
[4,2.14]	tatra mokṣasvarūpaṃ tu vādinaḥ pratibhāśrayāt / nānā vadanti puṃsāṃ hi matayo guṇabhedataḥ / pṛthak pṛthak prajāyante tamasaivānyathāmatiḥ //
[4,2.15]	rajasā miśrabuddhitvaṃ sattvenaiva yathā matiḥ / guṇātītā vimuktānāṃ matiḥ śuddhacitiryataḥ //
[4,2.16]	sāmyagevātha nityā ca tattanmāhātmyayogataḥ / bahaḷā cātiviśadā spaṣṭā caiva śriyo matiḥ //
[4,2.17]	mahāśuddhacititvena tato 'pyatimahācitiḥ / aśeṣoruviśeṣāṇāmatispaṣṭatayā dṛśiḥ / nityamekaprakārā ca nārāyaṇamatiḥ parā //
[4,2.18]	sūryaprabhāvadakhilaṃ bhāsayanti nirantarā / nirlepā vītadoṣā ca nityamevāvikāriṇī //
[4,2.19]	viśeṣāṃsatadgatāṃstyaktavā prāyastallakṣaṇā śriyaḥ / tathaiva spaṣṭatābhāvāt tattantratvācca kevalam / na tādṛśī brahmaṇastu prāya eva śriyo yathā //
[4,2.20]	muktānāṃ tu tadanyeṣāṃ samudrataraḷopamā / agnijvālāvadeva syāt smṛtigānāṃ dṛśo bhavaḥ //
[4,2.21]	evaṃvidheṣu jñāneṣu tamasā muṣyadṛṣṭayaḥ / khadyotasadṛśātyalpajñānatvādanyathādṛśaḥ / vadanti vādino mokṣaṃ nānāmatasamāśrayāt //
[4,2.22]	āśritya pratibhāmāha jinastatrātitāmasīm / jñānāt karmakṣayānmokṣo bhaved dehākhyapañjarāt //
[4,2.23]	pañjaronmuktakhagavadalākākāśagocaraḥ / nityamūrdhvaṃ vrajatyeva pudgalo hastapādavān //
[4,2.24]	iti tat kena mānena mokṣarūpaṃ pradṛśyate / gatirūrdhvā ca duḥkhetā gatitvāllaukikī yathā / ityukte cānumānaikaśaraṇasya kimuttaram //
[4,2.25]	anūrdhvagatitā tatra yadyupādhiḥ khagasya ca / dūrordhvagamane duḥkhamiti sādhyānugo na saḥ //
[4,2.26]	pratisādhanarūpasya nānumānasya dūṣaṇam / upādhiḥ pratirūpaṃ hi sādhanaṃ tannacāparam //
[4,2.27]	athāpi saśarīratvaṃ cātropādhirna vai bhavet / gatitvaṃ yatra dehitvamiti yat sādhanānugam //
[4,2.28]	āgamānanusāritve prasaṅgo 'yaṃ yatastataḥ / nāpasiddhāntatā doṣaḥ prasaṅge yadi sā bhavet / tadaivātiprasaṅgaḥ syānna pasaṅgaḥ kvacid bhavet //
[4,2.29]	lokākāśagatitvaṃ cedupādhiḥ sādhanānugaḥ / so 'pītyukte vadet kiṃ sa tasmād vedodito bhavet //
[4,2.30]	mokṣa evaṃ svayaṃ viṣṇuryadyapīśo hyaśeṣavit / cakāra saugatamataṃ mohāyaiva cakāra yat //
[4,2.31]	asurāṇāmayogyānāṃ vedamārge pravartatām / ato 'surādhikāratvānna grāhyaṃ tanmataṃ kvacit //
[4,2.32]	catuṣprakāraṃ taccoktaṃ śūnyaṃ vijñānamekalam / anumeyabahistattvaṃ tathā pratyakṣabāhyagam //
[4,2.33]	iti tatra tu ye śūnyaṃ vadantyajñānamohitaḥ / te mokṣaṃ tādṛśaṃ brūyurniśśaṅkaṃ māyino yathā //
[4,2.34]	na kiñcinamuktayavasthāyāmātmātmīyamathāpi vā / ekasmin saṃsṛtermukte na kiñcidavaśiṣyate //
[4,2.35]	tatsaṃvṛtyaiva bhedo 'yaṃ cetanācetanātmakaḥ / dṛśyate saṃvṛterdhvaṃse nirviśeṣaiva śūnyatā //
[4,2.36]	na sattvaṃ naiva cāsattvaṃ śūnyatattvasya vidyate / na sukhatvaṃ na duḥkhatvaṃ na viśeṣo 'pi kaścana //
[4,2.37]	nirviśeṣaṃ syayambhātaṃ nirlepamajarāmaram / śūnyaṃ tattvamasambādhaṃ nānāsaṃvṛtivarjitam //
[4,2.38]	aśeṣadoṣarahitaṃ manovācāmagocaram / mokṣa ityucyate 'sadbhirnānāsaṃvṛtidūṣitam //
[4,2.39]	saṃsṛtyavasthaṃ vijñeyaṃ saṃvṛtyaiva viśeṣyate / sthitayā dhvastayā caiva saṃsṛtirmokṣa ityapi //
[4,2.40]	kecit teṣvanyathā prāhuḥ saṃvṛtyaiva tvanekadhā / avacchinnaṃ mahāśūnyaṃ nānānapudgalaśabditam //
[4,2.41]	yasya śūnyaikarasatā jñānāt sā tvapagacchati / sa pudgalatvanirmukto mahāśūnyatvameṣyati //
[4,2.42]	saṃvṛtyānyastvavacchinno duḥkhānyanubhavatyalam / ityevaṃ māyinaścāhurekajīvatvavādinaḥ //
[4,2.43]	bahujīvamatāśceti māyā teṣāṃ tu saṃvṛtiḥ / nirviśeṣatvavācaiva śūnyaṃ brahmaiva no bhidā //
[4,2.44]	saccitsukhādikaṃ caiva kiṃ kuto 'khaṇḍavādinaḥ / vyāvartyamātrabhedastu vidyate śūnyavādinaḥ //
[4,2.45]	anṛtāderapohaṃ tu svayameva hi manyate / nirviśeṣatvato naiva viśeṣo brahmaśūnyayoḥ //
[4,2.46]	prāmāṇyādi ca vedasya phalataḥ samameva hi / atattvāvedakaṃ yasmāt pramāṇaṃ tena kathyate / atattvāvedakatvaṃ yadaprāmāṇyaṃ satāṃ matam //
[4,2.47]	dīrghabhrāntikarī cet syādatattvāvedakapramā / rajjusarpādivijñānādapyādhikyādamānatā / syādāgamasyānivartyamahāmohapradatvataḥ //
[4,2.48]	talanailyādivijñānamākāśe mānatāṃvrajet / chatrākāratvavijñānaṃcandraprādeśatāmatiḥ //
[4,2.49]	nirbhedatvaṃ tu śūnyasya tenāpyaṅgīkṛtaṃ sadā / sattvāsattvādidharmāṇāmabhāva ubhayormataḥ //
[4,2.50]	na hi satpratiyogitvaṃ śūnyatvaṃ tena ceṣyate / na ca duḥkhavirodhitvādanyā hyānandateṣyate //
[4,2.51]	māyinā śūnyapakṣe 'pi jñānaṃ jāḍyavirodhi ca / dharmaste 'pi na santyeva ko viśeṣastatastayoḥ //
[4,2.52]	etādṛśānāṃ pakṣāṇāṃ dūṣaṇaṃ prabhurā kṛtam / svapakṣasādanenaiva nābhāva iti coktitaḥ //
[4,2.53]	ātmābhāve pumarthaḥ ka iṣṭasyātmāvadhiryataḥ / yadi nātmāvadhirmokṣo mokṣaḥ syād ghaṭaśūnyatā / kalpitatvād viśeṣāṇāṃ māyino 'pi samaṃ hi tat //
[4,2.54]	dṛśyamāne viśeṣe 'pi yadi cedaviśeṣatā / ghaṭābhāvo 'viśeṣaḥ syāt pāścātyaścedanāgataḥ //
[4,2.55]	na mokṣo vimato yasmādadeho ghaṭaśūnyatā / yathetyukte vadet kiṃ sa yo 'numāmātramānakaḥ //
[4,2.56]	na ca māyī vadet tatra pūrvoktenaiva vartmanā / amānatvācchrutestasya nacādehatvavādinī //
[4,2.57]	śrutiḥ kācidadehatvamaprākṛtaśarīragā / mokṣe bhogaṃ yato brūte jakṣan krīḍanniti śrutiḥ //
[4,2.58]	nirduḥkhatvānna tanmokṣaḥ pratipannaṃ yatheti ca / anumādūṣaṇaṃ kiṃ syād vādinoḥ śūnyamāyinoḥ //
[4,2.59]	duḥkhaṃ duḥkhādabhinnatvānmokṣo 'pi syādasaṃśayam / bhede sadvaitataiva syādityādyamitadoṣataḥ / heyaṃ māyāmatenaiva saha śūnyamataṃ budhaiḥ //
[4,2.60]	evaṃ vijñānavādo 'pi jñānamātraviśeṣataḥ / tasyāpi bhaṅguratvādiviśeṣamapahāya hi / advaitatāmataṃ sākṣāduktadoṣastato bhavet //
[4,2.61]	kālo na kevalajñānī kālatvāt pratipannavat / etayānumayā rodhānna tādṛṅmokṣarūpatā //
[4,2.62]	yadi kālo 'pi netyāha kadeti praśna uttaram / kiṃ vakṣyati yadāvasthāṃ vadet sā pakṣatāṃ vrajet //
[4,2.63]	avasthātvāditi hyeva hetuḥ sāpi kadeti ca / pṛṣṭe kālaśca vaktavyo nākālatvaṃ tato bhavet //
[4,2.64]	na kāla iti sāmānyaniṣedhe kālagapramā / niruṇaddhi vaktavyo nākālatvaṃ tato bhavet //
[4,2.65]	ekajīvatvapakṣe tu kālābhāvādiyaṃ pramā / kupitā kālamādāya dvaitamevopapādayet //
[4,2.66]	vimataḥ prapañcavān kālaḥ kālatvāt pratipannavat / iti cānyānumaikatvaṃ jīvasya vinivārayet //
[4,2.67]	kālaśabdeśvaraikatvamatānyapyevameva hi / nirākṛtāni teṣāṃ ca samatvāt pakṣadoṣayoḥ //
[4,2.68]	jñānaṃ svarasabhaṅgayeva nityasantāmiṣyate / bauddhābhyāmaparābhyāṃ tu tatrāpyuktānumā ripuḥ //
[4,2.69]	mokṣo na śuddhavijñānasantānī kālagatvataḥ / pratipanno yathetyetadanumānaṃ taduttaram //
[4,2.70]	anumānāni sarvāṇi pratisādhanayogataḥ / niṣiddhānyuktabhaṅgayaiva śrutayaścāsmaduktigāḥ //
[4,2.71]	sāṅkhayanaiyāyikādyāśca prāhurmokṣaṃ tu nissukham / icchādveṣaprayatnāderapi sarvātmanā layam //
[4,2.72]	tatrāhurnaitadapyatra śobhanaṃ śrutayo yataḥ / mahānandaṃ ca bhogaṃ ca niyamena vadanti hi //
[4,2.73]	prākṛtapriyahānistu priyāspṛṣṭiritīryate / apriyaṃ pratikūlaṃ tadaviśeṣeṇa śabditam //
[4,2.74]	nāsti hyaprākṛtaṃ duḥkhaṃ sato jīvasya kutracit / priyaṃ svarūpamevāsya balānandādivākyataḥ //
[4,2.75]	heyatvādapapriyasyaiva priyahāneraniṣṭhataḥ / na samastapriyābhāvo mokṣe prokte tu yujyate //
[4,2.76]	apriyasya svarūpatvamasureṣveva hi śrutam / asurā naivamevaṃ ca naivaṃ cākhilamānuṣāḥ / ityātmapriyahānāya ko yateta ca buddhimān //
[4,2.77]	sañjñā nāstītyapi hyasya nāmuktajñeyateti hi / dharmānucchittimevāsya yato vaktayuttaraśrutiḥ //
[4,2.78]	āśaṅkayāsya jñānahāniṃ maitreyyā mohamāha mām / bhavānityuktavatyā hi nāhaṃ mohaṃ vadāmi te / ityuktavā yājñavalkyo hi svarūpānāśamūcivān //
[4,2.79]	jñānarūpasya vijñānānāśastannāśa eva yat / iti śūnyamatocchittyai punarānandapūrvakān / dharmānāhāpyanucchinnāṃstārkikairvinivāritān / mātrāsaṃsargamapyāha tathā mādhyandinaśrutiḥ //
[4,2.80]	ācikṣepa mataṃ tacca yasmin na viṣayādanam / ghrāṇādibhogābhāvasya tvaniṣṭatvahṛdā śrutiḥ //
[4,2.81]	yenedamakhilaṃ veda vijñātāraṃ svameva ca / kena taṃ ca vijānīyādityaniṣṭaṃ hi sarvathā //
[4,2.82]	nākhilajñāpako viṣṇurajñeyo niyamena hi / tajjñānārthaṃ hi vedānāmakhilānāṃ pravartanam //
[4,2.83]	pratyakṣāgamātmavijñānāvirodhānubhavādapi / na svavijñānitāyāṃ ca virodhaḥ kaścaneyate //
[4,2.84]	kartṛkarmavirodhaśca nityānubhavavirodhataḥ / kathameva padaṃ gacched virodho dṛṣṭabādhanam //
[4,2.85]	so 'śnute sarvakāmaṃśca kāmānnī kāmarūpyatha / ityādiśrutayaścoktamarthameva vadanti hi //
[4,2.86]	asvātantryādivetyuktaṃ na dvaitābhāvataḥ kvacit / ātmaivābhūditi hyasmādaviśeṣaprasaṅgataḥ //
[4,2.87]	asvātantryopamābhedabhedeṣviva udīritaḥ / śabdatattva iti proktaṃ maitreyyuktottaraṃ ca kim //
[4,2.88]	sukhādidharmahānau tu mukteḥ kiñca prayojanam / yadyartho duḥkhahāniḥ syādanarthaḥ sukhanāśanam //
[4,2.89]	tayośca duḥkhahānāddhi sukhanāśo 'dhiko bhavet / prāpyāpi duḥkhaṃ sumahat sukhaleśāptaye janaḥ / yatate sukhahānau hi ko mokṣāya yatet pumān //
[4,2.90]	alpācca sukhānāśāddhi bibhetyatitarāṃ janaḥ / mahacca duḥkhamāpnoti sukhanāśanivṛttaye //
[4,2.91]	na ca rāganimittaṃ tad vītarāgā api sphuṭam / nāradādyāḥ sukhārthāya sahante duḥkhamañjasā / yuddhādidarśanaṃ yasmāt suduḥkhenāpi kuvarte //
[4,2.92]	yadendravairocanayorbrahmāstrābhyāṃ sutāpitāḥ / api naivājahuryuddharasāt te nāradādayaḥ / iti skāndavacastasmāt sukhābhāvasya ko yatet //
[4,2.93]	vimato duḥkhayug yasmāccetanaḥ san sukhojkhitaḥ / pratipanno yathetyeva cānumā kena vāryate //
[4,2.94]	sarvaśrutipurāṇeṣu sukhabhāvoktitastathā / muktau na grāhyamevaitat sukhābhāvamataṃ budhaiḥ //
[4,2.95]	so 'nānandād vimuktaḥ sannānandī bhavati sphuṭam / nirguṇe brahmaṇi mayi dhārayan viśadaṃ manaḥ / paramānandamāpnoti yatra kāmo 'vasīyate //
[4,2.96]	na viṣṇusadṛśaṃ daivaṃ na mokṣasadṛśaṃ sukham / na vedasadṛśaṃ vākyaṃ na varṇo 'kārasammitaḥ //
[4,2.97]	yatrānandāśca modāśca mudaḥ pramuda āsate / kāmasya yatrāptāḥ kāmāstatra māmamṛtaṃ kṛdhi //
[4,2.98]	iti śrutipurāṇāni tatratatra vadanti hi / ato mokṣe sukhābhāva iti yatkiñcideva hi //
[4,2.99]	śiraḥkarādyabhāvaśca na muktasya bhavet kvacit / śrutayaśca purāṇāni mānamatra bahūni ca //
[4,2.100]	na vartate yatra rajastamastayoḥ sattvaṃ ca miśraṃ na ca kālavikramaḥ / na yatra māyā kimutāpare hareranuvratā yatra surāsurārcitāḥ //
[4,2.101]	śyāmāvadātāḥ śatapatralocanāḥ piśaṅgavastrāḥ surucaḥ supeśasaḥ / sarve caturbāhava unmiṣanmaṇipravekaniṣkābharaṇāḥ suvarcasaḥ //
[4,2.102]	pravāḷavaiḍūryamṛṇāḷavarcasāṃ parisphuratkuṇḍalamaulimālinām / bhrājiṣṇubhiryaḥ parito virājate lasadvimānāvalibhirmahātmanām //
[4,2.103]	vidyotamānapramadottamābhiḥ savidyudabhrāvalibhiryathā nabhaḥ / śrīryatra rūpiṇyurugāyapādayoḥ karoti mānaṃ bahudhā vibhūtibhiḥ //
[4,2.104]	ṛcāṃ tvaḥ poṣamāste pupuṣvān gāyatraṃ tvo gāyati śakvarīṣu / brahmā tvo vadati jātavidyāṃ yajñasya mātraṃ vimibhīta u tvaḥ //
[4,2.105]	kāmānnarūpī caratītipūrvaśrutyā purāṇoktibhirapyadoṣaḥ / dehaḥ svarūpātmaka eva teṣāṃ muktiṃ gatānāmapi ceyate hi //
[4,2.106]	śiraḥkarādyairapi muktibhājo yuktā yataste puruṣā idānīm / yathetipūrvā anumāśca jīvasvarūpamaṅgādiyugāpayanti //
[4,2.107]	na brahmarūpatvamamuṣya dehino muktāvapi syāt pramayā kathañcit / sa brahmaṇā sahito 'śeṣabhogān bhuṅkte tathopetya sukhārṇavaṃ tam //
[4,2.108]	yattat paraṃ jyotirupetya jīvo nijasvarapūtvamavāpya kāmān / bhuṅkte sa daivaṃ puruṣottamo 'ja ātmeti cokto guṇapūrtihetoḥ //
[4,2.109]	setuḥ sa devo 'khilamuktibhāgāmutāmṛtasyeṣya iheśitā yat / ityādivākyairbhagavadvaśaḥ san bhuṅkte'khilān muktigato 'pi bhogān //
[4,2.110]	kālo 'pyasau naikyayutaḥ pareṇa jīvasya kālo yata eṣa yadvat / ityādikā apyanumāḥ pramāṇaṃ muktau ca jīvasya paratvarodhe //
[4,2.111]	kathaṃ ca yaḥ pūrvamasau na paścād bhavet sa evetyapi yuktimeti / yato na dṛṣṭaṃ yadabhūnna pūrvaṃ paścāt tadāseti kutaśca kiñcit //
[4,2.112]	nacaiva muktau tu hareḥ pṛthaktavamaikyaṃ tathā syāditi yuktimeti / yato na kutrāpi bhidābhidā ca dṛṣṭā citaścetanayā kutaścit //
[4,2.113]	itthaṃ matāni bhramajāni yasmānmokṣaṃ samuddeśyamapi bhrameṇa / vidurna samyag yadapīha laukikāḥ sukhaṃ mama syācca sadeti jānate //
[4,2.114]	audāryamuccāvacaśaktirātmasvarapūdārḍhyaṃ ca nijasvabhāvaḥ / svātantryamāpūrṇaviśeṣayogyatā virodhahāniśca caturthapāde //
[4,2.115]	vyavasthitistvaviśeṣaḥ sthitiśca niṣedhasāmānyavidhikriyāṇām / vibhaktatā cātvarayaiva siddhirvipakṣasamprāptiviruddhahetavaḥ //
[4,2.116]	suśakyatā śaśvadatiprasiddhivivekavinyāsavicārasañjñāḥ / nānāpravṛttiḥ kṛtakṛtyatā ca vipakṣatarkāḥ samatītapāde //
[4,2.117]	mahāphalatvaṃ praviviktatā ca sandhigrahaḥ sādhanamāptakṛtyam / viśeṣakāryaṃ kṛtisaṃsthitiśca suyuktayo nirṇayagāḥ svapakṣe //
[4,2.118]	vyāmiśratā kāryakaratvamarthakḷptiḥ sudārḍhyaṃ paratantratā ca / samānadharmaḥ kṛtaśeṣatā ca lokopamā pūrvamatānusārāḥ //
[4,2.119]	viśeṣasāmyaśrutirāḍhyatā ca samānalopo mahimā viśeṣaḥ / kṛtārthatā śaśvadanupravṛttiḥ siddhāntanirṇītiviśiṣṭahetavaḥ //
[4,2.120]	pradhānavāyustviha vāyunāmā bhūteṣvitiproktagato 'pi yuktayā / yasmācchrutau pavate ceti bhūri prokto yato bhūtamānī ca so 'pi / mahāmānī tvalpamānī ca yasmāt tacchabdenāpyucyate tena so 'pi //
[4,2.121]	tasmin layaṃ yānti bhūtānyaśeṣakramāvirodhena sa eva viṣṇau / indrādīnāṃ tatra layaḥ kramaṃ tu proktaṃ viśeṣādanusṛtya nānyat //
[4,2.122]	tasmādaśeṣā girijāṃ praviśya tayaiva rudraṃ saha tena vāṇīm / tayā patiṃ prāpya sahaiva tena layaṃ harau yānti samastajīvāḥ //
[4,2.123]	somastu vārīśayuto 'niruddhaṃ viśatyasau kāmamasau ca vāruṇīm / sā śeṣadevaṃ sa giraṃ ca saiva vāyuṃ viśatyañja itīha nirṇayaḥ //
[4,2.124]	umāgirīśāvapi bhāratīrāviti sma vāg vedagatā bravīti / ahīndrapatnīmahipaṃ viriñcapatnīṃ viriñcaṃ ca vimuktikāle //
[4,2.125]	ta eva yat tatpadamāpnuvanti tatkāla etān samupāsya jīvāḥ / brahmatvakāle praviśanti caitānīti sma vāk tādṛśatāmupaiti //
[4,2.126]	sūryo 'gniyukto gurumāpya tena śakraṃ sahainena suparṇapatnīm / tayā suparṇaṃ saha tena vāṇīṃ brahmāṇametadgata eva yāti //
[4,2.127]	indrapraveśastu yadocyate 'tra tadā hyumetyeva suparṇapatnī / uktā suparṇaśca girīśanāmnā tato virodhaśca na kaścanātra //
[4,2.128]	bhṛgvādayo dakṣamavāpya tena prāpyendrametena suparṇapatnīm / viśanti ye manavo rājamukhyā manuṃ praviśyātra gatā mahendram //
[4,2.129]	ākāśa urvī ca guruṃ praviśya tenaiva yātaḥ puruhūtadevam / sanādayo yatayaḥ kāmameva viśanti śiṣṭā api havyavāham //
[4,2.130]	varṇāśramācāraratā manuṣyā dharmaṃ manuṃ so 'pi sameti kāle / tameva sarve pitaraḥ surānugāḥ sarve kuberaṃ sa ca somameva //
[4,2.131]	vimuktikāle praviśantyabhīkṣṇaṃ bhogāṃśca taddehagatāḥ prabhuñjate / ānandasuvyaktiramutra teṣāṃ bhavatyataśceṣyata eva nirgatāḥ / krīḍanti bhūyaśca samāviśanti tāneva sāyujyamidaṃ vadanti //
[4,2.132]	sāyujyahīnāśca laye tu sarve proktena mārgeṇa viśanti sṛṣṭau / bahiśca niryānti tato 'nyadāpi sāyujyabhājāṃ bhavati praveśaḥ //
[4,2.133]	uktaṃ samastaṃ paramaśrutau hi proktaṃ tu sargakramato viparyayaḥ / muktau laye yadvadatho layaśca viparyayeṇetyavadad girāṃ patiḥ //
[4,2.134]	layo yato muktiriyaṃ surāṇāṃ bhogo viśeṣeṇa ca yaṃ vadiṣyati / uktaśca bimbapratibimbabhāvaḥ piṅgaśrutāvuktalayānusārataḥ //
[4,2.135]	bimbe layo yanniyataśca muktau cidātmanāṃ tadvaśatā ca sarvadā / tejo 'bhidhāṃ tu śriyamāpya viṣṇumagre tataḥ putratayaiva vāyuḥ / āptaḥ prasūtaḥ punareva viṣṇuṃ praviśya muktaḥ praḷaye 'tra tiṣṭhati //
[4,2.136]	sarve 'pi te muktagaṇā amandasāndraṃ nijānandamaśeṣato 'pi / bhuñjanta evāsata īśadehe laye 'tha sarge bahireva yānti //
[4,2.137]	prayāti dharmaṃ nirṛtistu śakraṃ marudgaṇāḥ pārṣadāstathaiva / sarve 'niruddhaṃ pṛtanādhipādyāsturaśrutirhītthamiyaṃ vimuktiḥ //
<iti śrīmadānandatīrthabhagavatpādācāryaviracite śrīmadbrahmasūtrānuvyākhyane caturthādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ ||>
{4,3}
[4,3.1]	utkrāntamārgaśca vimuktagamyaṃ pādoditam sukramavikramau ca / sāntānikaṃ prāptirabhīṣyatā ca saukayarmityanyamatasya tarkāḥ //
[4,3.2]	viśeṣasamprāptirurutvamāptiḥ kramānurāgaḥ kathitānuvṛttiḥ / siddhāntanirṇītikarāḥ pratīkaṃ dehādikaṃ tadgatameva ye narāḥ //
[4,3.3]	upāsate te purataḥ samāpnuyurbrahmāṇamasmānmatimāpya viṣṇum / prāpsyantyato 'nye 'pi tamāpya tasmāddhariṃ gatā muktibhājaḥ parānte //
<śrīmadānandatīrthabhagavatpādācāryaviracite śrīmadbrahmasūtrānuvyākhyane caturthādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ ||>
{4,4}
[4,4.1]	atikramoktiḥ kṛtirarthalābhaḥ parā gatiḥ pāragatistadokaḥ / samastakāryaṃ vaśitā ca viśvasambhāvanā yuktayastvanyapakṣe //
[4,4.2]	sāmānyarūpaṃ pratibhānamuktirāścaryatākṛtrimatāstadoṣaḥ / viśeṣakḷptiḥ kṛtaniḥśramaśca māhātmyamityeva sunirṇayārthāḥ //
[4,4.3]	ananyabhṛtyatvamihoditabhyastvanyasya bhṛtyatvanivāraṇāya / patiṃ yadeṣāmapi viṣṇumāha hyutāmṛtatvasya patitvavāgdhareḥ //
[4,4.4]	ete 'picānyādhipatitvayuktā viṣṇvanyacittvena yathā pumāṃsaḥ / prasiddhibhājastviti cānumaiva hyabhīṣyasiddhayai bhavatīha niścayāt //
[4,4.5]	muktasvakīyāvarayantṛtāsti muktāvapi brahmapurassarāṇām / anena devena tathāmunā ca hīṣye parārvāktanalokināmiti //
[4,4.6]	phalaṃ śrutirjñānata āha muktāvetacca sarvāśubhanāśaliṅgāt / lokādhipatyaṃ ca vidhātureva sarvātmanetyāha turaśrutiśca / sarve baliṃ devagaṇā vahantītyetacca nānyasya hi yuktimeti //
[4,4.7]	lokā itīhāpi tu lokināṃ vaco lokā iti hyeva ravaḥ prajāsu / prayujyate sarvajanaiḥ sadaiva tanmānino lokapadena coktāḥ / tadgāstu muktā iha lokaśabdā anyonyanāthā iti paiṅgināṃ śrutiḥ //
[4,4.8]	alokaśabdena vimuktibhājo vācyāḥ padaṃ tādṛgapīha yuktam / lokābhidhāścāpi yato hi muktāḥ prakāśarūpāḥ satataṃ ca sarve / brahmaiva lokādhipatirvimukto bhavediti prāha turaśrutiśca //
[4,4.9]	naceha vijñānaphalaṃ samuktaṃ lokādhipatyaṃ ravibimbato harau / uktaṃ pṛthak tacca puraiva yasmād bhedo 'munetyādi ca samyaguktaḥ //
[4,4.10]	tvapratyayaṃ cāpyatihāya naiva rūpeṇa teneti bhavedihārthaḥ / bhavatyasāvityaṇuśabdamatra vihāya vākyāni bahūni doṣaḥ //
[4,4.11]	ato jagadvayāpṛtimanta eva brahmādayaḥ pūrṇaguṇāḥ krameṇa / amandamānandamajasrameva bhuñjanta ātmīyamajāt samāsate //
[4,4.12]	namo namo 'śeṣaviśeṣapūrṇaguṇaikadhāmne puruṣottamāya / bhaktānukampādatiśuddhasaṃviddātre 'nupādhipriyasadguṇātmane //
[4,4.13]	yasya trīṇyuditāni vedavacane rūpāṇi divyānalaṃ baṭ tad darśatamitthameva nihitaṃ devasya bhargo mahat / vāyo rāmavaconayaṃ prathamakaṃ pṛkṣo dvitīyaṃ vapurmadhvo yattu tṛtīyametadanumā granthaḥ kṛtaḥ keśave //
[4,4.14]	niḥśeṣadoṣarahitakalyāṇākhilasadguṇa / bhūtisvayambhuśarvādivandyaṃ tvāṃ naumi me priyam //
<iti śrīmadānandatīrthabhagavatpādācāryaviracite śrīmadbrahmasūtrānuvyākhyāne caturtho 'dhyāyaḥ ||>
